# 💰 BOYCOTT SCOREBOARD — ARE THEY ACTUALLY HURTING?

> Added March 5, 2026. The short answer: **It depends on who.** Tesla is getting destroyed. Amazon barely felt it. But the *international* boycott is costing the US economy up to **$90 billion.**

---

## DOMESTIC BOYCOTTS — COMPANY BY COMPANY

| Company | Why Targeted | Stock Impact | Revenue Impact | Verdict |
|---------|-------------|-------------|----------------|---------|
| **Tesla** | Musk/DOGE | Down **50%** from peak (recovered ~11% YTD) | First-ever annual revenue decline: **-3%** ($94.8B). Deliveries **-9%** (1.63M). Profit **-46%** | 🔴 **DEVASTATING** |
| **Target** | Rolled back DEI | Stock dropped **32%** (Jan–Apr 2025: $142→$97) | Sales and foot traffic declined. Cutting 500 jobs in 2026 | 🔴 **Significant** |
| **Spotify** | ICE ads, Rogan/DOGE ties | Down **23%** in 3 months | Advertiser pullback | 🟡 **Moderate** |
| **Amazon** | Bezos/Trump, killed DEI, killed tariff price display | Down 4.6% during boycott week — **but Nasdaq fell too** | Transactions actually **rose 1%** during boycott. Q1 revenue **up 5-9%** YoY | 🟢 **Minimal** |
| **Home Depot** | ICE in parking lots, cut DEI | Stock **rose 8%** in 6 weeks after boycott | No measurable impact | 🟢 **None** |
| **Walmart** | Tariff compliance, DEI rollback | Stock held | Regional losses but national growth | 🟢 **Minimal** |
| **Meta** | Zuckerberg/Trump alignment, cut DEI | Underperformed Mag 7 | 3.54 billion daily users. Ad revenue still 97.8% of income | 🟢 **None** |
| **American Eagle** | Controversial ad campaign | Stock **up 75%** in 3 months | Counter-supporters *boosted* sales | 🟢 **Backfired** |

### Why Tesla Got Hit So Hard

Tesla isn't just facing a domestic boycott — it's a **global one**, and the numbers are staggering:

| Market | Impact (Jan 2026) |
|--------|-------------------|
| **France** | Sales down **42%** |
| **Netherlands** | Sales down **67%** |
| **Norway** | Sales down **88%** |
| **Germany** | 61% say they'd no longer consider Tesla; 36% reject it completely |
| **Global** | BYD overtook Tesla as #1 EV seller worldwide (2.26M vs 1.63M) |

Tesla also **discontinued the Model S and Model X** and lost emissions credit revenue as Toyota and Stellantis exited the CO₂ pool. Musk is pivoting to AI/robotics, but the EV business is still 75% of revenue — and it's cratering.

---

## THE INTERNATIONAL BOYCOTT — THIS IS THE BIG ONE

The *domestic* boycotts are a mixed bag. The **international** boycott of all American products is where the real economic damage lives.

### GDP Impact

| Estimate | Source |
|----------|--------|
| **$28B – $83B** hit to US GDP (0.1–0.3%) | Goldman Sachs |
| **Up to $90B** | Goldman Sachs (updated) |
| **$12.5B** in lost tourism revenue | World Travel & Tourism Council |
| **$20B** in US retail spending at risk | Bloomberg |
| **$5.7B** in lost tourism from Canada alone | US Travel Association |

### Country by Country

| Country | Boycott Participation | Details |
|---------|----------------------|---------|
| 🇨🇦 **Canada** | **53%** actively boycotting | 91% want less reliance on US. Air Transat cancelled ALL summer 2026 Florida flights. WestJet suspended 10 US cities (-30% demand). Canadians are the **#1 source of US tourists (28%)** |
| 🇫🇷 **France** | **62%** support boycotts; **32%** already boycotting | Targeting Coca-Cola, McDonald's, KFC, Tesla, X |
| 🇸🇪 **Sweden** | **70%** considered or actively boycotting | 10% boycotting ALL US goods |
| 🇩🇰 **Denmark** | **~50%** deliberately avoiding US products | Since inauguration |
| 🇪🇺 **Europe overall** | **44%** turning away from US brands | ECB survey |
| 🇰🇷 **South Korea** | Favorability down **38 points** | Morning Consult |
| 🇲🇽 **Mexico** | Favorability down **32 points** | Morning Consult |

### Tourism Collapse

- **International tourism spending** forecast down **3.2%** for 2025
- **European tourism to US** down **17%** overall
- Ireland, Germany, Norway: declines **exceeding 20%**
- US global favorability dropped **20 points** in just 2 months (Jan→Mar)
- Winners: Mexico, UK, Caribbean, and domestic Canadian tourism are all surging as alternatives

### Will It Last?

FIFA World Cup 2026 (co-hosted by US) may provide a temporary tourism boost. But consumer surveys suggest the **behavioral shift may outlast the tariffs** — Canadians are discovering they prefer traveling within Canada or to Europe. Brand loyalty, once broken, is hard to rebuild.

---

## THE SCORECARD

### What's Working (Boycotts That Hurt)

| Target | Why It Worked |
|--------|--------------|
| **Tesla** | Musk is personally identified with DOGE/Trump. Easy to switch to competitors. Global participation |
| **Target** | Core customer base (suburban moms) was the exact demographic offended by DEI rollback |
| **US Tourism** | Easy substitution — go to Mexico, UK, Caribbean instead. 28% of US tourists are Canadian |
| **International US brands** | National pride + tariff anger = sustained behavioral change |

### What's NOT Working

| Target | Why It Failed |
|--------|--------------|
| **Amazon** | Monopoly position. No real alternative for Prime, AWS. Too convenient |
| **Home Depot** | Essential purchase (home repair). Customers need the products regardless |
| **Meta** | Network effects. You can't boycott Facebook if your community is on Facebook |
| **Walmart** | Low-income consumers can't afford to boycott the cheapest store |

### The Pattern

**Boycotts work when:**
1. There's an easy substitute (Tesla → BYD/VW/Hyundai)
2. The CEO is personally identified with the offense (Musk)
3. The core customer base is the offended demographic (Target)
4. National pride is involved (Canada, Europe)

**Boycotts fail when:**
1. The company is a monopoly/essential service (Amazon, Meta)
2. There's no affordable alternative (Walmart)
3. The boycott requires actual sacrifice (convenience, price)

---

# 🧠 TRUMP'S MENTAL FITNESS — THE GROWING CONCERN

> Added March 5, 2026. Public concern about Trump's cognitive state is now approaching the same levels that forced Biden out of the 2024 race. Multiple experts, a former White House attorney, a family member, allied heads of state, and even Steve Bannon have raised the alarm.

---

## THE POLLING

| Poll | Finding |
|------|---------|
| **Reuters/Ipsos** | **61%** say Trump has "become erratic with age" — including **30% of Republicans** |
| **ABC/WaPo/Ipsos** | **56%** say Trump doesn't have the mental sharpness to serve effectively (+13 points since May 2023) |

For context: Biden was at ~62% when he dropped out. **Trump is approaching that threshold.**

---

## THE INCIDENTS — A TIMELINE

| Date | Incident | Details |
|------|----------|---------|
| **Sep 2025** | UN General Assembly | Spent extended time complaining about a broken teleprompter and escalator before making unsubstantiated claims |
| **Oct 2025** | "Razin Caine" | Said "Whoever disappears in Razin Caine is no good... raise your hand" — left military leaders and viewers confused. Went viral |
| **Oct 2025** | Wandered off in Tokyo | Video of Trump wandering away from Japan's first female PM Sanae Takaichi at Akasaka Palace |
| **Jan 2026** | Davos speech | Rambling, slurred speech at World Economic Forum — railed against windmills, relitigated 2020, demanded Greenland. Room was dead silent |
| **Jan 2026** | "Dear Jonas" letter | Sent threatening letter to Norway's PM, citing his perceived Nobel Prize snub as justification for tariffs on allies. Senator: "He isn't OK" |
| **Jan 2026** | Didn't know American hostage | Asked about Dennis Coyle (American held by Taliban for nearly a year), Trump said "Well, if you give me the name" — the host had *just* said it |
| **Feb 2026** | "Champion of Coal" | Slurred: "I'm proud to officially name the undispuut..." then muttered unintelligible sounds for ~2 seconds. Newsom: "The sundowning starts earlier every day" |
| **Mar 2026** | AI / "The Grid" speech | Slurred repeatedly while rambling about "fixing the grid." Lincoln Project circulated the clip |

---

## WHO'S TALKING

### People Who Know Him Personally

| Person | Relationship | What They Said |
|--------|-------------|----------------|
| **Mary Trump** (niece) | Family | "Donald has never been fit in any capacity... age-related cognitive declines compounded by serious, undiagnosed and untreated psychiatric disorders, which are only going to worsen" |
| **Ty Cobb** (former WH attorney) | Worked for him | "The dementia and the cognitive decline are palpable" — called it "significant decline" |
| **Steve Bannon** (former chief strategist) | Inner circle | Newly released Epstein investigation texts show Bannon discussed **removing Trump via the 25th Amendment** back in 2018 — over the same concerns |

### Medical/Psychiatric Experts

| Expert | Assessment |
|--------|-----------|
| **Dr. Bandy Lee** (Yale psychiatrist) | Identified "incoherence, impaired memory, and confabulation" (filling memory gaps with fabricated details), plus amplification of paranoid and antisocial personality traits |
| **Drs. John Gartner & Harry Segal** (clinical psychologists) | Trump's public appearances "increasingly show signs of early dementia" |
| **Dr. Vin Gupta** (NBC medical analyst) | Said behavior "crossed a line of proper adult behavior" — could indicate early Alzheimer's or frontotemporal dementia |
| **Robert Reich** (former Labor Secretary) | "Showing growing signs of dementia... increasingly unhinged. He's 79 with a family history of dementia" |

### Elected Officials

| Official | What They Said |
|----------|---------------|
| **Sen. Brian Schatz (D-HI)** | "He is not stable at all, and his reality is warped" |
| **Sen. Ed Markey (D-MA)** | Formally called on Cabinet and VP Vance to invoke the 25th Amendment |
| **Gov. JB Pritzker (D-IL)** | Called for 25th Amendment removal, citing "mental unfitness and authoritarian threats" |
| **An unnamed Senator** | "He isn't OK. He's degraded significantly in the last year, and he's about to get us into a war with our allies" |

### International Leaders

| Leader | What They Said |
|--------|---------------|
| **Lars-Christian Brask** (Deputy Speaker, Danish Parliament) | "With this mad and erratic behavior, you have to ask the question: Is the president capable of running the United States?" |

---

## THE 25TH AMENDMENT — CAN HE BE REMOVED?

### How It Works (Section 4)

1. The **Vice President** and a **majority of the Cabinet** must declare the President "unable to discharge the powers and duties of his office"
2. VP immediately becomes Acting President
3. If the President contests it, **Congress votes** — requires **2/3 of both chambers** to keep the President removed

### Why It Won't Happen

| Obstacle | Reality |
|----------|---------|
| **VP Vance** | Would need to lead the effort — and Vance owes his career to Trump |
| **The Cabinet** | Entirely Trump loyalists. Pete Hegseth, Tulsi Gabbard, Kash Patel — none would vote to remove |
| **Congress** | Even if Cabinet acted, Trump would contest and you'd need 2/3 of both chambers (same bar as impeachment conviction) |
| **The Brennan Center** | Called it "the unworkable amendment" — designed for medical emergencies (coma, surgery), not political fitness disputes |

### The Real Risk

The 25th Amendment is a dead letter. But the **underlying condition** — if real — is not. A president with cognitive decline:
- Is **more susceptible to manipulation** by advisors (Vance, Miller, Bannon)
- Makes **more erratic decisions** (Greenland letter, Iran escalation, threatening allies)
- Is **less able to course-correct** when policies fail
- Creates a **power vacuum** that unelected figures fill

The question isn't whether Trump will be removed via the 25th. He won't. The question is **who is actually running the country** if the concerns are valid.

---

## THE OFFICIAL WHITE HOUSE POSITION

- **April 2025:** Walter Reed physical — scored **30/30 on MoCA** (Montreal Cognitive Assessment). WH: "No obvious cognitive impairment detected"
- **July 2025:** Diagnosed with **chronic venous insufficiency** (reduced blood flow to limbs — explains bruised hands, swollen ankles)
- **WH spokesperson:** "President Trump's mental sharpness is second to none"

### The MoCA Problem

Experts note that the MoCA is a **screening tool, not a diagnostic one** — it catches moderate-to-severe impairment but can miss early-stage decline. It asks you to draw a clock and name animals. **Reagan would have passed it in 1985** — and he was already showing signs of Alzheimer's.

---

## HISTORICAL PARALLEL

| President | Condition | Who Actually Governed | How Long Hidden |
|-----------|----------|----------------------|-----------------|
| **Woodrow Wilson** | Massive stroke (1919) | Wife Edith Wilson + aides | 17 months — until end of term |
| **FDR** | Severe cardiovascular disease | Inner circle managed schedule | Died in office (April 1945) |
| **Reagan** | Early Alzheimer's (likely by 1986) | Chief of Staff, Nancy Reagan | Not publicly confirmed until 1994 |

In every case, the inner circle **covered for the President** rather than invoke constitutional mechanisms. There is no historical precedent for a Cabinet removing a President via the 25th Amendment.

---

# 📁 THE EPSTEIN FILES — WHERE IT STANDS (March 5, 2026)

> The Epstein Files Transparency Act was signed by Trump in November 2025. What followed is one of the most explosive document releases in modern American history — and a growing cover-up scandal involving Trump's own DOJ.

---

## TIMELINE

| Date | Event |
|------|-------|
| **Jul 2025** | DOJ claims no Epstein "client list" exists. Bipartisan outrage. Congress mandates full release |
| **Nov 2025** | Epstein Files Transparency Act passes unanimously in Senate. Trump signs it |
| **Dec 19, 2025** | First batch released — widely criticized for **excessive redactions** |
| **Jan 30, 2026** | **3 million+ pages** released, plus 2,000+ videos and 180,000+ images. DOJ says it's fulfilled its obligations |
| **Feb 1, 2026** | Attorneys for **200+ victims** ask federal judges to take down the DOJ Epstein site — names of victims were NOT redacted, while names of abusers WERE |
| **Feb 6, 2026** | DOJ opens a "reading room" — lawmakers can view unredacted files in person, no electronic devices allowed |
| **Feb 9, 2026** | Reps. **Massie (R)** and **Khanna (D)** review unredacted files, criticize DOJ. Khanna: "If we found six men they were hiding in two hours, imagine how many men they are covering up for" |
| **Feb 10, 2026** | **Khanna reads 6 names** on the House floor from unredacted files |
| **Feb 24, 2026** | **NPR investigation** reveals DOJ withheld and removed files related to Trump |
| **Mar 4, 2026** | DOJ admits to **removing 47,635 files** from public database |
| **Mar 4, 2026** | House Oversight Committee **subpoenas AG Pam Bondi** (24-19 vote, 5 Republicans cross over) |

---

## THE COVER-UP: DOJ REMOVING TRUMP-RELATED FILES

This is the biggest sub-story. Here's what NPR found:

### What Was Removed

- **47,635 files** removed from the publicly available database — links now return "page not found"
- Among them: **FBI interview notes with a woman who alleges Trump sexually abused her when she was a minor**
- The FBI interviewed this accuser **4 times**. Only the first interview (July 24, 2019) — which does NOT mention Trump — is in the public database
- Of **15 documents** listed for this accuser, only **7** remain available
- Also removed: **50+ pages of FBI interviews** and notes mentioning Trump alongside Epstein accusations

### DOJ's Response

DOJ spokesperson: "We have not deleted any files from the library" — claims they were taken down for "redactions" and will be restored. As of March 5, they have not been restored.

### What's Still Missing

The DOJ released ~3.5 million pages. Lawmakers say the full Epstein file set is **over 6 million pages**. That means roughly **1.45 million pages** remain unreleased. DOJ claims these include:
- Duplicates
- Attorney-client privileged material
- Materials depicting violence
- Items "unrelated to the case"

Congress does not accept this explanation.

---

## WHAT THE FILES SHOW

### Trump — 1,800+ Mentions

A search of "Donald Trump" on the DOJ Epstein site yielded **1,800+ hits**. These include:
- News articles Epstein shared about Trump
- Epstein's commentary about Trump to journalists and associates
- **FBI-compiled list of sexual assault allegations** against Trump (August 2025)
- Flight logs, phone records, communications

DOJ said the sexual assault allegations against Trump in the documents "were false." No public evidence they were deemed credible by the FBI.

### Steve Bannon — Closer to Epstein Than Known

- Files reveal Bannon was in **much more regular contact** with Epstein than previously reported
- **Video released** of Bannon interviewing Epstein in 2019 — Bannon asks him if he thinks he's "the devil"
- Separately, Bannon texts (from the separate Epstein *investigation*) show him discussing **removing Trump via the 25th Amendment** in 2018

### Other Names

| Person | What the Files Show |
|--------|-------------------|
| **Navy Secretary John Phelan** | On two 2006 flight manifests — NY to London with Epstein and back |
| **Bill Gates** | March 2017 email: Epstein encouraged Gates to meet Tom Barrack |
| **Bill & Hillary Clinton** | Both gave closed-door depositions to House Oversight. Bill's longstanding Epstein connections re-examined |
| **Commerce Secretary Howard Lutnick** | Under scrutiny for Epstein ties — agreed to committee interview, no date set |
| **6 unnamed wealthy men** | Names found by Khanna/Massie in unredacted files but missing from public database |

---

## WHAT HAPPENS NEXT

| Action | Status |
|--------|--------|
| **AG Bondi subpoena** | Passed March 4. Closed-door testimony with video to be released. No date yet |
| **Howard Lutnick interview** | Agreed to appear. No date set |
| **1.45 million unreleased pages** | DOJ says they're reviewing. Congress says they're stalling |
| **Parallel Democratic investigation** | House Oversight Dems investigating DOJ's decision to remove Trump-related documents |
| **Victim lawsuits** | 200+ victims' attorneys fighting over redactions — victims exposed, abusers protected |
| **May Day deadline?** | Some lawmakers pushing for full release by May 1, 2026 |

### The Political Dynamics

This is one of the rare **genuinely bipartisan** issues. The subpoena vote included:
- **Nancy Mace (R)** — leading the push
- **Tim Burchett (R-TN)**, **Lauren Boebert (R-CO)**, **Michael Cloud (R-TX)**, **Scott Perry (R-PA)** — all crossed party lines
- **Marjorie Taylor Greene** reportedly resigned partly over this — she wanted full release, Trump allies didn't

The irony: **Trump signed the Transparency Act** expecting it to damage Democrats (Clintons). Instead, his own DOJ is now removing files that mention *him*.

---

## "START A WAR TO MAKE IT GO AWAY" — THE FAKE AUDIO AND THE REAL CONCERN

### The Viral Recording: FAKE

In late February/early March 2026, audio clips circulated on social media appearing to show Trump saying he'd start a war to distract from the Epstein files. **These are confirmed AI-generated fakes**, created using OpenAI's Sora 2. Snopes and PolitiFact both debunked them. The original came from TikTok user @fresh_florida_air.

⚠️ **Any "leaked audio" of Trump talking about Epstein/wars/elections should be treated with extreme skepticism.** AI audio fakes are now indistinguishable from real recordings.

### But the Real Political Argument Is Very Much Alive

Even without fake audio, **the timeline speaks for itself:**

| Date | Epstein Event | Military/Political Event |
|------|--------------|------------------------|
| **Jan 30** | 3 million pages released | — |
| **Feb 9** | Khanna/Massie review unredacted files, read names on House floor | — |
| **Feb 24** | NPR reveals DOJ removing Trump-related files | — |
| **Feb 28** | — | **Iran airstrikes begin** |
| **Mar 4** | Bondi subpoenaed | Iran Day 5, Senate war powers vote fails |

**Rep. Thomas Massie (R)** — co-sponsor of the Transparency Act: "Bombing a country on the other side of the globe won't make the Epstein files go away."

**Marjorie Taylor Greene:** "For years we demanded to release the Epstein files... Instead, we get a war with Iran on behalf of Israel."

**Al Jazeera analyst:** Google searches for "Epstein files" **plummeted** after the Iran strikes began.

**Maine Senate candidate Graham Platner (D):** Directly accused Trump of launching the Iran war to bury the Epstein files, calling Trump's allies "the Epstein class."

No one can prove causation. But the *correlation* is striking, and it's now a mainstream political argument — not just a fringe theory.

---

## "WE SHOULDN'T EVEN HAVE AN ELECTION" — TRUMP'S THREATS TO 2026 VOTING

### What Trump Has Actually Said (On the Record)

| Date | Statement | Context |
|------|-----------|---------|
| **Jan 14, 2026** | "We should take over the voting... nationalize the voting in at least 15 places" | Dan Bongino podcast |
| **Jan 14, 2026** | "When you think of it, we shouldn't even have an election" | Reuters interview |
| **Feb 13, 2026** | Will issue executive order for national voter-ID requirements | Press conference |
| **Feb 2026** | "NO MAIL-IN BALLOTS (EXCEPT FOR ILLNESS, DISABILITY, MILITARY, OR TRAVEL!)" | Truth Social |
| **Dec 7, 2020** | "Who's gonna stop you?" — pressured Georgia House Speaker to call special session to overturn results | Newly surfaced recording (Dec 2025) |

WH Press Secretary Leavitt said the "shouldn't even have an election" comment was Trump "simply joking" and "speaking facetiously."

### The SAVE America Act — "Show Your Papers" Voting

The legislative vehicle for Trump's election agenda:

| Requirement | Details |
|-------------|---------|
| **Proof of citizenship to register** | Valid US passport, OR birth certificate + photo ID |
| **Photo ID at the polls** | Required for all voters |
| **Mail-in voting restrictions** | Trump wants near-total ban (only illness/disability/military/travel) |
| **Hand-marked paper ballots** | Draft EO would require nationwide |
| **Re-registration** | Draft EO proposes all voters re-register with proof of citizenship for 2026 |

**Status:** Passed the House **218-213** (all but one Democrat voted no). Now in Senate — needs 60 votes (filibuster). Republicans have 53. **Sen. Lisa Murkowski (R-AK) opposes it.** Likely dead in the Senate.

### The Draft Executive Order

A leaked **17-page draft executive order** would give Trump extraordinary power over the 2026 midterms:
- Require hand-marked paper ballots nationwide
- Require all voters to re-register with proof of citizenship
- Give federal government oversight of state election administration

Trump denied he was "mulling" the order. But the draft exists.

### The Suppression Playbook

| Threat | Status |
|--------|--------|
| **SAVE America Act** | Passed House 218-213. Has 50 Senate votes but needs 60. **Effectively dead.** Thune (Feb 25): "There is not a unified Republican conference" to break filibuster. Murkowski and McConnell oppose. Collins supports the bill but opposes killing filibuster to pass it. Talking filibuster gambit also rejected. |
| **National voter-ID EO** | Threatened, not yet issued. Courts would likely block |
| **ICE/National Guard at polls** | Democrats warn this is being planned. NPR: election officials "preparing for interference" |
| **Cancel midterms outright** | Trump floated it. **He cannot legally do this.** Elections are administered by states, not the federal government. The Constitution gives Congress no mechanism to cancel congressional elections |
| **Mail-in voting ban** | Would require legislation. 46% of 2024 voters used mail/early voting. Can't be done by EO |

### The Center for American Progress Warning

If the SAVE America Act passes and is fully implemented, the 2026 elections would become **"practically unadministrable"** — millions of eligible voters would be unable to prove citizenship in time, creating mass disenfranchisement.

### The Constitutional Bottom Line

- **Can Trump cancel the 2026 elections?** No. States run elections. The Constitution mandates congressional elections every two years.
- **Can he "nationalize" voting rules?** Congress has some power here, but has never exercised it in 237 years. Any law would face immediate court challenges.
- **Can he deploy troops to polls?** The Posse Comitatus Act restricts it. But he's already violated it in other contexts.
- **Can he ban mail-in voting by EO?** No. States control their own election methods.
- **Can he require re-registration?** Not by executive order. States maintain their own voter rolls.

**The real danger isn't that Trump cancels elections outright. It's that he makes voting so difficult — ID requirements, re-registration, ICE at polls, mail-in restrictions — that turnout drops enough to save Republican majorities.**

---

# ✈️ THE F-22 RAPTOR — AMERICA'S $79 BILLION GHOST GOES TO WAR

> Added March 5, 2026. Yes, F-22s are deployed to the Iran war. And while they've technically seen *limited* combat before, this is the first time they've been used in a full-scale air war against a nation-state with real air defenses — which is **exactly what they were built for.**

---

## THE F-22'S COMBAT HISTORY — VERY THIN UNTIL NOW

The F-22 Raptor is the most expensive fighter program in history ($79 billion total). Only **187 were ever built** before production ended in 2011. For years, critics called it a Cold War relic that would never see real combat.

| Date | Operation | What Happened |
|------|-----------|--------------|
| **Sep 2014** | Syria / ISIS (Operation Inherent Resolve) | **First-ever combat mission.** Hit a single ISIS "command and control building." 204 sorties, 270 bombs on 60 locations total through mid-2015. But ISIS had **zero air defenses** — critics said any plane could've done it |
| **Feb 2018** | Syria / Khasham | Supported strikes against pro-Assad and Russian Wagner Group forces |
| **Nov 2017** | Afghanistan / Taliban | Bombed opium production facilities alongside B-52s |
| **Feb 2023** | Chinese spy balloon | **First air-to-air kill** — shot down the balloon at 60,000–65,000 feet off South Carolina. Historic but... it was a balloon |
| **Jun 2025** | Iran / "Midnight Hammer" (12-Day War) | Escorted B-2 bombers hitting Iran's nuclear facilities. Used to **draw out surface-to-air missile fire** ahead of bombing runs. First use against real air defenses |
| **Feb 28, 2026** | Iran / Operation Epic Fury | **Full-scale deployment.** 11 F-22s at Israel's Ovda Air Base — first-ever US combat aircraft deployed TO Israel. Part of the largest US air campaign since 2003 Iraq invasion |

### The Key Point

Before Iran, the F-22's combat record was almost embarrassing for a $79 billion program — bombing ISIS camps with no air opposition, and shooting down a weather balloon. **Iran is the first time the F-22 is being used as intended**: against a nation-state with Russian-supplied S-300 air defense systems, fighter jets, and integrated radar networks.

---

## WHAT THE F-22 IS DOING IN OPERATION EPIC FURY

| Role | Details |
|------|---------|
| **Air superiority** | Clearing Iranian airspace of fighters — retired Lt. Gen. Guastella: "the most air-to-air capable fighter in the world; nothing comes close" |
| **SEAD (Suppression of Enemy Air Defenses)** | Drawing fire from Iranian S-300 systems to reveal their positions for follow-up strikes |
| **Escort** | Protecting B-2 and B-52 bombers during deep-penetration runs on nuclear sites, command bunkers, missile batteries |
| **ISR (Intelligence, Surveillance, Reconnaissance)** | The F-22's sensors can map enemy positions while remaining undetected |

### The Stealth Advantage

An F-22 reportedly **flew directly under an Iranian fighter jet undetected** during the June 2025 12-Day War, then radioed the Iranian pilot: "You really ought to go home." The Iranian pilot had no idea the F-22 was there.

---

## THE NUMBERS IN THE REGION

| Aircraft | Quantity | Base/Carrier |
|----------|---------|-------------|
| **F-22 Raptor** | 11 | Ovda Air Base, Israel |
| **F-35A/B/C** | ~48 | Multiple bases + carriers |
| **F-15E Strike Eagle** | ~36 | European/Gulf bases |
| **F-16** | Unknown | Gulf bases |
| **A-10 Warthog** | Unknown | Gulf bases |
| **B-2 Spirit** | Classified (likely 3-6) | Diego Garcia / Whiteman AFB |
| **B-52H** | ~12 | Diego Garcia |
| **EA-18G Growler** | ~12 | Carrier-based (electronic warfare) |

Plus **two carrier strike groups** (USS Gerald R. Ford, USS Abraham Lincoln), Tomahawk-capable destroyers/cruisers, and aerial refueling/AWACS support.

**This is the highest concentration of US air power since the 2003 invasion of Iraq.**

---

## WHY IT MATTERS

The F-22 was designed in the 1980s to fight the Soviet Union. It was built in the 1990s-2000s. It sat on the bench through Iraq, Afghanistan, Libya, and most of Syria. Production ended in 2011 because Congress decided we'd never fight a peer adversary.

Now, with only 187 ever made and fewer combat-ready at any time, we're burning through their airframe hours against Iran. These planes **cannot be replaced** — the production line is closed, the tooling was destroyed. Every hour an F-22 flies over Iran is an hour it can't fly in a future conflict (China/Taiwan, for example).

Deploying 11 of ~120 combat-coded F-22s to a single theater is a **massive commitment** for an irreplaceable asset.

---

# 🚨 BREAKING: NOEM FIRED — FIRST CABINET SECRETARY TO FALL (March 5, 2026)

> Trump fired DHS Secretary Kristi Noem today. She is the **first Cabinet member to depart Trump's second term.** Replaced by Sen. Markwayne Mullin (R-OK), effective March 31.

---

## WHY SHE WAS FIRED

### The Minneapolis Disaster

The immediate cause: **Operation Metro Surge** in Minneapolis, where Noem deployed 3,000 federal officers for an immigration enforcement surge. Two US citizens were killed:

| Victim | What Happened |
|--------|--------------|
| **Renee Nicole Good** | Killed during ICE operation in January 2026. Her death triggered the Minneapolis general strike (~100,000 people) |
| **Alex Pretti** | Shot **multiple times at close range** as he tried to help a woman pushed to the ground. Had a registered gun but **never displayed it** |

Noem labeled both as "domestic terrorists" — then **refused six times** in Senate testimony to retract it, even after other federal officials confirmed there was no evidence of terrorism.

**~190 members of Congress** co-sponsored articles of impeachment against Noem after the Pretti shooting.

### The $143 Million Corruption Scandal

- Noem awarded a **$220 million no-bid contract** to "Safe America Media" for DHS ads
- Safe America subcontracted **$143 million** to "The Strategy Group" — run by the **husband of former DHS spokesperson Tricia McLaughlin**
- ProPublica investigation exposed the connection
- Multiple senators demanded answers; Noem refused to provide them

### The FEMA Catastrophe

- **Required personal approval** on all FEMA expenses over $100,000 — bottlenecking Hurricane Helene disaster relief
- Cycled through **3 acting FEMA administrators** in one year
- Presided over mass FEMA cuts while disaster victims waited
- Sen. Tillis (R-NC) threatened to **block ALL Trump nominees** until Noem answered questions about FEMA money being held up in North Carolina

### The Senate Hearing That Ended Her (March 3)

The final straw was a brutal two-day Senate Judiciary hearing:
- **Sen. Tillis (R-NC):** Called her tenure "a disaster," accused her of violating the law
- **Sen. Murkowski (R-AK):** Demanded resignation
- **Sen. Kennedy (R-LA):** After the hearing, Trump called Kennedy. Kennedy told CBS: "He was pissed" — Trump's version of events didn't match Noem's testimony
- **Sen. Fetterman (D-PA):** "Immediately fire her. She is betraying DHS's core mission"
- **Rep. Raskin (D-MD):** Pressed her on calling Pretti a domestic terrorist — she refused to answer 6 times

**Two days later: fired.**

---

## THE REPLACEMENT: SEN. MARKWAYNE MULLIN (R-OK) — "A MAGA WARRIOR AND MMA FIGHTER"

| Detail | Info |
|--------|------|
| **Age** | 48 (born July 26, 1977, Tulsa, OK) |
| **Current role** | US Senator from Oklahoma (since 2023) |
| **Previous** | US House of Representatives (2013-2023), 10 years |
| **Education** | No bachelor's degree — only sitting senator without one |
| **Heritage** | Enrolled citizen of Cherokee Nation — first tribal citizen in the Senate in nearly 20 years |
| **MMA record** | **5-0 professional** (Nov 2006 – Apr 2007) |
| **Business** | Plumbing company (Mullin Plumbing), grew it to $50M+ revenue |
| **Confirmation** | Requires Senate vote — date TBD |
| **Start date** | Trump says March 31, 2026 |

### The Personality: "Stand Your Butt Up"

Mullin's defining characteristic is **physical aggression in political settings.** This is the man Trump chose to run the department that controls ICE, Border Patrol, the Coast Guard, FEMA, Secret Service, and TSA.

| Incident | What Happened |
|----------|--------------|
| **Nov 2023 — Sean O'Brien fistfight** | During a Senate hearing, Mullin stood up, started removing his ring, and challenged Teamsters president O'Brien to fight: **"This is the time, this is the place. Stand your butt up."** Bernie Sanders had to bang the gavel and yell "You're a United States senator!" to stop it. Next day, Mullin said on a podcast: **"I'm not afraid of biting. I will bite... I'm not above it."** |
| **Feb 2026 — Al Green confrontation** | Before Trump's State of the Union, Mullin physically tried to grab a protest sign from Rep. Al Green (D-TX) on the House floor. Video went viral. Later posted: "I cannot stand the man from Texas called Al Green" |
| **Jan 2025 — Hegseth defense** | Defended Pete Hegseth against alcohol abuse allegations by accusing fellow senators of workplace intoxication |

### The O'Brien Plot Twist

After the near-fistfight, Trump actually **brokered a reconciliation** between Mullin and O'Brien. They're now reportedly friends who speak every few weeks. This relationship is believed to have influenced O'Brien's decision **not to endorse the Democratic ticket in 2024** — which was a significant blow to the Harris campaign.

### Ethics Issues

Mullin faced a multi-year House ethics investigation for continued involvement in his family's businesses while serving. The committee concluded he made "good faith efforts" but required him to return **$40,000 "mistakenly paid to him."**

---

## MULLIN vs. NOEM — WHAT CHANGES?

| Dimension | Noem | Mullin |
|-----------|------|--------|
| **Background** | Governor (executive experience) | Senator/House (legislative, no executive experience) |
| **Management style** | Micromanager (demanded personal sign-off on FEMA spending >$100K) | Unknown — no executive track record |
| **Immigration** | Hard-line but **operationally incompetent** (Minneapolis disaster, $220M ad scandal) | Hard-line and **personally aggressive** (physically confrontational) |
| **Relationship with Trump** | Sycophantic but fell out of favor | MAGA loyalist, personally close — Trump brokered his friendship with O'Brien |
| **Congressional relations** | Bipartisan hatred by end of tenure | Known for getting along across the aisle *when he's not trying to fight people* |
| **Temperament** | Defensive, evasive (refused to retract "domestic terrorist" label 6 times) | Hot-headed, confrontational, physically threatening |
| **FEMA** | Catastrophic — bottlenecked Helene relief | Unknown |
| **Senate confirmation** | Was confirmed for DHS | Will need confirmation — likely passes but expect pointed questions |

### The Concern

Noem's problem was **incompetence**. She couldn't manage the department, couldn't manage the optics, and couldn't manage the money.

Mullin's potential problem is **temperament**. This is a man who:
- Tried to start a fistfight during a Senate hearing
- Said he's "not above biting"
- Physically grabbed a protest sign from a congressman
- Has no executive management experience
- Will be running a department with 260,000+ employees, including armed federal agents who just killed two US citizens

The question: **Does Trump want someone who can manage DHS, or someone who will be more aggressive than Noem?** The answer appears to be the latter.

### What This Means for the DHS Shutdown

DHS is in **Day 19 of a partial shutdown** — Democrats forced it after the Minneapolis shootings. Noem's firing removes a key obstacle but doesn't resolve it. Democrats demanded changes to ICE enforcement practices, not just a personnel swap. Mullin's reputation for physical aggression may make negotiations *harder*, not easier.

### Will Mullin Get Confirmed?

**Almost certainly yes.** Here's why:

| Factor | Details |
|--------|---------|
| **Senatorial courtesy** | The Senate almost always confirms one of its own members. Mullin is personally liked by colleagues on both sides |
| **Fetterman (D-PA)** | Already announced he's voting YES: "I'm not sure how many fellow Democrats will vote to support our colleague @SenMullin as the next DHS Secretary, but I am AYE" |
| **Tillis (R-NC)** | Called him "a great guy and a great choice to lead DHS" — and joked: "Another big positive: he likes dogs" (Noem dig) |
| **Graham (R-SC)** | "One of the most knowledgeable people I know regarding how to protect America" |
| **Vacancy Act** | Even before confirmation, Mullin can serve as **acting DHS Secretary** as long as his nomination is pending — so delay doesn't stop him |

### The Democratic Calculation

Democrats *could* try to use the confirmation hearing as leverage on the DHS shutdown / ICE reform demands. But:
- They lack the votes to block (need 50+1 to deny, Republicans have 52 without Mullin)
- Fetterman already broke ranks
- Blocking a popular colleague would look petty during a war
- Mullin explicitly said: "We're not going to keep ICE from doing their job"

**Prediction: Confirmed with 65-75 votes**, including 10-20 Democrats. The hearing will be contentious but the outcome is not in doubt.

### The Oklahoma Senate Seat

Mullin's departure creates a vacancy:
- **Gov. Kevin Stitt (R)** will appoint a temporary replacement
- Oklahoma will elect a senator in November 2026
- Filing deadline: April 3, 2026
- Primary: June 16, 2026
- Oklahoma is R+20 — no Democrat has won statewide since 2006
- **4 Democrats filed** (Troy Green, Rebekah LaVann, Jim Priest, N'Kiyla Thomas) — but all underfunded and low-profile
- **Net effect on Senate math: almost certainly zero**

### BUT — The Texas Lesson

You're right to push back. Look at what just happened **two days ago** in Texas:

| Texas Data Point | Number |
|-----------------|--------|
| **State lean** | R+14 (Trump won by 14 in 2024) |
| **Cornyn vs. Talarico polling** | Cornyn **+1** (44-43). ONE point. In TEXAS. |
| **Paxton vs. Talarico** | Paxton +2 (46-44) |
| **Campaign spending** | **$122 million** — a record for a Senate race |
| **Cornyn forced to runoff** | Couldn't clear 50% against scandal-plagued Ken Paxton. Runoff May 26 |
| **Talarico** | Won Dem primary cleanly, can now focus on general while Rs tear each other apart |

Texas was rated **"Likely Republican"** by every major forecaster. It's now polling within the margin of error. In 2018, Beto came within 3 points of Cruz — and the political environment is *worse* for Rs now than it was then.

### The Broader Red State Picture

| State | Incumbent | Lean | Why It Could Surprise |
|-------|-----------|------|----------------------|
| **Texas** | Cornyn (R) | R+14 | Polling at +1. Cornyn forced into ugly runoff with Paxton. Talarico is strong. $122M spent |
| **Iowa** | OPEN (Ernst retiring) | R+12 | Ernst quitting. Open seat in a wave year. Iowa swung 18 points D in 2018 |
| **Nebraska** | Ricketts (R) | R+20 | Dan Osborn (I) lost by only 6 in 2024 (vs Trump +20). Running again. NE Dems endorsed him, not fielding their own candidate |
| **Oklahoma** | OPEN (Mullin to DHS) | R+20 | Open seat, but no credible Dem candidate. Probably the least competitive of these |
| **Florida** | Scott (R) | R+7 | Scott barely won in 2024 (+1.2%). But no top-tier Dem has entered yet |
| **Alaska** | Sullivan (R) | R+9 | Ranked choice voting + Murkowski factor. But Sullivan is popular |
| **North Carolina** | Tillis (R, retiring) | R+3 | OPEN seat. NC elected a Dem governor in 2024. Very competitive |
| **Ohio** | Vance (to VP, appointee) | R+7 | Appointee Bernie Moreno never won a general. Ohio still has swing DNA |

### What "R+20" Actually Means in a Wave

In a normal year, R+20 means safe. But waves can move margins **15-20 points:**
- 2018 (Blue wave): Texas moved from R+20 to R+3. Iowa moved from R+10 to D+3.
- Beto lost by 2.6 in R+14 Texas
- If the 2026 environment is +13 D (current special election average), that brings an R+20 state down to... R+7. Still Republican. But no longer laughable.

**Oklahoma specifically?** Still very unlikely to flip. No Democratic infrastructure, no top-tier candidate, no ranked choice voting. But the Mullin vacancy + open seat + wave year means it's worth watching. Stranger things have happened — Doug Jones won *Alabama* in 2017.

**Texas is the real story.** A +1 race in Texas would be the biggest Senate upset in modern history.

---

## NOEM'S "SOFT LANDING"

Trump gave her a new title: **"Envoy for The Shield of the Americas"** — described as leading a "new Security Initiative in the Western Hemisphere." This is almost certainly a made-up role to avoid the optics of a pure firing. It has no confirmed budget, staff, or authority.

---

## THE BIGGER PICTURE

Noem is the **9th senior Trump official** to leave/be fired in 14 months. The turnover rate in Trump's second term is tracking ahead of his first (which set modern records):

| Official | Role | Departed |
|----------|------|---------|
| **Kristi Noem** | DHS Secretary | March 5, 2026 (fired) |
| **Marjorie Taylor Greene** | House member | Resigned (Epstein clash) |
| **3 acting FEMA administrators** | FEMA | Cycled out under Noem |
| **Multiple inspectors general** | Various | Fired in mass purge |

The pattern: loyalty gets you in, but incompetence — or becoming a political liability — still gets you out. Noem survived the dog-shooting book scandal, the plagiarism scandal, and months of bipartisan criticism. What she didn't survive was **making Trump look bad on live TV** and then giving testimony that contradicted what Trump told senators privately.

# 🎯 HOMELAND ATTACK RISK — HOW REAL IS IT?

> Added March 5, 2026. With Iran's supreme leader killed and the regime facing an existential threat, every expert agrees: **the risk of retaliation on US soil is the highest it's been since 9/11.** The question is what form it takes.

---

## THE THREAT LEVEL

| Source | Assessment |
|--------|-----------|
| **DHS** | "Heightened threat environment in the United States" — no specific credible threats identified as of March 5 |
| **FBI** | Counterterrorism teams on high alert. JTTF actively monitoring pro-Iran networks. Personnel redirected to CT roles |
| **Colin Clarke (Soufan Center)** | "For Iran, this war is existential. I would fully expect Tehran to activate any sleeper cell capacity it has in the West" |
| **Google Threat Intelligence** | "We expect Iran to target the U.S., Israel, and Gulf Cooperation Council countries with disruptive cyberattacks" |
| **Fortune** | Iran is on "death ground" — an existential threat with "no incentive to hold anything back" |
| **West Point CTC** | Published specific analysis of "terror pathways for Iran to strike in the United States" |

### Iran's Pre-War Warning

Before the strikes, Iran reportedly sent a direct message to Trump threatening to **"activate sleeper-cell terror inside the United States"** if the US military attacked Iran. The US attacked anyway.

---

## THREAT VECTOR 1: SLEEPER CELLS & PHYSICAL ATTACKS

### What We Know About Iranian/Hezbollah Networks in the US

Hezbollah and Hamas have had a presence in the US **since the 1980s.** Here's what's been documented:

| Evidence | Details |
|----------|---------|
| **Alexei Saab** (convicted Hezbollah operative) | Conducted surveillance of: **UN HQ, Statue of Liberty, Rockefeller Center, Times Square, Empire State Building, airports, tunnels, and bridges** in New York |
| **Saab's statement** | Said the sleeper cell "would expect to be called upon if the U.S. ever went to war with Iran or targeted Hezbollah" — **both lines have now been crossed** |
| **Cell locations** | Major cities initially (New York, Houston, Detroit, Los Angeles, Boston) — after becoming aware of FBI surveillance, operatives reportedly **shifted to smaller cities** to blend in |
| **Iran's threat** | Direct message to Trump pre-war: would "activate sleeper-cell terror inside the United States" |

### Austin, TX Shooting — Under Investigation

On March 1, 2026, a shooting in **Austin, Texas** killed 2 and wounded 14. The FBI is investigating it as a potential act of terrorism:
- Gunman wore a sweatshirt reading **"Property of Allah"**
- Had a T-shirt with the **Iranian flag**
- A **Quran** was found in his vehicle
- FBI Special Agent: "indicators on the gunman and in his vehicle that suggest a potential nexus to terrorism"

⚠️ **No confirmed link to Iran established yet.** Could be a lone wolf inspired by — but not directed by — Iranian intelligence.

### Most Likely Physical Attack Scenarios

| Scenario | Likelihood | Impact |
|----------|-----------|--------|
| **Lone wolf / inspired attacks** | High | Low-medium (individual shootings, vehicle attacks) |
| **Coordinated sleeper cell activation** | Low-medium | Very high (Mumbai-style multi-site attacks) |
| **Attack on US military base / facility** | Medium | High (domestic military installations) |
| **Attack on Jewish/Israeli targets** | Medium-high | Medium (synagogues, cultural centers, businesses) |
| **Infrastructure sabotage** | Low-medium | Very high (power grid, water systems) |

---

## THREAT VECTOR 2: CYBERATTACKS

### Iran's Cyber Capability

Iran has a sophisticated cyber warfare program. Past attacks include:
- 2012: Shamoon virus destroyed 30,000 Saudi Aramco computers
- 2013: Infiltrated a New York dam's control system
- 2020: Attempted to poison a Florida water treatment plant (attributed to Iran-linked actors)
- 2024: Multiple attacks on US water utilities
- 2025: 700% increase in cyberattacks targeting Israel after strikes on Iran

### Current Cyber Threat

| Assessment | Source |
|-----------|--------|
| "Low-to-medium sophistication disruptions" expected in near term | Palo Alto Networks Unit 42 |
| Iran's internet connectivity dropped to **1-4%** after Feb 28 strikes — limiting state-directed operations | Unit 42 |
| Iran-aligned hacktivists **outside Iran** are the bigger near-term threat | CloudSEK |
| Targets: **power grids, water systems, financial networks, communications** | Google Threat Intelligence |

### The Silver Lining (For Now)

Iran's internal internet infrastructure was **heavily degraded** by the strikes — connectivity dropped to 1-4%. This means:
- State-directed sophisticated cyber operations are **temporarily disrupted**
- Leadership/command structures needed to coordinate attacks are damaged
- The biggest cyber threat right now is from **Iran-aligned groups outside Iran** (Iraq, Lebanon, Yemen)

### The Vulnerability

CISA (Cybersecurity and Infrastructure Security Agency) is operating at **reduced capacity** due to:
- DHS partial shutdown (Day 19)
- DOGE-driven workforce cuts eliminated experienced cybersecurity personnel
- FBI's **specialized counterintelligence unit that monitored Iran was reportedly fired** days before Operation Epic Fury

---

## THREAT VECTOR 3: STRAIT OF HORMUZ

Not a homeland attack, but affects every American:

- Iran controls the Strait of Hormuz — **20% of global oil supply** passes through it
- Iran has already struck Gulf state oil infrastructure
- Missiles hit facilities near Abu Dhabi, Doha, Saudi Arabia, Kuwait
- If the Strait is mined or blocked: **oil spikes to $150-200/barrel**, gas hits $6-8/gallon in the US
- This is Iran's most powerful non-nuclear weapon

---

## WHERE IS MOST/LEAST SAFE?

### Higher Risk Areas

| Location | Why |
|----------|-----|
| **New York City** | Documented Hezbollah surveillance targets. Highest-profile symbolic value |
| **Washington, DC** | Government/military targets. Already heavily militarized (2,400 National Guard) |
| **Major military installations** | Especially Navy bases (Fifth Fleet connection) |
| **Jewish community centers / synagogues** | Historical Iranian/Hezbollah targeting pattern |
| **Critical infrastructure** (power plants, water treatment, data centers) | Cyber + physical attack potential |
| **Houston / Detroit / Los Angeles** | Known historical Hezbollah cell presence |

### Lower Risk Areas

| Location | Why |
|----------|-----|
| **Small/medium cities with no military or symbolic value** | Not worth the operational risk for a sophisticated attack |
| **Rural areas** | No strategic targets |
| **Interior states** | Less accessible to foreign operatives |

### Jersey City Specifically

**Moderate risk.** JC is in the NYC metro area, which is the #1 documented target zone for Hezbollah operatives. However:
- JC itself has no iconic symbolic targets
- The Lincoln Tunnel and Holland Tunnel (connecting JC to Manhattan) were on Saab's surveillance list — but as transit infrastructure, not JC targets per se
- NYPD/NJSP counter-terrorism is among the best in the world
- The main risk to JC residents would be a major NYC attack creating regional disruption, not a JC-specific attack

---

## THE BIG PICTURE: PROBABILITY ASSESSMENT

| Scenario | Probability (next 6 months) | Notes |
|----------|----------------------------|-------|
| **No significant homeland attack** | ~50% | FBI/JTTF interdiction, Iran's degraded command structure |
| **Lone wolf / inspired attack(s)** | ~30% | Austin shooting may be the first. Hardest to prevent |
| **Cyberattack on infrastructure** | ~40% | Most likely from Iran-aligned groups outside Iran |
| **Coordinated sleeper cell attack** | ~10% | High impact but requires command structure Iran may have lost |
| **Major 9/11-scale attack** | ~2-5% | Iran's capability is degraded but not zero. Existential motivation is maximum |
| **Strait of Hormuz disruption** | ~60% | Already partially happening. Most likely form of retaliation |

### The Terrible Irony

The agencies that would protect the homeland — FBI counterintelligence, CISA cybersecurity, DHS broadly — have been **gutted by DOGE cuts and the DHS shutdown** in the months leading up to this war. The FBI unit specifically monitoring Iranian threats was reportedly **fired days before the strikes began.**

---

# 📰 LAST 24 HOURS — March 5-6, 2026

---

## 🔥 IRAN WAR — DAY 6-7

### By the Numbers

| **Targets struck** | 1,250+ (first 48 hrs) + ~200 more in last 72 hrs |
| **Cost** | **$3.7 billion** in first 100 hours ($891M/day). Most unbudgeted |
| **US service members killed** | **6** |
| **Iranian deaths** | 550+ (Iran Red Crescent) |

| **IDF waves of strikes on Tehran** | 12 completed |
| **Air power comparison** | SecDef Hegseth: "**Twice the air power of Shock and Awe** (Iraq 2003)" |

### Key Developments (Last 24 Hours)

- **B-2 bombers** dropped dozens of 2,000-pound penetrator bombs on deeply buried ballistic missile launchers near Tehran
- IDF released footage of an **F-35I shooting down an Iranian Yak-130 jet** over Tehran — first confirmed air-to-air kill of the campaign
- IDF killed **Hezbollah intelligence chief Hussein Makled** in overnight strike on Beirut
- US targeting **Iran's space capabilities** — satellites, ground stations, data relay infrastructure
- Iran's **ballistic missile retaliation capacity down 90%**, navy "wiped out," production capacity "being demolished" (Hegseth)
- Iranian FM told NBC: "We have not asked for a ceasefire." When asked about US ground troops: **"No, we are waiting for them"**
- Trump posted on Truth Social: **No deal without "unconditional surrender"** — oil prices hit session highs immediately after
- SecDef Hegseth heading to CENTCOM HQ at MacDill AFB for war update

### Friendly Fire Incident

**Kuwait mistakenly shot down 3 US fighter jets.** Details remain classified but this is the first confirmed friendly fire incident of the campaign.

---

## 🇷🇺 IS RUSSIA JOINING? — NO, BUT...

### The Short Answer

**Russia will not fight America over Iran.** But it IS helping behind the scenes — and a **breaking Washington Post report** (March 6) changes the picture significantly.

### What Russia Is NOT Doing

| Action | Status |
|--------|--------|
| **Sending troops** | No |
| **Providing air cover** | No |
| **Declaring war on US/Israel** | No |
| **Invoking mutual defense** | No — Russia's deputy FM explicitly said the 2025 Russia-Iran treaty is **not a mutual defense pact** |

### What Russia IS Doing

| Action | Source | Details |
|--------|--------|---------|
| 🚨 **Providing targeting intelligence to hit US forces** | **Washington Post (March 6)** | Russia is giving Iran intelligence to target American forces in the Middle East. BREAKING |
| **Spy satellite** | Multiple sources | The Khayyam satellite (Russian-built Kanopus-V) gives Iran 1.2-meter resolution imagery of US/Israeli bases |
| **Su-35 fighter jets** | SpecialEurasia | Delivering 48 Su-35 "Flanker-E" jets (~$6.5B) with electronic warfare pods designed to detect F-35s |
| **Radar systems** | SpecialEurasia | Provided Rezonans-NE over-the-horizon radar capable of tracking stealth aircraft |
| **Missiles & ammunition** | Multiple | Shipped to Tehran |
| **Diplomatic cover** | UN | Called Epic Fury an "unprovoked act of armed aggression." Same day launched 106 missiles at Ukraine |

### What China Is Doing

| Action | Source | Details |
|--------|--------|---------|
| 🚨 **Satellite intelligence** | Pravda/multiple | Transmitting **exact coordinates of US ships and bases** to Iran using its 500+ satellite fleet |
| **BeiDou navigation** | SpecialEurasia | Iran's military switched from GPS to **China's BeiDou-3** — centimeter-level accuracy, jam-resistant, includes encrypted comms even when local networks are down |
| **Air defense systems** | Defense Security Monitor | Delivered HQ-16 and HQ-17AE SAM systems + loitering munitions |
| **Anti-ship missiles** | SpecialEurasia | CM-302 supersonic cruise missiles designed to threaten US Navy ships |
| **Cyber defense** | SpecialEurasia | Replacing Western software in Iran with Chinese systems to prevent CIA/Mossad infiltration |
| **Strait of Hormuz talks** | CNBC | China negotiating with Iran for **safe passage** for Chinese oil tankers through the Strait |

### Why They Won't Go Further

1. **Russia is consuming the same weapons in Ukraine** — can't spare inventory for Iran
2. **China is watching US missile stocks drain** — every Tomahawk fired at Iran is one less available for a Taiwan scenario
3. Neither wants a direct military confrontation with the US
4. Both benefit more from the **war continuing** than from joining it — it drains US resources, diverts attention from Ukraine/Taiwan

### The Strategic Calculation

Russia and China are playing the **long game**: help Iran enough to keep the war going, drain American munitions and money, and wait. A Heritage Foundation report warned that US interceptors (SM-3, SM-6, PAC-3, THAAD) **would be exhausted within days** of sustained combat. China is watching the inventory deplete in real time.

## 🌍 THE PROXY WAR IS EXPANDING

### Hezbollah — Back in the Fight

- **Launched missiles and drone swarm at Israeli military base near Haifa** — first cross-border raid since late 2024
- Israel responded massively: **123 killed, 683 wounded** in Lebanon this week
- IDF killed Hezbollah intelligence chief in Beirut overnight strike
- **Lebanese government formally outlawed Hezbollah's military activities** — PM Salam: "We will not allow the country to be dragged into new adventures"
- But Hezbollah is "a shadow of the force it once was" (CNN) — severely degraded from 2024 war

### Houthis — Finger on the Trigger

- Houthi leader Abdul Malik al-Houthi: **"Our fingers are on the trigger, ready to respond at any moment"**
- Internal debate ongoing — haven't formally re-entered the war yet
- Key difference from 2024: Houthis are now **manufacturing their own weapons in Yemen** — less dependent on Iranian supply
- Analysts say they're weighing: join Iran's war and risk massive US retaliation, or cut ties with a dying regime?

### Iraqi Militias

- Several PMF groups struck US bases in Iraq on Day 2
- Iraqi government pressuring them to stop — doesn't want Iraq dragged in
- Low-level rocket attacks continue

## ✊ RESISTANCE UPDATE — March 5-6, 2026

### Anti-War Protests Erupting

The Iran war has added an entirely new dimension to the resistance — it's no longer just about immigration and democracy. Now it's **anti-war + anti-authoritarian** combined.

| Event | Details |

### March 28 — "The Largest Protest in American History"

The third **No Kings** mobilization is 22 days away and organizers are predicting a historic turnout:

| No Kings # | Date | Attendance |
|-----------|------|-----------|
| **No Kings I** | June 14, 2025 | **5+ million** |

| **No Kings III** | **March 28, 2026** | **9 million expected** — "the largest protest in American history" (Ezra Levin, Indivisible) |

**New this time:** The Iran war. Minneapolis as the flagship location (site of the Pretti/Good killings). 260,000 people have already attended organizer training sessions. AFL-CIO is a co-organizer (labor joining formally for the first time).

If 9 million turn out, that would be **2.7% of the US population** — closing in on the **3.5% threshold** (Harvard Kennedy School / Erica Chenoweth) at which no government in history has survived nonviolent protest.

The ACLU is now fighting on **multiple fronts simultaneously**: immigration, war powers, voting rights, press freedom, DEI, gender-affirming care, and surveillance.

- $2M to League of Conservation Voters
- $1M to Indivisible Project

Right-wing media is using this to frame the resistance as "astroturfed." But the attendance numbers — 5M, 7M, projected 9M — can't be manufactured. You can fund organizers but you can't pay 9 million people to show up.

## 🏭 NEW JERSEY — ICE WAREHOUSE WARS

### This is happening in your backyard.

Two parallel stories in NJ: ICE raiding warehouses to arrest workers, AND buying warehouses to build detention camps.

---

### WAREHOUSE RAIDS — EDISON, NJ

ICE has conducted **at least 3 workplace raids** at Edison warehouses — the most of any NJ city:

| Date | Location | Workers Detained | Details |
|------|----------|-----------------|---------|
| **Jul 2025** | Alba Wine & Spirits, Edison | **15-20** | ICE arrived at 9am, surrounded building |
| **Aug 2025** | 65 Patrick Ave (bonded warehouse), Edison | **29** | ICE operated **drones inside the warehouse** to find workers hiding. Hourslong operation |
| **Later 2025** | Smart Supply Chain, Edison | **13** | Third known enforcement operation |

- Workers detained are being held at **Delaney Hall in Newark** — advocates say conditions are inhumane
- Edison officials confirmed they were notified but **did not participate** — NJ is a sanctuary state
- Rallies held demanding release of detained workers
- Advocates warn this is a **new phase** — workplace raids had largely stopped after Trump 1.0

### Why Warehouses?

NJ's logistics corridor (Edison, Elizabeth, Newark, Carteret) is the largest on the East Coast. Warehouses are **full of immigrant labor** — they store imported goods from the ports. ICE knows exactly where to find workers because **customs bonded warehouses** require federal paperwork that identifies who handles goods.

---

### ICE BUYING WAREHOUSES — ROXBURY, NJ

ICE is also buying warehouses to convert into **detention camps**. The biggest one is 40 minutes from Jersey City.

| Detail | Info |
|--------|------|
| **Location** | 1879 Route 46, Roxbury Township (Morris County) |
| **Size** | **470,000 sq ft** — would be the largest ICE detention facility on the East Coast |
| **Price** | **$129.3 million** |
| **Seller** | Goldman Sachs asset management fund + Dallas-based Dalfen Industrial |
| **Capacity** | Up to **1,500 detainees** |
| **Distance from JC** | ~45 miles / 50 minutes |

### The Opposition — Bipartisan

This is one of the rare issues where **Trump voters and progressives agree**:

| Who | Action |
|-----|--------|
| **Roxbury Township Council** (all-Republican) | Passed resolution opposing ICE's plans |
| **500+ residents** | Rallied outside Ledgewood Commons — environmental and moral concerns |
| **Roxbury Mayor** | "We will act swiftly and aggressively to stop the development of a detention center" — preparing legal challenge |
| **Gov. Mikie Sherrill** | Formally opposed, warned state will use "legal and regulatory tools" |
| **Sens. Booker & Kim** | Introduced **End Warehouse Detention Act** — would ban using federal funds to buy/convert warehouses for detention |
| **Assemblymembers Brennan & Bhalla** | Drafted the **FUCK ICE Act** (Fight Unlawful Conduct and Keep Individuals and Communities Empowered Act) — yes, that's the real acronym |

### The DHS Two-Step

The purchase was chaotic — DHS first told reporters they bought it, then said they hadn't, then confirmed the sale again on Feb 20. They're claiming it will bring 1,300 jobs and $161M in GDP. Nobody in Roxbury is buying it.

### What NJ Is Doing Statewide

| Action | Details |
|--------|---------|
| **Barred ICE from nonpublic state property** without a warrant |
| **Launched video portal** for residents to submit footage of ICE interactions |
| **Sanctuary state status** | Local police cannot assist ICE operations |
| **Hospital protection protocols** being written | To shield patients from ICE |
| **End Warehouse Detention Act** (federal) | Booker/Kim bill to ban warehouse-to-camp conversions |
| **FUCK ICE Act** (state) | Brennan/Bhalla bill to enable civil litigation against ICE |

### Can They Block It? — The Legal Reality

**Short answer: Probably not, but they're going to try everything.**

#### Why It's Hard to Stop

| Legal Principle | What It Means |
|----------------|--------------|
| **Supremacy Clause** | Federal law trumps state/local law. Once the feds own the property, they can largely do what they want |
| **Federal land immunity** | Courts have ruled since the 1950s that the federal government is largely immune from local regulation on land it owns |
| **Oklahoma City precedent** | OKC acknowledged: "federal law explicitly exempts detention centers from local zoning regulations" |
| **Eminent domain threat** | The seller (Goldman Sachs/Dalfen) said they sold **"in lieu of the potential of eminent domain"** — if they'd refused, the government could have seized it anyway, potentially at a lower price |

#### The Zoning Gambit

Roxbury residents demanded the township rezone to make detention facilities a "nonpermitted use." Township Attorney Anthony Bucco (also NJ Senate minority leader) said it would have **"no impact"** — the federal government isn't bound by local zoning on property it owns.

#### Where There IS Legal Daylight

| Strategy | How It Works | Precedent |
|----------|-------------|-----------|
| **State environmental regulations** | NJ can enforce environmental/health standards — water, sewer, hazardous materials. Roxbury says the site has "significant limitations in water and sewer infrastructure" | PA governor exploring this approach |
| **State health & safety standards** | A federal appeals court ruled **Washington State can enforce health and safety standards** at federal detention centers — as long as standards are uniform across all facilities | *Washington v. ICE* |
| **Revoking permits for private contractors** | If ICE hires private companies to renovate/operate, those companies need local permits. Howard County, MD revoked a building permit for an ICE contractor | Howard County, MD |
| **Cutting off utilities** | Municipal utilities could potentially refuse to extend water/sewer to the facility — though this is legally untested against federal property | Novel theory |
| **NEPA environmental review** | Require a full environmental impact study before conversion — could delay by months/years | Standard federal construction law |

#### What's Working Elsewhere

**Public pressure has actually stopped some facilities:**
- Out-of-state warehouse owners in **Oklahoma City and Virginia** ended discussions with ICE after community opposition and boycott campaigns
- **Baltimore County** prohibited privately-owned warehouses from being used as detention centers — this works because the legal distinction is **federal-owned vs. privately leased** property
- **Maryland** is advancing legislation to ban state/local approval of private immigration detention centers

#### The Roxbury Play

Roxbury's best shot is a **multi-front attack:**
1. **Environmental/infrastructure challenge** — the site legitimately lacks water/sewer capacity for 1,500 people
2. **State regulatory authority** — Sherrill using health, safety, environmental regs
3. **Federal legislation** — Booker/Kim bill to ban warehouse conversions (longshot — needs Senate votes)
4. **Delay** — every legal challenge buys time. If Democrats flip the House in November, they can defund the facility through appropriations
5. **Political cost** — making it so painful politically that ICE pivots to another site

#### The Honest Assessment

| Scenario | Probability |
|----------|------------|
| **Roxbury blocks the facility permanently** | ~20% — the Supremacy Clause is very strong |
| **Roxbury delays it past November 2026** | ~40% — environmental/legal challenges can drag on |
| **Facility opens but at reduced capacity** | ~25% — infrastructure limitations may force downsizing |
| **Facility opens as planned** | ~15% — if DHS pushes through all opposition |

The **best realistic outcome** is delay. If Democrats win the House in November, they can strip funding through appropriations. The facility can't operate without money. That's 8 months away.

### For Your Family

The warehouse raids are concentrated in the **Edison/Elizabeth/Newark corridor** — not Jersey City directly. But the Roxbury detention facility is 45 miles away, and ICE has conducted operations in **Jersey City and Hoboken** (confirmed by NJ1015 reporting). The NJ sanctuary state protections and Gov. Sherrill's opposition provide a legal buffer, but ICE operates under federal authority and can override state preferences.

# 🎯 HOMELAND ATTACK RISK — UPDATED MARCH 6, 2026

> Previous section covered general threat landscape. This update adds: Austin shooting details confirmed, DHS website offline, West Point CTC analysis, specific city targeting intel.

## Austin Sixth Street Shooting — Full Picture

The attack we flagged earlier now has much more detail:

| Detail | Confirmed |
|--------|-----------|
| **Date** | March 1, 2026 — one day after Operation Epic Fury launched |
| **Location** | Buford's bar, West Sixth Street, Austin TX |
| **Dead** | **3** — Jorge Pederson (30), Savitha Shan (21), Ryder Harrington (19) |
| **Wounded** | 14 hospitalized, 2 still in hospital, 1 critical (as of March 5) |
| **Total hit** | 19 including suspect |
| **Suspect** | **Ndiaga Diagne**, 53, Senegalese-born, naturalized US citizen (2013) |
| **Method** | Circled block in SUV, turned on hazard lights, fired pistol → parked → switched to rifle, walked east on 6th St |
| **Clothing** | "Property of Allah" hoodie, Iranian flag T-shirt underneath |
| **Home search** | Photos of Iranian leaders found at residence in Pflugerville TX |
| **Social media** | Pro-Iranian posts under investigation |
| **Prior record** | 2022 arrest after car crash, "history or pattern of committing family violence" — did NOT prevent gun ownership |
| **FBI assessment** | Investigating as **potential terrorism**, believes **lone actor** (not organized cell) |
| **Prior radar** | Was NOT on FBI or local LE radar before attack. Only prior contact: 2022 welfare check |
| **Immigration** | Arrived 2000 on tourist visa → green card 2006 → naturalized 2013 |

### Key Takeaway
This looks like a **self-radicalized lone actor** inspired by — but not directed by — Iran. That's actually the hardest threat to defend against, because there's no communication chain to intercept.

Sources: [CBS News](https://www.cbsnews.com/news/mass-shooting-at-austin-texas-bar-leaves-at-least-3-dead-multiple-people-wounded/), [KVUE](https://www.kvue.com/article/news/local/austin-mass-shooting/active-attack-reported-in-downtown-austin/269-1a19c462-1416-4316-8dba-732c395fbfcf), [KUT Radio](https://www.kut.org/crime-justice/2026-03-02/austin-tx-shooting-bufords-bar-6th-street-suspect-ndiaga-diagne-texas)

## DHS Is Offline During a War

This is genuinely insane:

- The **DHS website is not being actively managed** — they literally post a disclaimer saying so
- The **National Terrorism Advisory System (NTAS)** website — the thing that's supposed to warn Americans about threats — is **not being updated**
- **CISA** (Cybersecurity and Infrastructure Security Agency) has **canceled physical and cybersecurity assessments** for critical infrastructure
- CISA can't conduct simulation exercises, stakeholder trainings, or international engagements
- TSA suspended all courtesy/special privilege escorts at airports
- DHS employees started **missing paychecks** in early March

The DHS shutdown is now in **Day 20+**. We are fighting a war against a state sponsor of terrorism with the homeland security department **unfunded and partially closed**.

Sen. Collins (WaPo op-ed): The shutdown "undermines homeland security at a critical moment."

Sen. Cotton: "Democrats are highly irresponsible to keep Homeland Security unfunded while we're in the middle of a war against the world's worst state sponsor of terrorism."

Sources: [DHS.gov](https://www.dhs.gov/news/2026/02/22/1-week-democrats-shutdown-dhs-implements-emergency-measures-conserve-resources-and), [NPR](https://www.npr.org/2026/02/14/nx-s1-5713914/department-of-homeland-security-shutdown), [WaPo](https://www.washingtonpost.com/opinions/2026/03/02/dhs-shutdown-funding-iran-collins-austin/), [Government Executive](https://www.govexec.com/management/2026/03/congress-searches-shutdown-ramp-dhs-employees-start-missing-pay/411814/)

## West Point CTC Report: "Tehran's Homeland Option"

The **Combating Terrorism Center at West Point** published a comprehensive report on Iran's capacity to attack the US homeland. Key findings:

### Known Hezbollah Sleeper Cell Cities
The report documents that Hezbollah established cells in major US cities, then when they realized FBI was watching, **moved operatives to smaller cities to blend in**:

| Tier | Cities | Status |
|------|--------|--------|
| **Tier 1 — Original cells** | New York, Houston, Detroit/Dearborn, Los Angeles, Boston | Known to FBI, under surveillance |
| **Tier 2 — Relocated operatives** | Portland OR, Louisville KY, smaller cities | Deliberately moved to "blend in" |
| **Tier 3 — Unknown** | ? | The ones they haven't found |

### The Activation Trigger
Hezbollah operative **Kourani** (arrested, cooperating with FBI) said he was a sleeper agent and that certain scenarios would trigger cell activation — specifically **"if the United States ever went to war with Iran."**

The CTC report notes: **All those lines have now been crossed.**

### Iran's Pre-War Threat
Before the strikes, Iran reportedly sent a direct message to Trump threatening to **"activate sleeper-cell terror inside the United States"** if attacked. The CTC report says this should not be taken lightly given Iran's decade-long expansion of external operations.

### Expert Assessment
- **Michael Rubin (AEI):** "They pose a very grave threat... The Iranians are going to strike us where we are least defended."
- **Rubin warning:** "An Iranian sleeper cell might not be comprised of Iranians. It might be an Iranian-hired cell tapping into other existing criminal networks."
- **Former NATO commander:** "For Iran, this war is existential. And because it is, I would fully expect Tehran to activate any sleeper cell capacity it has in the West."
- **CTC conclusion:** "If there were ever a time Iran would want to activate its homeland option, this would be it."

### The Long Game
Even if the next few weeks pass without an attack, the threat persists. Iran took **years** preparing plots to avenge Soleimani's death (January 2020). They play the long game.

Sources: [West Point CTC](https://ctc.westpoint.edu/tehrans-homeland-option-terror-pathways-for-iran-to-strike-in-the-united-states/), [JNS](https://www.jns.org/very-grave-threat-of-iranian-sleeper-cells-in-us-experts-warn/), [Fortune](https://fortune.com/2026/02/28/iran-death-ground-existential-threat-us-attacks-retaliation-terrorism-cyberattacks-strait-of-hormuz/)

---

## Governor Abbott's Warning

Texas Gov. Greg Abbott went on Fox Business to warn that Iranian sleeper cells must be taken "seriously." He's ramping up Texas state security, which is notable because:
1. Texas is where the Austin attack happened
2. Houston is a Tier 1 Hezbollah cell city per the CTC report
3. Texas has a massive Iranian-American community in Houston

Source: [The Hill](https://thehill.com/homenews/state-watch/5764133-texas-governor-warns-iranian-sleeper-cells/), [Fox Business](https://www.foxbusiness.com/media/abbott-warns-iranian-sleeper-cells-must-taken-seriously-after-deadly-texas-shooting)

### The Terrifying Irony

The agencies responsible for preventing homeland attacks have been systematically degraded:
- **DHS** — shut down, Day 20+, employees unpaid
- **CISA** — canceled all security assessments and trainings
- **FBI counterterrorism unit** — the team monitoring Iranian threats was **fired by DOGE** before the strikes began
- **NTAS** — the public warning system is **not being updated**
- **FEMA** — non-disaster responses halted

We went to war against the world's leading state sponsor of terrorism **after** gutting the agencies designed to protect the homeland from terrorist retaliation.

### For Your Family

Austin confirmed the threat is real and already manifesting. The good news for Jersey City specifically:
- JC is not a Tier 1 or Tier 2 sleeper cell city in the CTC report
- NJ state police and NYPD/JTTF provide substantial coverage of the NYC metro area
- The most likely threat to JC is **proximity to NYC targets**, not direct targeting
- Your relocation destinations (Ireland, Netherlands, Canada) are categorically safer — they're not at war with Iran

| **Oil** | WTI $90.90 / Brent $92.69 (briefly hit $94) |
| **Strait of Hormuz** | Effectively closed — tanker traffic at standstill |

### Trump Demands "Unconditional Surrender"

This is the biggest escalation of the week. On March 6, Trump posted on Truth Social:

> "No deal with Iran except UNCONDITIONAL SURRENDER!"

He then told Axios that "unconditional surrender" could mean either Iran formally surrendering OR "when they can't fight any longer because they don't have anyone or anything to fight with."

He also said he has to be "involved" in choosing Iran's next leader after Khamenei. His words: "GREAT & ACCEPTABLE Leader(s)" must be selected, and "MAKE IRAN GREAT AGAIN (MIGA!)"

**Iran's response:** President Pezeshkian said the demand is "a dream that they should take to their grave." Iran's foreign minister rejected ceasefire talks entirely. Iran says it's prepared for a ground invasion.

**What this means:** There is now NO diplomatic off-ramp. Trump has made it impossible for Iran to negotiate without total humiliation. This war is going to last weeks minimum, possibly months.

Sources: [Al Jazeera](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/6/no-deal-with-iran-except-unconditional-surrender-trump-says), [Axios](https://www.axios.com/2026/03/06/trump-iran-war-unconditional-surrender), [NPR](https://www.npr.org/2026/03/06/nx-s1-5738448/iran-us-israel-war), [PBS](https://www.pbs.org/newshour/show/trump-demands-unconditional-surrender-as-war-on-iran-enters-new-phase)
