## 🏛️ DHS FUNDING, SAVE ACT, & THIRD TERM AMENDMENT — March 9

### Trump's Legislative Hostage-Taking

On March 8, Trump posted on Truth Social:

> *"I, as President, will not sign other Bills until this is passed, AND NOT THE WATERED DOWN VERSION — GO FOR THE GOLD."*

He's referring to the **SAVE America Act** — and he means it. No other bills. Not DHS funding. Not the budget. Nothing.

### What Is the SAVE America Act?

| Provision | Detail |
|-----------|--------|
| **Proof of citizenship to register** | Must present valid US passport OR birth certificate + photo ID |
| **Nationwide voter ID** | Photo ID required in all states to vote |
| **Mail-in ballot restrictions** | Limits who can vote by mail |
| **Transgender provisions** | Bans transgender participation in women's sports (yes, in an election bill) |
| **Purge mechanism** | Requires states to purge voter rolls of suspected non-citizens |

### Can It Pass?

| Chamber | Status | Votes | Threshold | Passes? |
|---------|--------|-------|-----------|---------|
| **House** | ✅ **PASSED** | 221-209 | Simple majority | ✅ Done |
| **Senate** | ❌ **BLOCKED** | ~50 R votes | 60 needed (filibuster) | ❌ No — need 7 Democrats, have 0 |

**Every single Democrat** except Fetterman has voted against it. Schumer calls it "Jim Crow 2.0."

### The Filibuster Problem

| Option | Status | Will It Work? |
|--------|--------|--------------|
| **Kill the filibuster** | Thune: "Not even close" to enough votes. Collins, Murkowski, McConnell opposed | ❌ Dead |
| **Talking filibuster** | Mike Lee pushing. Would force Dems to physically speak to block. Could take **weeks or months** | ⚠️ Possible but risky — could eat Senate floor time through midterms |
| **Reconciliation** | Can't be used for election law — doesn't qualify as budgetary | ❌ Not applicable |
| **7 Democratic defections** | Would need Fetterman + 6 more. Dems are unified | ❌ Not happening |

**Key GOP holdouts on filibuster reform:**
- **Collins (ME):** Will vote FOR the SAVE Act but will NOT change filibuster rules
- **Murkowski (AK):** "One-size-fits-all mandates from Washington seldom work in places like Alaska"
- **McConnell (KY):** Publicly opposed to talking filibuster — worried it gives Dems ability to gum up Senate for months

### Does the GOP Actually Believe Trump Won't Sign Anything?

| Camp | Position | Who |
|------|----------|-----|
| **"He's bluffing"** | Trump will cave when something he actually wants (war funding, tax cuts) needs his signature | Privately: several senior GOP aides (per Axios) |
| **"He means it"** | Trump has held hostages before (border wall shutdown 2018-19, 35 days). He'll do it again | Mike Lee, Freedom Caucus |
| **"It doesn't matter"** | The 10-day rule means bills become law without his signature IF Congress stays in session. Trump would need to pocket veto (only works during adjournment) | Constitutional scholars |

**The 10-day rule loophole:** Under Article I of the Constitution, if the president does not sign a bill within 10 days (Sundays excepted) while Congress is in session, **it becomes law automatically without his signature.** Trump can only truly kill a bill by:
1. **Vetoing it** (Congress can override with 2/3 majority)
2. **Pocket veto** (not signing while Congress adjourns — bill dies)

So Trump saying "I won't sign anything" is actually weaker than it sounds — Congress could pass bills and let them become law without him. The question is whether Congress has the political will to dare him.

### ⚠️ The Pocket Veto Play — Can the GOP Adjourn to Help Trump Kill Bills?

If Trump doesn't want to formally veto a bill (which is embarrassing and overridable), the GOP could **adjourn Congress** to let him pocket veto it instead. A pocket veto is **absolute** — it can't be overridden. The bill just dies.

**How it would work:**
1. Bill passes both chambers, lands on Trump's desk
2. Trump sits on it (doesn't sign, doesn't veto)
3. GOP leadership calls Congress into adjournment within the 10-day window
4. Bill dies automatically — pocket veto, no override possible

**Why this is a real concern:**
- GOP controls both chambers — they set the schedule
- McConnell/Thune could call adjournments strategically
- Trump gets to kill bills without the political cost of a formal veto
- No override vote = no vulnerable GOP members on record

**BUT — there are defenses:**

| Defense | How It Works | Who Controls It |
|---------|-------------|----------------|
| **Pro forma sessions** | Either chamber can stay technically "in session" by gaveling in for ~30 seconds every 3 days. No actual business, but prevents adjournment. Congress has done this routinely for decades | **Either party can do this** — one senator is enough |
| **Both chambers must agree to adjourn** | Article I, Sec. 5: "Neither House... shall, without the Consent of the other, adjourn for more than three days." The Senate can't adjourn if the House won't, and vice versa | **Democrats could block adjournment** if they control one procedural lever |
| **Agent designation** | Congress can designate an agent to receive veto messages during recess, which courts have ruled prevents pocket vetoes even during breaks | Routine practice since the 1970s |
| **Presidential adjournment power** | Art. II, Sec. 3: President can adjourn Congress if the two chambers can't agree on an adjournment date. **Never been used in US history** | Trump could theoretically try this — but it would be an unprecedented constitutional crisis |

**The scenario to watch:**

| Step | What Happens | Realistic? |
|------|-------------|-----------|
| 1. DHS funding bill passes both chambers | Possible if Dems cave or compromise | ⚠️ |
| 2. Trump refuses to sign | He's said he won't | 🔴 Likely |
| 3. GOP calls adjournment to enable pocket veto | Would require Senate + House GOP agreement | ⚠️ They could try |
| 4. Dems block via pro forma session | One senator gavels in every 3 days | ✅ Standard defense |
| 5. Trump tries to force adjournment via Art. II, Sec. 3 | Never been done. Immediate court challenge | ❌ Nuclear option — courts would likely block |

**Bottom line:** The GOP could TRY to adjourn to enable pocket vetoes, but Democrats have a simple, tested defense: **pro forma sessions.** One senator shows up, bangs a gavel, says "the Senate is in session," and leaves. Takes 30 seconds. Prevents pocket vetoes. Both parties have used this tactic for decades.

The wild card is Trump using the **Article II adjournment power** — forcing Congress to adjourn. He threatened this in 2020 and backed down. In a wartime context with an emboldened second-term Trump, would he try again? Possibly. But it would be an unprecedented constitutional crisis that even SCOTUS would likely block.

**Most likely outcome:** Trump formally vetoes anything he doesn't like, and Congress lacks the 2/3 to override because the GOP won't break ranks. The pocket veto play is available but clunky and defensible. The real leverage is the regular veto + party discipline.

### What This Means for DHS Funding

| Timeline | What's Happening |
|----------|-----------------|
| **Feb 14** | DHS partial shutdown began — Senate Dems blocked funding bill |
| **Feb-March** | House passed H.R. 7744 to fund DHS (221-209) |
| **Senate vote** | 51-45 — every Dem except Fetterman voted no. Needed 60 |
| **Dem demand** | Won't fund DHS without reforms to immigration enforcement (triggered by ICE killings) |
| **GOP demand** | Clean funding bill, no conditions |
| **Trump demand** | Won't sign DHS funding unless SAVE Act passes too |
| **Result** | **Total gridlock.** Dems block in Senate. Trump blocks on his desk. Nobody moves |

**ICE is still funded** — The One Big Beautiful Bill Act from last year gave ICE/CBP a multibillion-dollar cash infusion separate from DHS appropriations. So immigration enforcement continues even during shutdown. The agencies suffering are **TSA, FEMA, Coast Guard, and Secret Service.**

### Why Democrats Won't Budge

After ICE agents killed Renee Nicole Good and Alex Pretti in Minneapolis:
- Democrats reframed DHS funding as **funding the agency that killed US citizens**
- Schumer: "We will not write a blank check for an agency that shoots first and asks questions later"
- The political calculus flipped — voting to fund DHS is now seen as dangerous for Dems in blue districts
- The longer the shutdown drags, the worse it looks for everyone, but Dems believe the war + TSA chaos ultimately hurts Trump more

## 👑 TRUMP THIRD TERM — THE 22ND AMENDMENT QUESTION

### The Proposal

**H.J.Res.29** — introduced January 23, 2025 by Rep. Andy Ogles (R-TN):
- Changes 22nd Amendment from "no person shall be elected more than **twice**" to "more than **three times**"
- BUT: disqualifies anyone who served **two consecutive terms** — so Obama, Bush, and Clinton can't run
- **Tailored specifically for Trump** (two non-consecutive terms)

### Can It Pass?

| Step | Requirement | Realistic? |
|------|-------------|-----------|
| **House** | 2/3 majority (290 of 435) | ❌ Would need ~70 Democrats. Not happening |
| **Senate** | 2/3 majority (67 of 100) | ❌ Would need ~14 Democrats. Not happening |
| **State ratification** | 38 of 50 states | ❌ 24 blue/purple states would block |
| **Total amendments proposed since 1992** | ~1,400 | **Zero** have passed |

**Probability of ratification: essentially 0%.** This is performative loyalty, not serious legislation.

### The "Wartime" Angle — More Concerning

On August 18, 2025, during a meeting with Zelensky, Trump said:

> Zelensky: *"Ukrainian law prohibits elections during active armed conflict."*
> Trump: *"So you're saying during the war you can't have elections? So, let me just say, three-and-a-half years from now…"*

At the time, it was dismissed as a joke. **It's not funny anymore.**

| Then (August 2025) | Now (March 2026) |
|---------------------|-------------------|
| No active US war | **US at war with Iran — Day 10+** |
| Trump said "there are methods" for a third term | Hegseth: "We're just getting started." Trump: "No time limits" on the conflict |
| Constitutional amendment route = dead | **Wartime "emergency powers" angle = being discussed** |
| Midterms not yet a concern | **Midterms November 2026 — 8 months away** |
| Trump still needed to face voters | **Second-term Trump has nothing to lose — can't run again (legally)** |

### The Real Risk Isn't a Third Term — It's 2026 Midterm Interference

The 22nd Amendment has no wartime exception. The amendment is ratified and unambiguous. Trump cannot legally run in 2028.

**But here's what he CAN do:**

| Action | Legal? | Already Happening? |
|--------|--------|-------------------|
| Deploy National Guard to blue cities during midterm voting | ⚠️ Contested — courts blocking some | ✅ Already deployed to several cities |
| Use ICE to intimidate voters near polling places | ❌ Illegal under Voting Rights Act | ⚠️ Blue states preemptively banning ICE from polls |
| Hold DHS/FEMA/TSA hostage through midterms | ⚠️ Legal but destructive | ✅ Happening now |
| Use SAVE Act to purge voter rolls before November | Would need to pass first | ❌ Blocked in Senate |
| Declare "election emergency" using war powers | ❌ No legal basis — Constitution requires elections | ⚠️ Rhetoric is escalating |
| Contest/refuse to certify midterm results | ❌ Illegal but tested Jan 6 | ⚠️ Possible |

### Bottom Line on the Third Term

| Threat | Probability | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------|
| **Constitutional amendment passes** | **~0%** | Dead on arrival. Performative only |
| **Trump cancels/postpones 2028 election** | **< 1%** | Military wouldn't comply. Courts would block. States run elections, not the president |
| **Trump interferes with 2026 midterms** | **15-25%** | This is the REAL threat. NG in cities, DHS shutdown, SAVE Act purges, ICE near polls. All the tools are in place |
| **Trump uses wartime powers to expand executive authority** | **40-50%** | Already happening — Senate can't rein in war powers, DOGE gutting agencies, ruling by executive order. Third term not needed if you've already neutered Congress |

**The scariest insight:** Trump doesn't need a third term if he's already made the presidency so powerful that Congress and courts are irrelevant. The third-term amendment is a distraction. The real power grab is happening through executive orders, wartime authority, and institutional destruction — right now, in his second term.

## 📢 TRUMP ANNOUNCEMENTS — March 9, 2026

### 1. 🔴 "THE WAR IS VERY COMPLETE" + TAKING OVER THE STRAIT OF HORMUZ

In a phone interview with CBS News from his Doral, Florida golf club, Trump made several major claims:

| Claim | Reality |
|-------|---------|
| "The war is very complete, pretty much" | Day 10 of an active war. Hormuz closed. Oil $100+. 8 US soldiers dead. Iran launching missiles at Gulf states daily |
| "They have no navy, no communications, no air force" | Iran has launched 500+ ballistic missiles and ~2,000 drones SINCE the war began. Still hitting targets across the Gulf |
| "Their missiles are down to a scatter" | Qatar intercepted 17 ballistic missiles + 6 drones on March 9 alone |
| "I'm thinking about taking it over" (re: Strait of Hormuz) | Would require occupying both sides of a strait bordered by Iran AND Oman. Military experts: would need 100,000+ troops and permanent naval presence |
| "If they do anything bad, that would be the end of Iran and you'd never hear the name again" | Implicit threat of nuclear weapons or total destruction of a country of 88 million people |

**Market reaction:** Oil dropped ~6% on the Hormuz takeover comment (from $100+ to ~$85-88). Markets briefly believed he might actually force it open. Whether this holds depends on whether it's rhetoric or action.

**What "taking over" Hormuz would actually require:**

| Factor | Detail |
|--------|--------|
| **Geography** | 21 miles wide at narrowest. Iran on north shore, Oman on south. Two 2-mile-wide shipping lanes |
| **Iran's assets** | Anti-ship missiles, sea mines (estimated 5,000+), fast attack boats, shore-based cruise missiles, submarine fleet |
| **Mine clearance alone** | Would take weeks-months. Iran can re-mine faster than US can clear |
| **Troops needed** | Analysts estimate 50,000-100,000+ for sustained control of both shores |
| **Oman's position** | Neutral. Would they allow US troops on their territory? Unclear |
| **Duration** | Not a one-time operation — would need PERMANENT military presence |

This isn't "taking over" — it's an occupation. And it would essentially mean a ground war in Iran through the back door.

Sources: [CBS News](https://www.cbsnews.com/news/trump-iran-cbs-news-the-war-is-very-complete-strait-hormuz/), [CNBC](https://www.cnbc.com/2026/03/08/crude-oil-prices-today-iran-war.html), [CNN](https://www.cnn.com/2026/03/06/business/strait-of-hormuz-open-trump)

### 3. 🔴 DISSOLVING USMCA — CUTTING CANADA OUT

- If USMCA dissolves and US-Canada trade relations deteriorate, Canada becomes a more complicated destination
- Could affect work permit processing, cross-border employment
- BUT: Immigration is separate from trade — Express Entry wouldn't be directly affected
- Canada's immigration system is federal and doesn't depend on US trade agreements

## 🏛️ DHS SHUTDOWN — HOW FAR APART ARE THEY? (March 9)

### The Gap

**Day 24 of shutdown.** Both sides say they're "still far apart." No vote scheduled. Congress expected to recess again without a deal.

### What Each Side Wants

| Issue | Democrat Demand | Republican Position | Gap |
|-------|----------------|-------------------|-----|
| **Body cameras** | MANDATORY for all ICE/CBP agents | Bill includes $20M for cameras but does NOT mandate use. "Funding without wearing means nothing" — Blumenthal | 🟡 Closest to agreement — scattered GOP support for mandating |
| **Masks** | Ban agents from wearing masks during enforcement | "Matter of safety" — agents need masks for protection. Homan: "I don't like masks but they need them" | 🔴 Far apart |
| **Warrants** | Judicial warrants required for home entries | Current policy allows administrative warrants (signed by ICE supervisors, not judges) | 🔴 Far apart |
| **Roving patrols** | End broad dragnet stops of suspected undocumented people | Core of Trump's enforcement strategy — won't give this up | 🔴 Non-starter for GOP |
| **Agent IDs** | Agents must display visible identification | Some GOP openness | 🟡 Possible |
| **Use of force policy** | Codify reformed use-of-force standards into law | Oppose legislating operational rules | 🔴 Far apart |

### The Structural Absurdity

Here's the thing that makes this shutdown almost meaningless as leverage:

| Agency | Shutdown Impact | Why |
|--------|----------------|-----|
| **ICE** | ❌ **Still fully funded** — $75B from One Big Beautiful Bill sits outside annual appropriations | Dems are shutting down DHS to force ICE reform, but ICE doesn't need DHS funding |
| **CBP** | ❌ **Still funded** — same supplemental money | Border operations continue |
| **TSA** | ✅ **Workers unpaid** — 3+ hour lines, spring break chaos | TSA has nothing to do with ICE reform |
| **FEMA** | ✅ **Furloughed** — 23,000 employees sent home | FEMA has nothing to do with ICE reform |
| **Coast Guard** | ✅ **Working without pay** — during active naval conflict with Iran | Coast Guard has nothing to do with ICE reform |
| **Secret Service** | ⚠️ Partially funded through workarounds | Secret Service has nothing to do with ICE reform |
| **CISA (cybersecurity)** | ✅ **Gutted** — during wartime cyber threats from Iran/Russia | CISA has nothing to do with ICE reform |

**The agencies Democrats want to reform (ICE/CBP) are fully funded and unaffected by the shutdown. The agencies being hurt (TSA, FEMA, Coast Guard, CISA) have nothing to do with immigration enforcement.**

Democrats know this. Their leverage isn't the shutdown itself — it's the **political blame** as TSA lines get worse, spring break gets ruined, and Coast Guard members go unpaid during a war.

### Who's Winning the Blame Game?

| Metric | Detail |
|--------|--------|
| **GOP framing** | "Democrat shutdown" — Dems are endangering national security during wartime by holding DHS hostage for "radical immigration demands" |
| **Dem framing** | "ICE is killing Americans" — we won't fund an agency that shoots first. Trump is the one holding bills hostage for the SAVE Act |
| **Public polling** | Split — ~45% blame Dems, ~42% blame Trump/GOP, ~13% blame both (Morning Consult, March 5) |
| **The TSA factor** | Every day the shutdown continues, millions more travelers experience 3-hour lines. This anger is accumulating and mostly hurting whoever's in power (Trump) |
| **Wartime angle** | GOP is using the Iran war to pressure Dems: "You're defunding homeland security during wartime." Dems respond: "Then tell Trump to negotiate" |

### Why There's No Deal Coming Soon

| Blocker | Explanation |
|---------|-------------|
| **Trump** | Won't sign DHS funding unless SAVE Act passes. SAVE Act can't pass Senate. So even if Dems and GOP strike a deal, Trump blocks it |
| **Schumer** | "They haven't budged on key issues. Crickets." Won't bring another vote without real concessions |
| **Thune** | "It's never enough... they don't want a deal." Won't pressure Trump on SAVE Act demands |
| **Noem fired** | Trump replacing DHS Secretary mid-shutdown adds chaos. Some Dems said Noem leaving could help talks, but no movement yet |
| **Recess** | Both chambers expected to recess again. Clock keeps ticking but no urgency to resolve |

### Timeline Projection

| If deal reached... | DHS reopens... | TSA paychecks resume... |
|-------------------|---------------|------------------------|
| **This week** | ~March 12-14 | ~March 21 (next pay cycle) |
| **End of March** | ~April 1 | ~April 7 |
| **After spring break** | Mid-April | Late April |
| **Never (runs into FY27)** | New fiscal year Oct 1 | Would need new appropriations bill entirely |

**Most likely scenario:** This drags through March. The TSA crisis during spring break creates enormous pressure, but Trump's SAVE Act demand is an immovable object. Some kind of face-saving compromise happens in **late March or April** — probably body cameras + agent IDs (easy wins) without the mask ban or warrant requirements (deal-breakers). Democrats declare partial victory. Republicans declare total victory. TSA workers get back pay. Nothing fundamentally changes about ICE enforcement.

**Wildcard:** If the war escalates dramatically and a homeland security incident occurs (another Austin-style attack, cyberattack on infrastructure), the pressure to fund DHS immediately could force both sides to a clean bill with no conditions. Nothing motivates Congress like fear.

## 📰 LAST 48 HOURS — March 8-10, 2026

### 🔴 IRAN WAR — DAY 9-11

#### Black Rain Over Tehran (March 8)

Israeli strikes hit fuel storage and distribution sites across Tehran and Alborz provinces. **80 Israeli fighter jets** in the largest single attack of the war. Result:

| Impact | Detail |
|--------|--------|
| **"Black rain"** | Burning fuel depots created toxic smoke plumes over Tehran (pop. ~10 million). Oil-tainted rainfall fell across the city |
| **Health warnings** | Iranian Red Crescent: rain is "highly dangerous and acidic" — chemical burns, lung damage. Residents reported burning eyes, headaches, difficulty breathing |
| **Environmental** | Fine particulate matter linked to cancer and heart disease now in Tehran's air and water supply |
| **Framing** | Common Dreams: "Intentional Chemical Warfare." Iran FM: "dangerous new phase with deliberate strikes on energy infrastructure" |
| **Deaths from fuel strikes** | 4 confirmed from fuel depot hits specifically |

This is the most significant attack on **civilian infrastructure** so far — not military targets, fuel depots that supply an entire city of 10 million.

Sources: [TIME](https://time.com/7383099/iran-news-oil-strikes-tehran/), [CGTN](https://news.cgtn.com/news/2026-03-09/When-war-falls-as-black-rain-in-Iran-s-Tehran-1LnodMXlKoM/p.html), [HRANA](https://www.en-hrana.org/day-nine-of-the-u-s-israeli-war-on-iran-polluted-air-and-black-rain-in-tehran/), [Common Dreams](https://www.commondreams.org/news/toxic-black-rain-iran)

| **Iranian schools hit** | 65 |

#### Iran Says Missiles NOT Destroyed

IRGC rejected US claims that its missile program is destroyed. Said they're deploying projectiles "in greater numbers" with warheads **over 1 tonne.** This directly contradicts Trump's CBS claim that "their missiles are down to a scatter."

Evidence: Qatar intercepted **17 ballistic missiles + 6 drones** on March 9 alone.

#### Hegseth: Tuesday Will Be "Most Intense Day" of Strikes

Defense Secretary said March 11 (Tuesday) will see the heaviest bombardment since the war began. This suggests a major escalation, not the wind-down Trump is claiming.

#### Trump Advisers Privately Urging Exit Plan

Per WSJ: Some advisers are privately urging Trump to articulate an exit strategy, arguing the military has "largely achieved its objectives":
- ✅ Iran's navy destroyed
- ✅ Nuclear facilities struck
- ⚠️ Missile program degraded but NOT destroyed (Iran says otherwise)
- ❌ Highly enriched uranium NOT secured (would require ground troops)
- ❌ Regime change NOT achieved (Mojtaba Khamenei already installed)
- ❌ Regional proxy support NOT ended
- ❌ Hormuz NOT reopened

**4 of 7 stated objectives are unmet.** The advisers want to declare victory and leave anyway. Sound familiar?

#### DOGE — THE FULL AUTOPSY

**DOGE is effectively dead.** OPM Director Scott Kupor told Reuters in November 2025 that DOGE "doesn't exist" — dissolved 8 months before its July 4, 2026 charter expiration.

**Timeline:**

| Date | Event |
|------|-------|
| **Jan 20, 2025** | DOGE established by executive order. Musk starts as Special Government Employee (130-day limit) |
| **Jan-May 2025** | Musk's reign — mass firings, USAID shuttered, contract cancellations, data access controversies |
| **May 29, 2025** | Musk steps down after 130 days. Press conference with Trump in Oval Office |
| **Summer 2025** | Core leadership team follows Musk out. Staffing collapses |
| **Oct 2025** | 45 staffers remain. One-time civil service buyout drives 60% of total workforce cuts |
| **Nov 2025** | OPM Director: DOGE "doesn't exist." Functions absorbed by OPM |
| **Dec 2025** | Musk: DOGE was "only somewhat successful." He wouldn't do it again |
| **Mar 2026** | Appeals court blocks Musk deposition on USAID. DOJ says DOGE "may have misused" Social Security data |

**What DOGE Actually Accomplished:**

| Goal | Claimed | Reality |
|------|---------|---------|
| **Cut spending** | Saved $180 billion | 🔴 **FALSE.** Federal spending INCREASED $248B in 2025 vs 2024. Cato Institute: "DOGE had no noticeable effect on the trajectory of spending." An observer who didn't know when DOGE started couldn't identify it in the data |
| **Reduce workforce** | Cut wasteful government jobs | 🟡 **PARTLY TRUE.** 271,000 federal workers cut (~9% decline). Largest peacetime workforce reduction on record. But many were rehired after wrongful termination lawsuits |
| **Save taxpayer money** | $160B in savings | 🔴 **NET NEGATIVE.** Nonpartisan analysis: DOGE's actions will COST taxpayers ~$135B this year (paid leave, re-hiring, lost productivity). Senate investigation: $21.7B in DOGE-generated waste |
| **IRS cuts** | Eliminate bloated IRS | 🔴 **CATASTROPHIC.** Yale Budget Lab: IRS workforce cuts could forfeit $323B in tax revenue over next decade from lower compliance and fewer audits |
| **Cut debt** | Reduce national debt | 🔴 **OPPOSITE.** National debt grew $2+ trillion since Jan 20, 2025. Interest payments up $100B |

**Verified savings:** Politico analyzed $32.7B in claimed contract savings → could verify only **$1.4 billion** in actual savings. Out of a $6.7 trillion federal budget. That's 0.02%.

**The irony:** DOGE's biggest lasting impact was gutting federal agencies — including counter-terrorism, cybersecurity (CISA), weather forecasting (NOAA), and disease surveillance (CDC) — right before a war, energy crisis, and ongoing pandemic variants. The institutional knowledge that was fired can't be rehired overnight.

**Recent developments (March 2026):**

| Development | Detail |
|-------------|--------|
| **Appeals court blocks Musk deposition** | 2-1 ruling shields Musk from testifying about shuttering USAID. Court said lower judge "abused discretion" |
| **DOGE data scandal** | DOGE affiliate signed "Voter Data Agreement" as SSA employee with advocacy group. Received private info on ~1,000 people |
| **DOGE Social Security misuse** | Trump admin's own DOJ says DOGE "may have misused" Social Security data |
| **Musk net worth** | ~$850 billion (Forbes, March 7) — his companies suffered during DOGE tenure but recovered |

Sources: [Cato Institute](https://www.cato.org/blog/doge-produced-largest-peacetime-workforce-cut-record-spending-kept-rising-0), [CBS News](https://www.cbsnews.com/news/doge-cuts-cost-135-billion-analysis-elon-musk-department-of-government-efficiency/), [TIME](https://time.com/7336327/doge-disbanded-elon-musk/), [NPR](https://www.npr.org/2025/05/30/nx-s1-5415641/musk-leaves-doge-what-comes-next), [Al Jazeera](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/6/6/has-doge-really-saved-the-us-government-180bn)

#### US Consulate Adana (Turkey) — Evacuated

State Department ordered non-emergency US government employees and families to leave Consulate General Adana, Turkey. Safety risk from the war.

### 🗽 NEW JERSEY — YOUR BACKYARD

#### Federal Judge Threatens ICE with Criminal Contempt

| Detail | Fact |
|--------|------|
| **Judge** | US District Judge Michael Farbiarz |
| **Issue** | ICE violated **17 court injunctions** barring them from transferring immigrants out of NJ |
| **Example** | One migrant sent to Peru despite active no-transfer order |
| **ICE's excuse** | "Logistical delays" in communicating orders to "overwhelmed" agents |
| **DOJ admission** | Violated court orders **52 separate times** since early December — nearly 1 in 10 cases |
| **New remedy** | Prosecutors must sign declarations under penalty of perjury confirming ICE received orders. ICE must countersign |
| **Threat** | Criminal contempt if violations continue |

#### DOJ Sues New Jersey

Trump DOJ filed lawsuit against NJ over Governor Sherrill's executive order barring ICE from private areas of state buildings and from using state property as staging areas. Claims it violates the Supremacy Clause.

#### NJ Immigrant Protection Bill Advancing

NJ panel advancing bills to codify the 2018 Immigrant Trust Directive (restricts local police cooperation with ICE). Latest version allows police to notify ICE of an impending release IF the person has a **final order of removal signed by a federal judge** — a compromise from the earlier version which banned all notification.

#### Trenton ICE Raid Dispute

Rep. Bonnie Watson Coleman accused ICE of covering security cameras at a Trenton auto repair shop and detaining people without warrants. ICE denied leading the operation, covering cameras, or raiding the shop — said arrests were by "federal partners" on a criminal warrant.

#### Iran Internet Blackout — 240+ Hours

| Fact | Detail |
|------|--------|
| **Total offline in 2026** | **240+ hours** — one-third of the year |
| **Connectivity level** | **1% of normal** (NetBlocks) |
| **Population affected** | ~90 million people in complete digital darkness |
| **Who's exempt** | Senior officials + state media only — operating on "white SIM cards" |
| **Economic cost** | $35.7 million/DAY (Iran's own communications minister admitted) |
| **Why it matters** | Hides true death toll, prevents civilians from accessing safety info, food, shelter during active bombing |
| **HRW** | "Internet shutdown violates rights, escalates risks to civilians" |
| **Amnesty** | Blackout hiding "the true extent of human rights violations" |

**If we can't verify casualties from inside Iran, the real death toll could be FAR higher than 1,300.**

Sources: [NetBlocks](https://netblocks.org/), [HRW](https://www.hrw.org/news/2026/03/06/iran-internet-shutdown-violates-rights-escalates-risks-to-civilians), [The National](https://www.thenationalnews.com/future/technology/2026/03/10/is-iran-internet-still-down/)

#### SAVE Act Escalation — Now Includes Mail-In Ballot Ban

**New wrinkle:** At the GOP retreat in Doral, Trump added a new demand beyond the SAVE Act: he also wants to **end mail-in voting entirely.**

| Original SAVE Act | Trump's New Demand |
|-------------------|-------------------|
| Proof of citizenship to register | Same |
| Photo ID to vote | Same |
| Purge voter rolls | Same |
| — | **END MAIL-IN VOTING** 🆕 |

This is a massive escalation. Mail-in voting is used by **46 million Americans** including:
- Military deployed overseas
- Elderly and disabled
- Rural voters
- States like Oregon, Washington, Colorado, Utah, Hawaii that are **100% vote-by-mail**

Ending mail-in voting would disenfranchise tens of millions — including military families. In red states.

## 🏛️ THUNE vs. TRUMP vs. MAGA — THE SAVE ACT SHOWDOWN (March 10-11)

### What's Happening

Thune IS scheduling a floor vote on the SAVE Act next week. But it's a **show vote** — and MAGA is furious about it.

### The Three-Way Fight

| Player | Position | What They Want |
|--------|----------|---------------|
| **Trump** | "I won't sign ANY bills until SAVE Act passes. Use the talking filibuster!" | SAVE Act passed by any means necessary. Also now wants mail-in voting banned |
| **Thune** | "I'll bring it to a vote. But the votes aren't there for a talking filibuster. Period." | A messaging vote to put Dems on record, then move on to other business |
| **MAGA/Freedom Caucus** | "Thune is scheduling a SHOW VOTE. This is a betrayal!" | Talking filibuster to force Dems to physically hold the floor for weeks |
| **Democrats** | "We will not help pass the SAVE Act under any circumstances. Total gridlock, so be it." — Schumer | Kill it. Call it Jim Crow 2.0 |

### What Is a "Show Vote" vs. a "Talking Filibuster"?

| Approach | How It Works | Outcome | Time |
|----------|-------------|---------|------|
| **Show vote** (what Thune is doing) | Bring SAVE Act to floor. Standard cloture vote. Needs 60. Gets ~51. Fails. Done | ❌ Bill dies. Dems on record voting no. GOP moves on | ~1-2 days |
| **Talking filibuster** (what Trump/MAGA want) | Force Dems to physically speak on the floor to block it. If they stop talking, vote happens at 51. Could take weeks | ⚠️ Maybe passes IF Dems physically exhaust. But Dems could hold for months. Paralyzes all Senate business | Weeks to months |

### Why Thune Won't Do the Talking Filibuster

Thune was blunt: **"The votes aren't there."**

| Reason | Detail |
|--------|--------|
| **Not enough GOP support** | Collins, Murkowski, McConnell all oppose changing filibuster rules. Even for a "talking" version |
| **Senate business paralyzed** | A talking filibuster locks up the floor. No confirmations, no DHS funding, no war resolutions, nothing — for potentially months |
| **60+ nominees waiting** | Executive nominations backed up. 40 judicial vacancies. None move during a filibuster standoff |
| **DHS shutdown** | Can't negotiate DHS funding while floor is locked in a SAVE Act filibuster marathon |
| **It might not even work** | Dems have 47 senators. They could rotate speakers and hold the floor indefinitely. There's no guarantee the GOP would outlast them |
| **Backfire risk** | If Dems successfully hold a talking filibuster for weeks, it becomes a massive PR win for them — "We stood for 30 days to protect your right to vote" |

### MAGA's Fury

Conservative media and MAGA activists are calling Thune's show vote a "betrayal" and "capitulation":

- Daily Signal: confirmed it's a "show vote"
- Mike Lee: still pushing for talking filibuster, says "we're a few votes shy"
- Trump allies want Thune primaried
- Freedom Caucus: "If Thune won't fight, replace him"

### What Actually Happens Next Week

| Step | What Happens | Result |
|------|-------------|--------|
| 1 | Thune brings SAVE Act to floor | Debate begins |
| 2 | Cloture vote (60 needed) | ~51 R votes. All Dems except maybe Fetterman vote no |
| 3 | Vote fails | Bill dies (for now) |
| 4 | GOP says: "Democrats voted against election integrity" | Messaging for midterms |
| 5 | Dems say: "We stopped Jim Crow 2.0" | Messaging for midterms |
| 6 | Trump: "I still won't sign anything" | Gridlock continues |

### The Real Consequence: TOTAL LEGISLATIVE GRIDLOCK

Here's what CAN'T move while Trump holds everything hostage:

| Bill/Action | Status | Blocked By |
|-------------|--------|-----------|
| **DHS funding** | Day 26 of shutdown. TSA workers unpaid | Dems block in Senate + Trump won't sign without SAVE Act |
| **War authorization** | No AUMF for Iran war. Running on executive authority alone | Trump doesn't want one. Congress can't pass war powers resolution |
| **Farm bill** | Expired. Farmers hurting | Trump won't sign |
| **Housing bill** | Bipartisan support | Trump won't sign |
| **Crypto regulation** | Industry wants clarity | Trump won't sign |
| **60+ executive nominees** | Awaiting confirmation | Can't schedule floor time if filibuster standoff |
| **40 judicial vacancies** | Federal courts shorthanded | Same |
| **Debt ceiling** | Approaching limit again | Trump won't sign anything |

**Trump is holding the entire legislative branch hostage for a bill that can't pass the Senate.** Thune knows it. MAGA knows it. Democrats know it. Nobody has an off-ramp.

### Bottom Line

**Thune is NOT forcing a real vote.** He's scheduling a show vote to get it on the record and move on. MAGA is furious. Trump is still demanding the impossible. The SAVE Act will fail next week in the Senate, and then the question becomes: does Trump actually veto everything that hits his desk for the rest of the year?

If he does, the government essentially runs on autopilot — executive orders, existing appropriations, and emergency powers. Which is arguably what Trump wants anyway.

## 🏛️ DHS SHUTDOWN — THE MULLIN CARD (March 10-11)

### Current State: Day 26, Getting Worse

| Impact | Detail |
|--------|--------|
| **TSA** | Partial paychecks only. Hours-long lines at Houston, New Orleans, Atlanta. First FULL missed check: **March 14** (3 days from now) |
| **100,000+ workers** | Unpaid or furloughed |
| **Spring break** | **Now.** Millions traveling. TSA chaos at peak |
| **Negotiations** | "Still far apart" — Schumer. "Stalled" — multiple sources |
| **Next Senate vote** | None scheduled |

### Mullin Confirmation — The Potential Off-Ramp

Trump fired Noem on March 5 and nominated Sen. Markwayne Mullin (R-OK) to replace her. This is creating an unexpected opening:

| Factor | Detail |
|--------|--------|
| **Confirmation hearing** | **March 18** — Rand Paul targeting "a week from Wednesday" |
| **Committee** | Senate Homeland Security (Paul chairs, Peters is ranking Dem) |
| **Mullin's approach** | Offered to sit down with Democratic leadership to hear their concerns. More diplomatic than Noem |
| **Fetterman** | Already vowed to back Mullin |
| **Murkowski** | Suggested things "can be resolved under new management" — hinting Mullin is an improvement |

### Why Democrats Are Cautiously Interested

| Noem | Mullin |
|------|--------|
| Zero engagement with Democrats | Offered to sit down with Dem leadership |
| Stephen Miller's proxy | Some GOP suggest he'd be a "counterweight" to Miller |
| Oversaw ICE killings, escalated enforcement rhetoric | Former senator — understands the chamber, knows how deals work |
| Democrats hated her personally | Democrats don't hate him (yet) |

**BUT:** Mullin is still a Trump ally with hardline immigration views. Blumenthal: "He's given no indication he plans the kind of reforms Americans are demanding."

### The Play

Democrats could use the confirmation hearing to extract concessions:

| Dem Demand | Could Mullin Agree? | Likelihood |
|-----------|-------------------|-----------|
| **Body cameras** | ✅ Possible — low cost, high optics | 🟢 Most likely concession |
| **Agent IDs** | ✅ Possible — easy win | 🟢 Likely |
| **Mask ban** | ⚠️ Unlikely — GOP framing it as safety issue | 🟡 Maybe a compromise (masks allowed but must show badge) |
| **Judicial warrants** | ❌ GOP has firmly ruled out | 🔴 Dead |
| **End roving patrols** | ❌ Core Trump policy | 🔴 Dead |

### The Three-Track Timeline

Everything is happening simultaneously:

| Track | Date | What |
|-------|------|------|
| **SAVE Act show vote** | ~March 17-18 | Fails at 60. Goes on record. Thune moves on |
| **Mullin confirmation hearing** | March 18 | Dems use this to negotiate ICE reforms |
| **TSA first full missed paycheck** | March 14 | Pressure intensifies dramatically |
| **Spring break peak** | March 14-28 | TSA chaos hits millions of families |
| **No Kings III** | March 28 | 9M+ expected. Gas prices + war + TSA lines fueling turnout |

### The Off-Ramp Scenario

Here's how this COULD resolve:

1. **March 14:** TSA workers miss full paycheck. Airport chaos goes viral. Pressure spikes
2. **March 17-18:** SAVE Act show vote fails. Thune declares it dead for now
3. **March 18:** Mullin hearing. He offers body cameras + agent IDs as personal commitments
4. **March 19-25:** Dems and GOP negotiate a DHS deal: body cameras + IDs codified into law, mask ban dropped, warrants dropped. Mullin confirmed as part of the package
5. **Late March:** DHS funding bill passes Senate with 60+ votes (Dems get body cams/IDs, GOP gets DHS funded)
6. **Trump signs it** because Mullin (his guy) is attached and the SAVE Act fight is separate

**Probability of this scenario:** ~25-30%. It requires Trump to separate DHS funding from the SAVE Act demand, which he may not do.

### The Gridlock Scenario

1. SAVE Act fails. Trump doubles down: "I still won't sign anything"
2. Mullin hearing gets contentious. Dems demand reforms Mullin won't commit to
3. DHS stays shut through spring break
4. TSA workers start calling out sick en masse (can't afford gas to drive to work at $4+/gallon while unpaid)
5. Airport system starts breaking down
6. No Kings III becomes even more massive
7. Midterms approach with DHS still closed

**Probability:** ~40-50%. The likeliest outcome is continued gridlock through March.

### DeLauro's Bill — The Narrow Fix

Rep. Rosa DeLauro (D) has proposed a bill to fund JUST the non-controversial agencies — TSA, FEMA, Coast Guard, CISA — while leaving ICE/CBP funding as the separate fight.

| Advantage | Problem |
|-----------|---------|
| Ends TSA crisis immediately | GOP won't pass it — it removes their leverage |
| Funds Coast Guard during wartime | Democrats lose their leverage too |
| Bipartisan appeal | Neither side wants to give up the hostage |

**This is the cleanest solution and the least likely to happen.** Both sides need the shutdown pain to motivate the other side to deal.

### Bottom Line

**Mullin's confirmation hearing on March 18 is now the key date.** It's the best opportunity for a package deal: confirm Mullin + pass DHS funding with body cameras/IDs attached. If that window closes without a deal, this drags into April and possibly beyond.

Meanwhile, TSA workers miss their full paycheck in 3 days. Spring break is happening right now. And gas prices are heading toward $4.

## ICE/DHS SHOOTINGS — FULL ACCOUNTING (as of March 11, 2026)

The picture is much worse than just Good and Pretti. Here's the full scope.

### Fatal Shootings by DHS Agents (Since Trump 2.0)

| # | Name | Date | Location | Agency | US Citizen? | Key Detail |
|---|------|------|----------|--------|-------------|------------|
| 1 | **Ruben Ray Martinez** | Mar 15, 2025 | South Padre Island, TX | ICE (HSI) | ✅ Yes | Shot 3x directing traffic at car crash. 23 years old, celebrating birthday. **Video released March 2026 contradicts ICE claim he "ran over" agent** — car barely moving, he was braking. Grand jury declined to indict. ICE hid involvement for 11 months. |
| 2 | **Silverio Villegas González** | Sep 2025 | Chicago suburb, IL | ICE | No (Mexican citizen) | Father, worked as a cook. Killed trying to flee. |
| 3 | **Isaias Sanchez Barboza** | Dec 2025 | Rio Grande City, TX | Border Patrol | No (Mexican citizen) | Killed during attempted detention. |
| 4 | **Keith Porter** | Dec 31, 2025 | Northridge, LA | ICE (off-duty) | ✅ Yes | 43-year-old Black father of two. Off-duty ICE agent Brian Palacios shot him at their apartment complex. DHS called it "active shooter response." Palacios accused of racist remarks about Black people and Latinos in court records. |
| 5 | **Renee Nicole Good** | Jan 7, 2026 | Minneapolis, MN | ICE | ✅ Yes | 37-year-old mother of three. Agent Jonathan Ross filmed himself, caught calling her "fucking bitch" after shooting her. Video shows Ross standing OUTSIDE the vehicle's path when he fired. DHS called it "domestic terrorism" within 2 hours. |
| 6 | **Alex Pretti** | Jan 24, 2026 | Minneapolis, MN | Border Patrol (CBP) | ✅ Yes | 37-year-old ICU nurse at VA hospital. Legally carrying firearm — never unholstered it. Video shows he was disarmed BEFORE being shot. Agents tackled him, took his gun, then killed him. |

**Total fatal shootings: At least 9 dead across all DHS agencies since Trump 2.0 began.**

At least **5 of those shot were US citizens.**

### Non-Fatal Shootings

At least **33 total shootings** by immigration agents since Jan 20, 2025, with **14 people shot** since June 2025.

Notable non-fatal:
- **Marimar Martinez** (Oct 2025, Chicago) — Shot 5 times in the arm by Border Patrol Agent Charles Exum. Body cam captured an agent telling her to "do something, bitch" before Exum opened fire.
- **Julio Sosa-Celis** (Minneapolis) — Shot during ICE operation. Federal charges against two Venezuelan men initially blamed were dropped.
- **13 instances** of agents firing at or into civilian vehicles (WSJ count as of Jan 2026).

### Deaths in ICE Custody (January 2026 alone: 6 dead)

| Name | Date | Facility | Cause | Notes |
|------|------|----------|-------|-------|
| Geraldo Lunas Campos | Jan 3 | Camp East Montana, El Paso, TX | **Homicide** (medical examiner ruling) | Asphyxia from neck/torso compression. Witnesses saw guards choking him. Family filed wrongful death suit. |
| Luis Gustavo Núñez Cáceres | Jan 5 | Hospital in TX | Congenital heart failure | Arrested Nov 17, hospitalized Dec 23. Multiple medical emergencies ignored. |
| Luis Beltrán Yáñez-Cruz | Jan 6 | Calexico, CA | Stomach/chest pain | 68 years old. Lived in US 26 years. Arrested in Newark, NJ, shipped to California. |
| Parady La | Jan 9 | FDC Philadelphia, PA | Fentanyl withdrawal | Cambodian, came to US at age 2. Told officers he was withdrawing. Received no treatment. |
| Heber Sánchez Domínguez | Jan 14 | Lovejoy, GA | Unknown | 34-year-old husband and father. |
| Victor Manuel Díaz | Jan 14 | Camp East Montana, El Paso, TX | Suspected hanging (disputed) | Body sent to Army medical center instead of county ME — family attorney calls it "extremely suspicious." Second death at same facility in 11 days. |

**2025 total: 32 deaths in ICE custody** — highest in 20+ years, tied for all-time record.

### The Pattern: Shoot First, Lie After

Every single fatal shooting follows the same playbook:

1. **Agent kills someone** (usually shooting into or near a vehicle)
2. **DHS issues statement within hours** claiming self-defense/"ran over agent"/"active shooter"
3. **Video later emerges** contradicting DHS narrative
4. **Grand jury declines to indict** (every time so far)
5. **No agents criminally charged** (as of March 11, 2026: zero)

This pattern held for Martinez (video showed car barely moving), Good (video showed Ross outside vehicle path), Pretti (video showed he was disarmed before being shot), and Porter (witnesses contradict "active shooter" claim).

### Agent Conduct Issues

- **Jonathan Ross** (killed Renee Good): Caught on his own video calling her a slur after shooting her. 10-year ICE veteran, former Army National Guard.
- **Brian Palacios** (killed Keith Porter): Accused of racist remarks about Black people and Latinos in court records.
- **Unidentified agent** (Marimar Martinez shooting): Told victim to "do something, bitch" before partner shot her 5 times.
- **ICE's internal culture**: American Oversight obtained ICE use-of-force records through FOIA lawsuit, revealing systemic training and oversight failures.

### New Development: Martinez Video (March 7-10, 2026)

This is the big story from the last week. Texas DPS released 160+ pieces of evidence from the Ruben Martinez case:

- **ICE hid its involvement for 11 months** — didn't confirm an ICE agent killed Martinez until February 2026
- **Video shows Martinez's car barely moving**, brake lights on, receiving conflicting instructions from multiple agencies
- **No evidence he "ran over" anyone** — directly contradicts ICE spokesperson's claim
- **After being shot 3 times, Martinez was pulled from his car, thrown face-down, and handcuffed.** No medical care provided until after handcuffing.
- **Cameron County grand jury** ruled justifiable homicide despite the video evidence
- ICE response: "We stand by the grand jury's unanimous decision"

This case is critical because it was the **first** known DHS killing of a US citizen under Trump 2.0 — and they hid it for almost a year.

### Why This Matters for You

The combination of:
- Zero criminal accountability for any agent
- Systematic lying by DHS after every shooting
- Pattern of shooting into vehicles (your family drives)
- Agents with documented racist/sexist attitudes
- ICE operating without body cameras (key DHS shutdown demand)

...is exactly the kind of escalating state violence that reinforces the case for having Canada as a longer-term option.

### 🔴 IRAN WAR — Day 12-13

**The big new development: Iran has a new Supreme Leader, and he's worse.**

Mojtaba Khamenei (son of the assassinated Ali Khamenei) issued his first public message on March 12. He was NOT seen or heard — the statement was read by someone else, fueling rumors he was seriously injured or killed in the initial strikes. Key points from his message:

- **Strait of Hormuz stays closed** — called it a "tool to pressure the enemy"
- **All US bases in the region must close or will be attacked**
- **Vowed revenge** for the assassination of his father
- **Threatened to open "new fronts"** where the US has "limited experience"
- **Demanded compensation** — warned Iran could seize assets or destroy property
- **Invoked Yemen and Iraq** — said armed groups "will also do the job"

Mojtaba, 56, is considered **more hardline than his father**. Trump told Fox News he's "disappointed" and doesn't believe Mojtaba "can live in peace."

**This effectively kills any near-term peace talks.** Iran's new leader just publicly committed to escalation, not de-escalation.

**Military situation:**
- US has now struck **5,000+ targets** in Iran
- Trump says there's "practically nothing left to bomb" — war could end "soon"
- Israel's defense minister says the opposite: **"no time limit"**
- Pentagon disclosed **$11.3B cost in first 6 days alone** (~$890M-$1B/day continuing)
- **8 US troops killed, ~140 wounded** (still the official count)
- School strike investigation: US military confirms the Feb 28 strike on an elementary school that killed **168+ children and 14 teachers** was likely due to **outdated intelligence** about a nearby naval base. 75+ Democratic members of Congress demanding answers about AI targeting.
- **16 mine-laying vessels destroyed** near Hormuz
- **3 commercial ships hit** near Hormuz (Japanese, Thai, Marshall Islands flagged)
- Iranian boats packed with explosives hit 2 Iraqi tankers — **Iraqi oil ports completely shut down**
- **IEA releasing record 400M barrels** of crude reserves to stabilize markets

- IDF Chief apologized to public for not warning about the Hezbollah barrage
- **Only 2 Israeli soldiers killed** vs 634+ Lebanese — massively disproportionate
- France sending 60 tonnes of humanitarian aid

Sen. John Cornyn (R-TX), locked in a competitive primary runoff and chasing Trump's endorsement, now says he'll support "whatever changes to Senate rules that may prove necessary" to pass the SAVE Act. This is a reversal from years of defending the filibuster.

**But it doesn't matter** — Thune says the votes to nuke the filibuster still aren't there. "The opposition to nuking the filibuster runs very, very deep in our conference."

Other SAVE Act opposition:
- **Murkowski** (R-AK): Opposes, calls it "federal overreach"
- **Collins** (R-ME): Expressed misgivings
- **McConnell** (R-KY): Misgivings
- **All 47 Democrats**: Schumer calls it "Jim Crow 2.0"

Thune scheduling the cloture vote next week, conceding it will fail: "It's about the math."

- The housing bill (89-10 Senate vote) goes to Trump's desk... and sits there
- DHS funding can't move
- Farm bill frozen
- Debt ceiling approaching
- **Total legislative paralysis continues**

### 🟢 SENATE HOUSING BILL — Passed 89-10

Genuine bipartisan breakthrough — **21st Century ROAD to Housing Act** (Warren + Tim Scott):

- Bans large institutional investors from buying single-family homes
- Creates grants and pilot programs for housing construction
- Addresses rural housing, homelessness, veteran housing

- Already passed House 390-9 last month
- **BUT:** Trump has said he won't sign anything until SAVE Act passes
- House Speaker Johnson says it needs conference anyway
- **This bill is a hostage of the SAVE Act standoff**

- Israeli Air Force killed Abdollah Jalali-Nasab and Amir Shariat (senior Iranian intelligence replacements — they're now killing the replacements of the people they already killed)
- Hezbollah launched 97 attack waves in 48 hours — **March 14 was the most intense day of the war**: 56 attack waves in a single day
- [Source: Alma Research Center](https://israel-alma.org/daily-report-the-second-iran-war-march-15-2026-1800/)

**March 14: Baghdad Green Zone attacked**
- Kata'ib Hezbollah security commander Abu Ali al-Askari killed in airstrike on Baghdad
- **A drone hit the Royal Tulip Al Rasheed Hotel in Baghdad's Green Zone** — the first two floors were destroyed while hosting an **EU and Saudi Arabian diplomatic delegation**. Attack unclaimed but suspected Iranian.
- This is an attack on diplomats in a neutral country. Major escalation.
- [Source: Times of Israel liveblog](https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog-march-12-2026/)

**March 15: Isfahan strikes**
- US and Israel struck Isfahan in early hours — at least 15 killed
- Tehran's governor: **10,000+ residential homes damaged or destroyed**
- Hegseth claimed 15,000+ "enemy targets" struck total
- Oil loading resumed at UAE's Fujairah port (briefly)
- Trump weighing options to strike Iran's **critical oil infrastructure** directly
- [Source: Al Jazeera Day 16](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/15/iran-war-what-is-happening-on-day-16-of-us-israel-attacks)

**March 16: NATO refuses to help**
- Trump asked NATO allies to provide military support to reopen the Strait of Hormuz
- **Every single NATO ally in Europe said no**
- Trump called it a "very foolish mistake"
- Then rebuked Japan, South Korea, and Australia for also refusing
- Hezbollah: 37 more attack waves (78% rockets/missiles, 13.5% UAVs, 8% anti-tank)
- [Source: Al Jazeera Day 17](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/16/iran-war-what-is-happening-on-day-17-of-us-israel-attacks)

**March 17: GROUND INVASION OF LEBANON + Targeted Killings**
- **Israel launched a ground invasion of southern Lebanon** — "limited and targeted ground operations" against Hezbollah positions. IDF says operations will continue at least **3 more weeks**
- Goal: seize everything south of the Litani River (~40km / 25 miles deep)
- **Largest Israeli ground invasion of Lebanon since 2006**
- Ali Larijani (former parliament speaker) and Basij chief Gholamreza Soleimani killed in Israeli airstrikes — confirmed by Iranian state media
- Iran retaliated: missile barrage killed **2 Israeli civilians in Ramat Gan**
- IDF ordered sweeping evacuations south of Zahrani River
- UN: Israeli attacks on Lebanon "may amount to war crimes"
- France, Canada, Germany, Italy, UK issued joint statement: "gravely concerned"
- [Sources: Washington Post](https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2026/03/12/israel-hezbollah-lebanon-war/), [Axios](https://www.axios.com/2026/03/14/israel-lebanon-ground-invasion-hezbollah), [Al Jazeera](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/17/mapping-israeli-attacks-and-the-displacement-of-one-million-in-lebanon)

**March 18 (TODAY): South Pars — The Big One**
- **Israel struck the South Pars natural gas field** — the **world's largest natural gas reserve**, jointly operated by Iran and Qatar
- 4 gas treatment facilities damaged in US-coordinated drone strikes
- Facilities taken offline. Fire reported, later said to be "under control"
- Iran killed Israeli intelligence minister Esmaeil Khatib in overnight strike — confirmed by President Pezeshkian
- **Iran threatened to retaliate against Gulf energy facilities by name**: Samref refinery (Saudi), Sadara petrochemical complex (Saudi), Qatar Chemical (Doha), Ras Laffan refinery (Qatar), Al-Hosn gas field (UAE)
- Qatar slammed the attack as "dangerous, irresponsible"
- **Energy producers across the Gulf are evacuating sites**
- US dropped **5,000-pound bunker-buster bombs** on Iranian missile sites near Hormuz
- Oil surged to **$109.95/barrel** before settling around $108
- [Sources: Bloomberg](https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2026-03-18/iran-says-strikes-hit-key-south-pars-gas-field-oil-facilities), [Al Jazeera](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/18/iran-threatens-to-strike-gulf-energy-facilities-after-south-pars-attack), [CNBC](https://www.cnbc.com/2026/03/12/strait-of-hormuz-closure-iran-oil-prices-mojtaba-khamenei.html)

#### 💥 JOE KENT RESIGNATION — March 17

**The biggest domestic story of the week.**

Joe Kent — Trump's own Director of the National Counterterrorism Center — resigned, saying he could not "in good conscience" support the war.

Key quotes from his resignation letter:
- **"Iran posed no imminent threat to our nation"**
- **"It is clear that we started this war due to pressure from Israel and its powerful American lobby"**
- Referenced his first wife Shannon, killed in Syria in 2019: "She had been killed in a war manufactured by Israel. I cannot support sending the next generation off to fight and die in a war that serves no benefit to the American people"

Background:
- Kent served **11 combat tours** over a 20-year Army career, then became a CIA officer
- He was a **MAGA loyalist** — this isn't a Never Trumper; this is one of Trump's own people
- He met with VP Vance and DNI Gabbard before resigning; Vance encouraged him to talk to Susie Wiles first
- Trump dismissed him: "I always thought he was weak on security... didn't know him well"
- Administration bracing for an expected **Tucker Carlson interview** with Kent

**Why this matters:** This is the first crack in the MAGA wall on the war. Kent has enormous credibility with the base — combat veteran, Gold Star spouse, MAGA true believer. If Tucker gives him a platform, this could shift Republican opinion on the war overnight.

[Sources: CBS News](https://www.cbsnews.com/news/top-trump-counterterrorism-official-resigns-over-iran/), [NPR](https://www.npr.org/2026/03/17/nx-s1-5750426/joe-kent-counterterrorism-official-resigns-trump), [Al Jazeera](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/17/us-national-counterterrorism-center-director-joe-kent-resigns-over-iran-war), [Washington Post](https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2026/03/17/joe-kent-resigns-iran-war/)

### 🔴 DHS SHUTDOWN — Day 32 (Second-Longest in US History)

**TSA is in freefall:**

| Metric | March 11 | March 18 | Change |
|--------|----------|----------|--------|
| National callout rate | ~6% | **Spiking** | Getting worse |
| Houston Hobby peak callout | 53% | **55%** (March 14) | Still climbing |
| TSA officers who've quit | 300+ | **366+** | Still losing people |
| Airports threatening closure | 0 | **Multiple small airports** | NEW |
| Missed paychecks | Partial (Feb 28) | **First FULL paycheck: March 14** | Devastating |
| Airport wait times | Up to 3.5 hrs | **Still 3+ hours at major hubs** | Not improving |

**Acting Deputy TSA Administrator Adam Stahl**: "It's not hyperbole to suggest that we may have to quite literally **shut down airports**, particularly smaller ones, if call-out rates go up."

Airline CEOs sent open letter to Congress: "TSA officers just received **$0 paychecks**. That is simply unacceptable."

World Central Kitchen (José Andrés) providing free meals to TSA workers — over 8,000 meals served.

**The White House offer (March 17):**

The White House revealed 5 concessions it's willing to make:

| # | Concession | Details |
|---|------------|---------|
| 1 | Body cameras | $100M (up from $20M), IG audits, noncompliance reviews |
| 2 | Sensitive locations | No enforcement at hospitals/schools (with nat'l security exceptions) |
| 3 | Officer IDs | Visible identification required, must verbalize agency on request |
| 4 | Detention oversight | Congressional oversight of facilities |
| 5 | US citizen protections | Won't knowingly deport or detain US citizens (except criminal violations) |

**Democrats sent a counteroffer the same night.** Thune said it "didn't move the debate." Both sides calling each other's offers non-starters.

**Mullin confirmation hearing — TODAY (March 18):**

It was a circus:
- **Rand Paul opened by attacking Mullin** — reminded everyone Mullin called him a "freaking snake" and said he "understood why" Paul's neighbor assaulted him. Paul says he will **NOT vote for Mullin**.
- Mullin did not apologize. Doubled down: "I said I could understand, because of the behavior you were having, that I can understand why your neighbor did what he did."
- **Key policy statement: Mullin said he would require JUDICIAL WARRANTS for ICE to enter homes/businesses** — a significant shift from Noem
- Fetterman (D-PA) praised Mullin: "my experience with you has been consistent kindness and professionalism" — likely Dem vote for confirmation
- Paul demanding classified briefing on Mullin's overseas travel — could delay committee vote
- **Committee vote expected Thursday. Mullin on track to be confirmed** with simple majority

[Sources: Washington Post](https://www.washingtonpost.com/immigration/2026/03/18/markwayne-mullin-dhs-confirmation-hearing-live-updates/), [NPR](https://www.npr.org/2026/03/18/nx-s1-5749360/markwayne-mullin-dhs-confirmation-hearing), [CNBC](https://www.cnbc.com/2026/03/18/markwayne-mullin-dhs-confirmation-senate-immigration.html), [Time](https://time.com/article/2026/03/17/airport-close-delays-dhs-shutdown-tsa/)

### 🟡 SAVE ACT — Debate Begins, Dead on Arrival

**March 17: Senate voted 51-48 to BEGIN DEBATE** on the SAVE America Act.
- Murkowski (R-AK) joined all Democrats in voting NO
- Tillis (R-NC) didn't vote
- This is NOT passage — this just opens debate. The bill still needs 60 votes for cloture.

**The math hasn't changed:** 53 Republicans (minus Murkowski = 52) vs. 60 needed. They're 8 votes short with zero Democratic support.

**Thune concedes it will fail:** "It's about the math." He's promised a "full and robust debate" that could last **a week or more**.

**Mike Lee (R-UT) threatening primary challengers** against Republicans who won't support nuking the filibuster. Thune warned this "could jeopardize the Republican majority."

**Cornyn flip:** Now says he'll support "whatever changes to Senate rules may prove necessary" — but Thune says the votes to nuke the filibuster still aren't there.

**Trump's position unchanged:** Won't sign anything until SAVE passes. This means:
- Housing bill (89-10) → hostage
- DHS funding → hostage
- Farm bill → frozen
- Debt ceiling → approaching
- All other legislation → dead

[Sources: Axios](https://www.axios.com/2026/03/17/save-act-senate-vote-republicans-procedual-filibuster), [CNBC](https://www.cnbc.com/2026/03/17/save-act-trump-2026-election-senate-voter-id-bill.html), [Washington Post](https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/2026/03/17/trump-voting-bill-senate-talking-filibuster/)

### 🟢 HOUSING BILL — Passed, Held Hostage

**21st Century ROAD to Housing Act passed Senate 89-10** (Warren + Tim Scott). Already passed House 390-9.

Key provisions:
- Bans large institutional investors from buying single-family homes
- Grants and pilots for housing construction
- Rural housing, homelessness, veteran housing
- Also includes CBDC ban

**Problem:** Trump won't sign it until SAVE Act passes. A bill with 89% Senate support and 98% House support is being held hostage by a bill that can't get 60 votes.

**Housing EOs (March 13):** Two orders aimed at affordability:
1. "Promoting Access to Mortgage Credit" — loosens CFPB mortgage rules, helps smaller banks lend
2. "Removing Regulatory Barriers to Affordable Home Construction" — reduces EPA/Army Corps permitting

**Anti-Fraud Task Force (March 16):** Vance-led task force targeting federal benefits fraud, focused on Democratic-led states. Specifically mentions Minnesota Somali community fraud cases to justify ICE operations.

**Made in America EO (March 13):** Requires truthful advertising for "Made in America" claims.

[Sources: Bloomberg](https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2026-03-16/trump-signs-order-to-launch-vance-led-anti-fraud-task-force), [White House](https://www.whitehouse.gov/fact-sheets/2026/03/fact-sheet-president-donald-j-trump-promotes-access-to-mortgage-credit/)

## NO KINGS III — COMPREHENSIVE PRE-EVENT BRIEFING (March 28, 2026 — 10 Days Out)

### The Movement So Far

| Event | Date | Turnout (Organizer Est.) | Independent Est. | Locations |
|-------|------|--------------------------|-------------------|-----------|
| No Kings I | June 14, 2025 | **5 million** | ~4-5M | 2,000+ cities |
| No Kings II | October 18, 2025 | **7 million** | 5-6.5M | 2,700+ cities |
| **No Kings III** | **March 28, 2026** | **Target: 9 million** | TBD | **1,000+ confirmed** |

Context: No Kings I coincided with the Army's 250th Anniversary Parade and Trump's 79th birthday (June 14). No Kings II drew 300,000+ to Manhattan/Times Square alone.

**If organizers hit 9M, that would make it the largest single-day protest in American history.** The Women's March (2017) drew ~4.2M. No Kings II already surpassed it.

### What's Different This Time

**1. The triggers are worse:**

Since No Kings II (October), the following happened:
- Renee Nicole Good killed by ICE (Jan 7) — agent caught on video calling her a slur
- Alex Pretti killed by CBP (Jan 24) — video shows he was disarmed before being shot
- Ruben Martinez video released proving ICE lied about his killing
- Operation Metro Surge (3,000 federal agents in Minneapolis)
- General strikes (Jan 23 Minnesota, Jan 30 nationwide)
- DHS shutdown (Day 32 and counting)
- TSA workers getting $0 paychecks during spring break
- **Iran war** — 3,114+ dead including 207+ children, school bombing confirmed as "outdated intelligence"
- Ground invasion of Lebanon (March 17)
- Gas from $2.90 → $3.84 in one month
- South Pars gas field struck (March 18, today)
- Joe Kent (Trump's own counterterrorism chief) resigned over the war
- Housing bill passed 89-10 held hostage by SAVE Act
- 9 people dead from DHS agents, zero criminal charges

**Every single accelerant is firing simultaneously.** This is unprecedented.

**2. Unprecedented preparation:**

The coalition learned from the federal crackdown in Minneapolis and is approaching March 28 with military-grade organization:
- **"Eyes on ICE" training**: 200,000+ viewers on first session — teaches rights monitoring, documentation, de-escalation
- **Thousands of trained volunteer marshals** (Indivisible) maintaining nonviolent discipline
- **Legal observer networks** pre-positioned at every major event
- **Formal de-escalation teams** at all flagship events
- **"Real security and support infrastructure"** — organizers' words
- **2+ months of preparation** (vs. weeks for previous events)

[Sources: TIME](https://time.com/7358310/no-kings-protests-march-28-anti-trump-ice/), [Good Good Good](https://www.goodgoodgood.co/articles/no-kings-protest-march), [NBC News](https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/politics-news/no-kings-march-event-twin-cities-rcna256213)

### The Coalition (~300+ Organizations)

Major confirmed partners:
- **Indivisible** (lead organizer)
- **50501**
- **AFL-CIO**
- **ACLU**
- **American Federation of Teachers**
- **Human Rights Campaign**
- **League of Conservation Voters**
- **MoveOn**

[Source: ACLU](https://www.aclu.org/press-releases/no-kings-coalition-responds-to-escalating-brutality)

### Government Response — What Happened at NK1 & NK2 (Context for What May Come)

⚠️ **NOTE:** The deployments below are from **No Kings I (June 2025) and No Kings II (October 2025)**. As of March 23, no governor has yet announced National Guard activation specifically for No Kings III (March 28). Given that Abbott and Youngkin deployed both previous times, it would be surprising if they don't — but it's not confirmed yet.

**What happened at previous No Kings protests:**

| State | Governor | Action (NK1/NK2, 2025) |
|-------|----------|--------|
| Texas | Abbott (R) | **Deployed 5,000 National Guard + 2,000 state police** to Austin, Houston, Dallas, San Antonio. Called protests "antifa-linked." Did this for both NK1 and NK2. |
| Virginia | Youngkin (R) | Activated National Guard including "Quick Reaction Force" and "Non-Lethal Weapons Platoon" staged outside Richmond. Said he'd have "zero tolerance" for disruption. |
| California | — | Trump ordered Guard deployment without Newsom's consent — **blocked by federal judge** (Judge Charles Breyer) |
| Illinois | Pritzker (D) | **Supreme Court (6-3) ruled Trump CANNOT deploy Guard** without governor's consent (Dec 2025 ruling) |
| Oregon | — | Trump ordered Guard deployment, Hegseth federalized 200 Oregon Guard over Gov. Kotek's objection |
| Washington | Ferguson (D) | Called potential deployment "unconstitutional" — AG joined multistate lawsuit |
| Washington DC | — | Trump ordered Guard deployment ($660M projected cost through end of year per CBO) |

**Key legal backdrop:** The Supreme Court's December 2025 ruling in *Trump v. Illinois* (6-3, conservative justices split 3-3) held that Trump "failed to identify a source of authority" to deploy the Guard without governor's consent. BUT Justice Kavanaugh noted Trump has "other legal options" including the regular armed forces. This is the Insurrection Act question — still unresolved.

[Sources: NPR](https://www.npr.org/2025/12/23/nx-s1-5641959/supreme-court-chicago-national-guard), [PBS](https://www.pbs.org/newshour/nation/abbott-deploys-texas-national-guard-troops-ahead-of-no-kings-protests), [NBC News](https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/supreme-court/supreme-court-rejects-trump-bid-deploy-national-guard-illinois-rcna238630)

### 3.5% Threshold — Updated Assessment

The Chenoweth threshold for the US is **11.7 million people** (3.5% of ~335M).

| Factor | Assessment | Impact on Turnout |
|--------|------------|-------------------|
| Gas at $3.84, heading to $4+ | Hits every American daily | 🔴 Strong driver |
| TSA chaos during spring break | Personal experience of government failure | 🔴 Strong driver |
| 13 US soldiers dead | Gold Star families, veterans communities | 🔴 Growing |
| School bombing (168+ children) | Confirmed "outdated intelligence" — negligent | 🔴 Devastating |
| Ground invasion of Lebanon | Widening war, no exit strategy | 🔴 New since last assessment |
| South Pars strike + Gulf threats | Oil could hit $130+, gas could hit $5+ | 🔴 Escalating TODAY |
| Joe Kent resignation | First MAGA crack — Tucker interview coming | 🔴 Could shift Republican turnout |
| Housing bill hostage | 89-10 bipartisan bill blocked | 🟡 Moderate anger |
| DHS shutdown Day 32 | TSA/FEMA/Coast Guard suffering | 🔴 Strong driver |
| Zero accountability for ICE killings | Martinez video proved they lied | 🔴 Strong driver |
| Iran death toll 3,114+ | Including 207+ children | 🔴 Moral weight |

**Revised probability of hitting 11.7M (3.5%):**

Previous estimate: **20%**

Updated estimate: **25-30%**

The combination of the war escalating (South Pars, ground invasion, Kent resignation), gas prices becoming impossible to ignore, TSA collapse during spring break, and the school bombing being confirmed as negligence — these are all hitting simultaneously with 10 days to build momentum.

**The Tucker Carlson / Joe Kent interview could be the wildcard.** If it airs before March 28 and shifts even 5% of the MAGA base toward protest, that changes everything. The anti-war right showing up alongside the anti-war left would be historically unprecedented.

### What Could Still Go Wrong

1. **Weather** — Late March in the Northeast/Midwest could be cold/rainy
2. **Federal provocation** — If the Guard overreacts at an early event, it could suppress turnout elsewhere... or double it
3. **Protest fatigue** — Third event in 9 months; some people may stay home
4. **Iran ceasefire** — If a ceasefire happens before March 28, it removes a major accelerant (unlikely given Mojtaba's statements)
5. **Gas prices drop** — If IEA reserves actually stabilize prices (unlikely with Hormuz still closed)

### What Could Make It Bigger Than Anyone Expects

1. **Tucker + Kent interview airs** before March 28
2. **Iran retaliates against Gulf energy** → gas spikes to $5+
3. **Another ICE killing** — the pattern suggests it's a matter of when, not if
4. **TSA airport actually closes** → spring break travelers stranded
5. **Trump invokes Insurrection Act** → would massively backfire
6. **A major celebrity/cultural figure joins** (none confirmed yet)

**Three potential ground operations being discussed:**

2. **Hormuz shoreline operations** — Deploy troops to Iran's coast to secure tanker passage. Essentially occupying Iranian territory.

3. **Uranium stockpile seizure** — Special operations to secure highly enriched uranium. Most dangerous option — facilities deep underground, heavily defended, spread across multiple sites.

**The 5,000 Marines arriving end of March is the key signal.** The USS Tripoli departed Okinawa March 11 — that means the ground invasion force was deployed **before** South Pars, **before** Lebanon, and **before** today's Reuters report. This was planned weeks ago.

Cuba is exhibit A: you don't need to bomb a country to destroy it. Cut off their oil, sanction anyone who helps them, capture their main patron (Maduro), and wait.

**This is what a slow-motion regime change looks like.** No troops, no bombs, just 11 million people sitting in the dark while hospitals close and food runs out.
