## NO KINGS III — HOW I THINK IT GOES (Analysis, March 19)

### The Short Version

**It will almost certainly be the largest single-day protest in American history.** The question isn't whether it's big — it's whether it crosses the threshold where it actually changes anything, and whether the government does something stupid that either kills momentum or supercharges it.

---

### SCENARIO 1: The Base Case (55% probability)
**"Massive, peaceful, historically large — but the system absorbs it"**

**Turnout: 8-11 million**

This is the most likely outcome. Here's what it looks like:

- Turnout smashes the No Kings II record of 7M. Lands somewhere between 8M and 11M.
- 3,000+ events go off across all 50 states. The Twin Cities flagship draws 500K+. NYC draws 400K+. DC, Philly, Chicago, Atlanta, SF all draw 100K+.
- The day is **overwhelmingly peaceful** — the organizer infrastructure (trained marshals, de-escalation teams, legal observers, Eyes on ICE program) holds discipline at 95%+ of locations.
- A handful of incidents: maybe a car-ramming attempt somewhere (the pattern from previous No Kings), maybe tear gas in Austin or LA where National Guard is pre-deployed, maybe an arrest surge at one or two flashpoint cities.
- Cable news covers it wall-to-wall. The images are powerful. Aerial shots of millions in the streets.
- Trump tweets something dismissive. Calls them "communists" and "antifa." Posts AI images of himself in a crown again (he actually did this for No Kings II).
- Monday morning, everyone goes back to work. Congress doesn't change anything. The war continues. Gas prices keep climbing.

**Why this is the most likely outcome:** This is what happened with No Kings I and II. Massive turnout, peaceful, historically significant — and then nothing structurally changed. The system is designed to absorb protest. Protest alone doesn't create power; sustained disruption does. One day, even with 10M people, is a demonstration, not a revolution.

**The Chenoweth caveat:** Erica Chenoweth's own research says the 3.5% threshold requires **sustained mobilization**, not a single day. No government has fallen from a one-day event, no matter how large. The question is whether March 28 becomes the launchpad for sustained action or a cathartic release valve that dissipates energy.

---

### SCENARIO 2: The Breakthrough (20-25% probability)
**"Something happens that makes this ungovernable"**

**Turnout: 11-15 million (crosses 3.5% threshold)**

This is the scenario where it actually matters. For this to happen, you need at least one of these catalysts to hit **before or during** March 28:

**Pre-event catalysts (any one could do it):**
- Tucker Carlson airs the Joe Kent interview → pulls anti-war right into the streets alongside the left. **This is the single biggest wildcard.** If Tucker tells his audience "this war is wrong" and Kent — a Gold Star, 11-combat-tour MAGA veteran — backs it up, you could see a meaningful chunk of Republican voters join. That's never happened at a No Kings event. It would be transformational.
- Iran retaliates against Gulf energy → gas spikes past $5 overnight → everyone feels it
- Another ICE killing in the days before (pattern suggests this is when, not if)
- Marines visibly arriving in the Persian Gulf, broadcast on news → "ground invasion" becomes real, not theoretical
- TSA airport actually closes → stranded travelers join protests at airports
- Maduro court appearance March 26 (two days before) generates major coverage of the Venezuela operation

**Day-of catalysts:**
- Trump invokes the Insurrection Act or deploys federal agents against protesters → backfire effect. History is clear: violent government response to peaceful protest **increases** turnout and sympathy. Kent State didn't end the anti-war movement; it exploded it.
- National Guard confrontation goes viral in real-time → people who were staying home see it and come out
- Spontaneous general strike energy → if enough people simply don't go to work on Monday, March 30

**What breakthrough looks like:**
- March 28 isn't the end — it's the beginning of sustained action
- Ongoing occupations, rolling strikes, daily marches
- Congressional offices besieged
- "Don't go to work" campaigns gain traction
- The midterm election (November 2026) becomes a referendum on everything

**Why 20-25%:** Every accelerant is firing simultaneously — war, gas, TSA, ICE killings, housing — but converting a protest into a sustained movement requires organizational infrastructure that goes beyond a single day. The coalition has it (300+ orgs, trained marshals, ACLU/AFL-CIO/SEIU). The question is whether the moment is big enough that people don't go home.

---

### SCENARIO 3: Government Overreaction (15% probability)
**"They do something stupid and create a martyr moment"**

This is the scenario that scares me most — not for March 28 itself, but for what comes after.

**What "stupid" looks like:**
- National Guard in Texas or DC fires on protesters (even "less-lethal" — rubber bullets, tear gas on a massive scale)
- ICE agents arrest protest organizers pre-emptively (they've signaled willingness to do this)
- Trump federalizes the National Guard using the Insurrection Act (he's been threatening this since June 2025)
- A counter-protester car-ramming kills people (happened at Charlottesville, almost happened at previous No Kings)
- Federal agents raid the Twin Cities flagship event where 3,000 ICE/CBP agents are already deployed

**The ACLED data is concerning:** In 2025, 22% of all protests where police engaged saw "less-lethal" munitions used — **quadruple** the 2024 rate. The trend line is toward more aggressive police response, not less.

**If this happens:**
- It does NOT kill the movement. The historical pattern is unambiguous: violent government response to peaceful protest creates a backlash that's larger than the original movement.
- But people get hurt. Maybe killed.
- The country enters a fundamentally different phase — one where the legitimacy of the government itself is in open question.
- International response intensifies. Allied governments issue stronger statements. UN involvement possible.
- The comparison to Tiananmen, Bloody Sunday, Kent State becomes impossible to avoid.

**Why 15%:** The administration has shown willingness to use force (Minneapolis deployments, tear gas in Austin/LA/Seattle at previous No Kings, National Guard pre-positioning). But they also know the optics. Cracking down on millions of peaceful Americans protesting a war that 74% oppose would be political suicide heading into midterms. The rational play is to let it happen and dismiss it. But "rational" hasn't been the administration's strong suit.

---

### SCENARIO 4: Fizzle (5% probability)
**"It's smaller than expected and the moment passes"**

**Turnout: 4-6 million (below No Kings II)**

For this to happen, you'd need:
- Major weather event across multiple regions on March 28
- A ceasefire in Iran announced before March 28 (Mojtaba's statements make this nearly impossible)
- Gas prices somehow drop (they won't — Hormuz is closed and South Pars is offline)
- Protest fatigue overwhelms anger (3rd event in 9 months)
- A major domestic terror attack that changes the narrative

**Why only 5%:** Basically everything would have to break against the movement simultaneously. Every single indicator — gas, war, TSA, ICE, housing, the economy — is pushing toward maximum turnout. The accelerants aren't theoretical; they're hitting people's wallets, travel plans, and sense of safety every day. You'd need a miracle of bad luck for this to fizzle.

---

### MY HONEST ASSESSMENT FOR YOUR FAMILY

**Go to the Jersey City event (11 AM, Grove Street PATH).** Here's why:

1. **It will be safe.** Jersey City is a local, daytime, relatively small event. The coalition has marshals trained. The risk of confrontation is near-zero in JC — the danger is in Minneapolis, Austin, LA, DC where Guard is deployed.

2. **Take the kids if you want.** The organizers have explicitly designed family-friendly daytime events at the local level. The NYC march (2 PM Manhattan) is where things *could* get more intense — I'd skip that one with kids.

3. **Don't go to Manhattan with the family.** 300K+ people, NYPD in full force, potential for incidents. Go alone or with your wife if you want to, but not with small children.

4. **Be home by 2 PM.** If anything goes wrong nationally, it'll be afternoon/evening. The early local events are the safe window.

5. **This matters historically.** Your kids will ask someday what you did. "We went to the protest in Jersey City" is a good answer.

6. **But it probably won't change anything by itself.** One day of protest, no matter how large, doesn't overthrow a government. What matters is what happens March 29, 30, 31 and beyond. If the energy sustains into a general strike or rolling action, that's different. If everyone goes home Monday, it's a footnote.

### The Real Question

The real question isn't "how does No Kings go." It's **"what happens the week after."**

If 10 million people march on Saturday and nothing changes on Monday — the war continues, gas keeps climbing, TSA workers still aren't getting paid, the housing bill stays hostage — then the question becomes: **what are people willing to do beyond marching?**

That's where movements either become revolutions or become memories.

## LAST 7 DAYS — March 16-23, 2026

**The most consequential week since February 28.** Ground invasions, nuclear facilities targeted, a 2-hour Tucker interview that cracked the MAGA coalition, ICE deployed to airports, Trump claiming peace talks Iran says don't exist, and No Kings III now 5 days away with 3,000+ events.

---

### 🔴 IRAN WAR — Day 17 → Day 24

#### The Week in Five Turning Points

**1. Iran struck Dimona — Israel's nuclear facility targeted for the first time (March 22)**

IRGC commander Ghalibaf announced Iranian missiles struck near Dimona, Israel's nuclear research center, injuring 100+ people. He called it a "new stage of battle" and said "Israel's skies are defenceless." This is the first time Iran has targeted Israel's nuclear infrastructure — a massive escalation that signals Iran is willing to match Israel blow-for-blow on the most sensitive targets.

[Source: JPost](https://www.jpost.com/middle-east/iran-news/2026-03-22/live-updates-890731)

**2. Trump's 48-hour Hormuz ultimatum → postponement → "talks" (March 22-23)**

Saturday: Trump gave Iran 48 hours to reopen the Strait of Hormuz or face strikes on power plants.

Sunday/Monday: Trump posted on Truth Social that the US and Iran had "very good and productive conversations" with "major points of agreement." Said he's postponing power plant strikes for 5 days. Claims Witkoff and Kushner engaged in talks Sunday night. Said there are "15 points of agreement" including Iran accepting no nukes.

**Iran's response: They denied any talks are happening.** Semi-official Mehr news agency said no dialogue exists. State TV displayed: "U.S. president backs down following Iran's firm warning." An unnamed senior security official called it "psychological warfare."

Iran also warned that if power plants are hit, they will **"completely close" the Hormuz** (currently partially closed) and strike electrical plants and desalination facilities across Saudi Arabia, UAE, and Qatar.

**Translation:** Trump blinked. He issued an ultimatum, realized he couldn't follow through without triggering a global energy catastrophe, and is now claiming negotiations exist that Iran says don't. He bought himself 5 days.

[Sources: Al Jazeera](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/23/trump-postpones-military-strikes-on-iranian-power-plants), [Bloomberg](https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2026-03-23/trump-backs-off-from-iran-threat-as-ceasefire-talks-get-underway), [NBC News](https://www.nbcnews.com/world/middle-east/live-blog/live-updates-iran-war-trump-hormuz-deadline-energy-crisis-gulf-power-rcna264685), [CBS News](https://www.cbsnews.com/live-updates/iran-war-us-israel-gas-and-oil-prices-trump-netanyahu-strait-hormuz/)

**3. Iran attacking Gulf states directly (March 19-22)**

This is no longer theoretical:
- Iranian drones hit **Kuwait's Mina Al-Ahmadi oil refinery** (March 19-20) — fires, crews scrambling
- **3 ballistic missiles fired at Riyadh, Saudi Arabia** (March 22) — 1 intercepted, 2 landed in uninhabited area. Plus 6 drones shot down over eastern region
- **UAE intercepting missiles and drones over Dubai** — explosions during Eid prayers. Indian national injured by falling debris in Abu Dhabi
- **Debris from intercepts raining on Israeli communities** including Rehovot (near Tel Aviv)

Iran is now actively attacking **4 countries simultaneously** (Israel, Kuwait, Saudi Arabia, UAE). This is the regional war everyone feared.

**4. Trump "winding down" rhetoric vs. Marines still heading in (March 20-21)**

Trump posted: "We are getting very close to meeting our objectives as we consider winding down our great Military efforts." When asked about ground troops: "No. I'm not putting troops anywhere."

**Meanwhile:** The USS Tripoli with 5,000 Marines continues steaming toward the Persian Gulf. Expected arrival: end of March. The Pentagon hasn't recalled them. Nobody in the military is talking about winding down.

[Source: NPR](https://www.npr.org/2026/03/20/nx-s1-5754550/israel-strikes-tehran-iran-attacks-gulf)

**5. IEA: This is worse than the 1970s oil crises (March 23)**

The International Energy Agency's executive director said the current energy disruption is **"very severe" and worse than both the 1973 and 1979 oil shocks combined.** The near-total halt of Hormuz traffic has removed ~20% of global oil supply.

Oil prices: Brent hit $114, then crashed to $104 on Trump's "talks" claim, then bounced back. Goldman Sachs forecasts Brent averaging $110 through April. WTI swung from $100 to $91.

[Source: CNN](https://www.cnn.com/2026/03/20/energy/oil-gas-prices-intl-hnk)

### 🔴 THE TUCKER/KENT INTERVIEW — March 18 (THE WEEK'S BIGGEST STORY)

**This happened. It's as big as we predicted. Maybe bigger.**

Joe Kent sat with Tucker Carlson for **121 minutes** on March 18. Key bombshells:

**1. "No intelligence showed Iran was near a bomb"**
Kent said intelligence assessments did NOT show Iran posed an imminent threat or was close to a nuclear weapon — undercutting the central justification for the war.

**2. "Israel drove the decision"**
"The Israelis drove the decision to take this action, which we knew would trigger retaliation... They felt emboldened that no matter what they did, we would just have to react."

**3. Officials were shut out**
"A good deal of key decision makers were not allowed to come and express their opinion" to the President. "There wasn't a robust debate this time — it felt like a foregone conclusion."

**4. Iran's nuclear fatwa**
Kent cited Iran's 2004 religious ruling (fatwa) against developing nuclear weapons, saying no intelligence showed it had been violated or lifted.

**5. 💣 Kent insinuated Israel may have killed Charlie Kirk**
This is the one that blew up everything. Kent suggested to Carlson that Israel might have been behind the September 2025 assassination of Charlie Kirk — the MAGA influencer shot and killed at Utah Valley University — as part of a pressure campaign to stoke support for war with Iran.

For context: Charlie Kirk, 31, was shot and killed by a sniper on September 10, 2025 while speaking at a Turning Point USA event. Tyler James Robinson, 22, was arrested and is facing the death penalty. His preliminary hearing is May 18.

Kent's insinuation — without evidence — that Israel orchestrated this assassination has created a firestorm:
- **FBI launched investigation** into whether Kent shared classified material during the interview
- **McConnell condemned** Kent's statements as "virulent anti-Semitism"
- **Bannon praised Kent** on his show: "highly revered — 11 combat tours, valour and courage beyond question... you are going to have to investigate this"
- **MAGA base is now split** between pro-war (Haley, Graham, McConnell wing) and anti-war (Kent, Carlson, Bannon wing)

**Why this matters for No Kings:** The MAGA coalition is fracturing over the war. Kent + Carlson + Bannon represent the populist/isolationist right. If even 5% of the MAGA base starts questioning the war because of this interview, the political calculus changes. This fracture also makes it harder for Republicans to dismiss No Kings III as purely a "left-wing" event.

[Sources: CNN](https://www.cnn.com/2026/03/18/politics/joe-kent-iran-tucker-carlson), [Military.com](https://www.military.com/daily-news/headlines/2026/03/19/kent-tells-carlson-no-intelligence-showed-iran-near-bomb.html), [NPR](https://www.npr.org/2026/03/19/nx-s1-5752199/joe-kent-speaks-out-about-his-decision-to-resign-in-protest-over-the-iran-war), [JTA](https://www.jta.org/2026/03/19/politics/joe-kent-now-under-investigation-insinuates-to-tucker-carlson-that-israel-might-have-killed-charlie-kirk-to-stoke-iran-war), [CBC](https://www.cbc.ca/news/world/joe-kent-tucker-carlson-iran-war-criticism-9.7134242)

### 🔴 DHS SHUTDOWN — Day 37: ICE AT THE AIRPORTS

**This is the headline: Trump is deploying ICE agents to airports starting TODAY (March 23).**

| Metric | March 18 | March 23 | Change |
|--------|----------|----------|--------|
| DHS shutdown day | 32 | **37** | Week 6 |
| TSA officers quit | 366+ | **400+** | Still hemorrhaging |
| Single-day callouts (peak) | 3,000+ | **3,250+** (Saturday) | New record |
| Houston Hobby callout | 55% | **Still 50%+** | |
| Philadelphia | Checkpoints open | **3 checkpoints CLOSED** entirely | NEW |
| Missed paychecks | 1 full | **2nd full paycheck this week** | Devastating |
| Spring break travelers | Peak season | **2.8M/day, 171M total projected** | Worst timing |

**The ICE-at-airports move:**
- Trump announced Saturday via Truth Social that ICE would deploy to airports starting Monday
- Homan says "hundreds" of ICE officers will assist — checking IDs, covering exits, freeing TSA for screening
- ICE will NOT operate X-ray machines or do security screening
- **AFGE union (50,000+ TSA workers):** ICE agents "are not trained or certified in aviation security"
- **Flight Attendants Union:** Called it "latest threat of ICE invasion" and a "distraction from solutions"
- **Former senior ICE official:** Using CBP officers would make more sense since they already work at international airports
- **Elon Musk offered to personally pay TSA staff** — US law generally bars outside compensation for government employees

**The real purpose:** This isn't about airport security. It's about putting immigration agents in airports where millions of travelers will see them — during a protest week. ICE at airports 5 days before No Kings III is a provocation.

[Sources: Washington Post](https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/2026/03/21/trump-threatens-deploy-ice-airports-tsa-shortages-drive-delays/), [CNBC](https://www.cnbc.com/2026/03/23/airport-lines-government-shutdown-tsa.html), [CBS News](https://www.cbsnews.com/news/dhs-officials-trump-ice-agents-airport-security-tsa/), [NPR](https://www.npr.org/2026/03/21/nx-s1-5755796/airport-security-tsa-lines-travel-tips), [NBC News](https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/politics-news/tom-homan-ice-crowded-airport-security-tsa-screenings-wait-times-rcna264618)

**DHS Deal Talks:**
- Thune threatening to cancel Easter recess unless deal reached
- Top Republicans and Democrats huddled with Homan on Thursday
- NBC: "Bipartisan talks get serious" — but still no breakthrough
- Democrats' position unchanged: fund TSA/FEMA/Coast Guard separately, attach body cams/IDs to ICE
- Republicans' position: fund all of DHS together, no conditions on ICE

[Source: NBC News](https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/congress/bipartisan-talks-end-homeland-security-shutdown-get-serious-rcna264322)

**Progressive organizations:**
- MoveOn
- Public Citizen

- Planned Parenthood
- Working Families Party

**Interfaith Alliance** endorsing and organizing faith-based contingents

### WHAT THE GOP IS SAYING

⚠️ **IMPORTANT NOTE:** As of March 23, most top Republicans have NOT issued specific new statements about No Kings III. The quotes below from Johnson, Emmer, etc. are from **No Kings II (October 2025)** — they have been recycled in reporting as representative of the GOP stance, but we cannot confirm these exact phrases have been repeated for NK3. Trump himself has NOT addressed No Kings III — he is consumed by the Iran crisis and his March 29 deadline.

**What was said about No Kings I & II (for context):**

| Republican | Statement (NK1/NK2, 2025) | Framing |
|------------|-----------|---------|
| **Speaker Mike Johnson** | Called NK2 a **"hate America rally"** drawing "the pro-Hamas wing" and "the antifa people" (Oct 2025) | Delegitimize |
| **Majority Whip Tom Emmer** | Called NK2 "hate-America rally" — championed by **"the terrorist wing"** of the Democratic Party (Oct 2025) | Delegitimize |
| **Johnson on NK2 (after)** | "Begrudgingly lauded" No Kings II for being a "violent-free, free speech exercise" — an admission that undermined the "antifa" narrative | Concede |

**What IS confirmed for No Kings III (March 2026):**

| Republican | Statement/Action (NK3, March 2026) | Framing |
|------------|-----------|---------|
| **Gov. Abbott (TX)** | Deployed Guard for NK1 & NK2 (5,000 troops each time). No NK3 announcement yet as of March 23, but expected. | Militarize (likely) |

| **Sen. Roger Marshall** | Claimed protesters are "being paid" — suggested National Guard "might need to show up" | Criminalize |
| **Mitch McConnell** | Condemned Kent's statements as "virulent anti-Semitism" (indirect — re: Tucker interview, not NK3 directly) | Deflect from war criticism |
| **Never Trumper Republicans** | **$1M ad campaign** — Home of the Brave (Bill Kristol on board) placed ads in **300 newspapers across 31 states** supporting No Kings III. Genuinely new: Republicans publicly backing the protest. | Support |

**The GOP playbook (ongoing, recycled from NK1/NK2):** Three coordinated tactics:
1. **Delegitimize** — "hate America," "antifa," "pro-Hamas," "paid by Soros"
2. **Criminalize** — National Guard deployments, "paid protesters," hints at Insurrection Act
3. **Minimize** — "a joke," "not representative"

**The notable silence:** Trump, Johnson, and most top GOP leaders haven't specifically attacked NK3. Whether that's strategic (don't amplify it) or distraction (Iran consuming all bandwidth) is unclear.

[Sources: MSNBC](https://www.ms.now/rachel-maddow-show/maddowblog/ahead-no-kings-events-republicans-anti-protest-rhetoric-takes-ugly-tur-rcna237271), [Rolling Stone](https://www.rollingstone.com/politics/politics-news/trump-right-reactions-no-kings-protests-1235450106/)

**The dynamic:** Rank-and-file protesters are more radical than Democratic leadership. They see Schumer and Jeffries as too cautious. The movement is pushing the party leftward — or threatening to go around it entirely.

### WHAT CONSERVATIVE MEDIA IS SAYING

**Fox News' playbook is revealing:**

Fox's No Kings II coverage ran with the headline: **"Violent symbolism, threats steal show at nationwide 'No Kings' protests"**

Columbia Journalism Review investigated and called this **"an incredibly misleading headline and framing"** — the protests were overwhelmingly peaceful.

**The pattern:**
1. Fox finds isolated incidents (a threatening sign, an angry outburst) from events with millions of attendees
2. Makes that the headline
3. Ignores the 99.9% that was peaceful
4. Bret Baier did a segment: "There is no king here" — giving "radical No Kings protesters a reality check"
5. The Daily Show responded: "The only chaos at the No Kings protest happened in the Fox News control room"

**What Fox ISN'T covering:** The Tucker/Kent interview aired on Tucker's independent show, not on Fox. Fox has largely avoided covering Kent's claims about Israel driving the war or the Charlie Kirk insinuation. There's a **split between Fox (pro-war establishment right) and Tucker/Bannon (anti-war populist right)** that No Kings III is widening.

[Sources: CJR](https://www.cjr.org/analysis/did-the-no-kings-protests-get-enough-attention.php), [Fox News](https://www.foxnews.com/us/violent-symbolism-threats-steal-show-nationwide-no-kings-protests), [Rolling Stone](https://www.rollingstone.com/politics/politics-news/trump-right-reactions-no-kings-protests-1235450106/)

**No Kings has higher support than the Tea Party or Occupy ever achieved, and matches BLM.**

**Trump approval:** Slipping into low-to-mid 40s. Growing disapproval tied to Iran war and executive overreach.

**Midterm enthusiasm:** **65%+ of voters** rate their interest at 9 or 10 out of 10 — on par with levels typically seen **right before** a midterm, not 8 months out. The majority of those highly enthused voters want Democratic control of Congress.

### SAFETY INFRASTRUCTURE — THE DEEPEST LOOK

**This is the most organized protest infrastructure in American history.**

**Legal observers:**
- ACLU training legal observers in advance across multiple states
- Document police conduct, protect constitutional rights
- Trainings scheduled March 23 (today) and throughout the week
- [Source: InForum](https://www.inforum.com/news/fargo/legal-observer-training-scheduled-in-advance-of-next-no-kings-rally-in-fargo)

**Safety marshals:**
- Thousands trained by Indivisible
- Roles: guide marches, de-escalation, communicate with participants
- Written safety plans for every major event
- Dignity- and teamwork-rooted de-escalation techniques

**"Eyes on ICE" training:**
- 200,000+ viewers on first session
- Teaches: legal documentation of ICE, safe distance protocols, recording rights, de-escalation
- Goal: "Train millions of Americans in ICE observation"
- Run by: ACLU, Indivisible, Working Families Party
- Levin: "A big part of why we do No Kings is to bring new activists into the ongoing organizing work"
- [Source: Public Citizen](https://www.citizen.org/news/tonight-no-kings-coalition-hosts-eyes-on-ice-training-to-prepare-community-members-for-non-violent-documentation-of-trump-administration-repression/)

**Medical:**
- Community medic teams at all flagship events
- Supply distribution and coordination

**Know Your Rights (ACLU):**
- Constitutional right to peacefully protest
- What to do if police approach
- What to do if arrested
- Recording rights
- Next training: **March 23, 6:00 PM EST** (tonight)

**Why this level of preparation:** The federal response in Minneapolis — 3,000 agents, two citizens killed — showed that the government is willing to use force against Americans. The coalition learned from that and built infrastructure to match. This isn't 2017 Women's March spontaneous energy. This is organized, trained, legally prepared mass mobilization.

---

### THE BANNON/TUCKER WILD CARD

**This is the factor nobody predicted.**

The anti-war populist right — Bannon, Tucker, now Kent — is breaking with the pro-war establishment right (Fox, Graham, McConnell) over Iran.

- **Tucker's interview** (121 minutes, March 18) gave Kent a massive platform
- **Bannon praised Kent** as "highly revered" and demanded investigation into war's origins
- **Kent insinuated Israel killed Charlie Kirk** — explosive, unproven, but now in the discourse
- **FBI investigating Kent** for potentially sharing classified material

**The question for March 28:** Does any of this translate to right-wing bodies at No Kings events?

Probably not in large numbers. But even a few thousand MAGA-coded anti-war protesters showing up — veterans, populists, Bannon listeners — would be symbolically devastating for the administration. It would destroy the "this is just antifa" narrative overnight.

---

### THE MEDIA COVERAGE PROBLEM

**CJR identified a structural issue:** Major media undercovered No Kings I and II relative to their historical scale.

- The top Google result for No Kings II was a Fox News headline about "violent symbolism" — at a 7-million-person peaceful protest
- Kathleen Culver (UW-Madison journalism school): Called Fox's framing "incredibly misleading"
- Network TV gave No Kings II roughly the same coverage as a medium-sized natural disaster
- The New York Times ran No Kings II as a below-the-fold story

**Why this matters:** If 9 million people march and the coverage leads with one broken window, the public perception is distorted. The coalition is aware of this and has built its own media infrastructure (NoKings.org, social media, Eyes on ICE livestreams, trained citizen journalists).

[Source: CJR](https://www.cjr.org/analysis/did-the-no-kings-protests-get-enough-attention.php)

---

### THE MIDTERM CONNECTION

**Everyone — organizers, Reich, Democrats, even some Republicans — knows the real battleground is November 2026.**

- **Reich:** "Months from now, we should get out the largest midterm vote in history"
- **Indivisible:** Already pivoting toward "local legislative advocacy and voter protection initiatives"
- **Bernie Sanders:** Teaming with Run for Something — 5,000+ progressive candidates already signed up
- **NBC poll:** 65%+ of voters at 9-10/10 enthusiasm for midterms — unprecedented this early
- **Majority of enthusiastic voters** favor Democratic control and blame Republicans for the shutdown

No Kings III isn't just a protest. It's a **voter registration and mobilization machine** for the midterms. Every event has voter registration tables. Every training includes "what to do after March 28." The coalition is explicitly building toward November.

[Sources: NBC News](https://www.nbcnews.com/news/amp/rcna242391), [Robert Reich](https://robertreich.substack.com/p/get-ready-for-march-28-no-kings), [The Advocate](https://www.advocate.com/politics/no-kings-long-term-plans)

### THE CONVERGENCE — March 28-29

Everything hits at once:

| Date | Event | Connection |
|------|-------|------------|
| March 23 (today) | ICE deployed to airports | Provocation — armed immigration agents greeting spring break travelers |
| March 23 | ACLU Know Your Rights training 6 PM EST | Final mass training before the day |
| March 24 | SAVE Act debate continues | Legislative paralysis visible |
| March 26 | **Maduro court appearance (Brooklyn)** | Reminder of regime change — protests likely outside courthouse |
| March 27 | Pre-protest positioning | Marshals, legal observers, medics deploying |
| **March 28** | **NO KINGS III — 3,000+ events, 9M+ target** | **THE DAY** |
| **March 29** | **Trump's Iran 5-day deadline expires** | If no deal → does he bomb power plants while millions are still mobilized? |
| Late March | USS Tripoli + 5,000 Marines arrive in Gulf | Ground invasion force in theater |

**The timing is not coincidental.** Trump's self-imposed Iran deadline expires the day AFTER the largest protest in American history. If he follows through and bombs Iran's power plants on March 29 — while millions are still energized from the day before — the sustained mobilization scenario becomes much more likely.

And if he doesn't follow through, he looks weak. Again.

---

## DID NO KINGS I & II ACTUALLY ACCOMPLISH ANYTHING? — Honest Assessment

I said they "didn't change anything" in my scenario analysis. That was too dismissive. The truth is more complicated.

---

### WHAT THEY DIDN'T DO

Let's be honest about what did NOT happen:

- ❌ No major Trump policy was permanently reversed as a direct result
- ❌ Trump didn't moderate his behavior — if anything, he escalated
- ❌ No legislation passed because of the protests
- ❌ ICE operations continued and expanded
- ❌ The war happened anyway
- ❌ The DHS shutdown wasn't resolved
- ❌ Trump's base didn't abandon him

**The cynical take is correct at the surface level.** 12 million people marched across two events and Trump called them "a joke" and posted AI pictures of himself in a crown. That's real.

---

### WHAT THEY ACTUALLY DID

But here's what DID happen — and it matters more than it looks:

**1. They cratered Trump's approval rating**

| Period | Approval | Disapproval | Net |
|--------|----------|-------------|-----|
| Before No Kings I (May 2025) | ~46% | ~51% | -5 |
| After No Kings I (June 2025) | ~41-44% | ~54% | -10 to -13 |
| After No Kings II (Oct 2025) | **37-39%** | **58%** | **-19 to -21** |
| Current (March 2026) | **Low-to-mid 40s** | — | Trending down again |

Trump's post-No Kings II approval of **37%** was the lowest of his second term. That matters — not because Trump cares about polls, but because **Republican members of Congress do.** A president at 37% can't hold his caucus together. That's partly why the SAVE Act can't pass, why the filibuster hasn't been nuked, why Mullin is promising warrants.

[Sources: Newsweek](https://www.newsweek.com/donald-trump-approval-rating-polls-no-kings-protests-2087815), [YouGov](https://today.yougov.com/politics/articles/53277-new-second-term-low-donald-trump-job-approval-government-spending), [MSNBC](https://www.ms.now/the-weekend/watch/trump-s-approval-rating-drops-to-37-as-no-kings-protests-draw-millions-around-the-country-250190917519)

**2. They flipped the "MAGA vs. opposition" numbers**

- **43% of Americans** identify as No Kings supporters
- **30% of Americans** identify as MAGA supporters (down from 36% in March 2025)
- No Kings is now **more popular than MAGA** by 13 points

This had never happened before. The opposition to Trump now has a brand that outpolls his own movement. That's new.

[Source: NBC News poll via MSNBC](https://www.ms.now/rachel-maddow-show/maddowblog/poll-shows-no-kings-protest-movement-topping-maga-public-support-rcna241803)

**3. They shifted the "dictator" perception**

- Americans who describe Trump as a **"potentially dangerous dictator"**: **56%** (up from 52% in April)
- Americans who describe Trump as a **"strong leader"**: **41%** (down from 44%)
- Americans who think the president has **"too much power"**: **54%** (was 32% under Biden)

The protests didn't just express opposition — they *framed* the narrative. "No Kings" as a slogan connected Trump's behavior to America's founding story. It's simple, patriotic, and impossible for the right to argue against without sounding like they're defending monarchy.

[Source: PRRI survey via CNN](https://www.cnn.com/2025/10/22/politics/no-kings-rallies-trump-analysis)

**4. They reached Trump country**

This is the finding that should scare Republicans the most.

Harvard/Chenoweth Nonviolent Action Lab data:
- Protests reached **38% of all US counties** — including many that voted for Trump
- Average protest participation: **65 per 10,000 residents** (up 62.5% from Trump's first term)
- The protests weren't just coastal cities — they were in **rural red counties**

Jacobin's analysis: **"No Kings was a rebellion in Trump country."** The New Republic: **"Republicans should be afraid — just look at who joined."**

This is the Women's March comparison that matters. The Women's March was overwhelmingly coastal/urban/blue. No Kings penetrated Trump's base geography. That's the difference.

[Sources: Harvard Kennedy School](https://www.hks.harvard.edu/faculty-research/policy-topics/advocacy-social-movements/anti-trump-protests-are-making-headway), [Jacobin](https://jacobin.com/2025/06/no-kings-protests-trump-popularity), [New Republic](https://newrepublic.com/article/201970/republicans-afraid-who-joined-no-kings-protests)

**5. They built organizational infrastructure that didn't exist before**

- New Indivisible groups formed in small towns across the country because people raised their hands to organize No Kings events
- **325+ organizations** now in a functioning coalition
- Thousands of trained marshals, legal observers, de-escalation teams
- "Eyes on ICE" training program reaching hundreds of thousands
- **5,000+ progressive candidates** signed up through Run for Something (Bernie + Indivisible pipeline)

This is the invisible infrastructure that matters for November 2026. Every No Kings event created local organizing nodes. Those nodes don't disappear when the protest ends. They become voter registration drives, candidate recruitment operations, and midterm GOTV machines.

**6. They blocked specific legislation**

The ACLU tracked this directly:
- Generated **3 million+ digital actions** and **56,000+ constituent calls** to legislators
- Helped prevent **83% of federal anti-immigrant bills** from becoming law
- Blocked **all** new statutory restrictions on gender-affirming care
- Defeated **2 bills** threatening free speech

These aren't headline-grabbing wins, but they're real. Bills that would have passed in a quieter environment didn't pass because of the political cost No Kings created.

[Source: ACLU](https://www.aclu.org/news/civil-liberties/seven-million-people-unite-at-peaceful-no-kings-protests-to-defend-our-first-amendment-rights)

**7. They forced the DHS shutdown**

This is the one nobody talks about. The DHS shutdown happened because **Democrats had the political backbone to refuse funding without ICE accountability measures.** Where did that backbone come from?

Think about it: Would Senate Democrats have held firm on body cameras and officer IDs if 12 million people hadn't marched? Would they have risked being blamed for TSA chaos if they didn't know 43% of the country had their back?

The DHS shutdown — which has driven the body camera demand, the officer ID demand, the Mullin warrant promise — exists because No Kings gave Democrats the political cover to fight. The protests didn't directly cause the shutdown, but they created the conditions for it.

**8. They stiffened the spine on the Supreme Court ruling**

The December 2025 SCOTUS ruling (6-3) blocking Trump's National Guard deployment in Illinois didn't happen in a vacuum. Three conservative justices broke with Trump. That's partly about law, but it's also about political context — and the political context was 12 million people demonstrating that the country didn't support militarized domestic enforcement.

**9. 33% of Americans participated or knew someone who did**

One in three Americans. That's not a protest movement — that's a cultural event. That level of personal connection changes how people talk about politics at Thanksgiving, at work, at school pickup. It normalizes opposition in a way that no cable news segment or tweet can.

[Source: YouGov](https://today.yougov.com/topics/politics/survey-results/daily/2025/10/21/0f9b6/1)

---

### THE HONEST BOTTOM LINE

**No Kings I & II didn't overthrow Trump. They weren't going to. That's not what protests do in a single day.**

But here's what they DID do:

| Claim | Reality |
|-------|---------|
| "They accomplished nothing" | ❌ Wrong — cratered approval to 37%, flipped MAGA/opposition numbers, blocked legislation, built infrastructure |
| "They changed everything" | ❌ Also wrong — Trump escalated, the war happened, ICE kept killing people |
| "They were useless" | ❌ Wrong — created political conditions for DHS shutdown, Democrats' spine, SCOTUS ruling, 5,000 candidates |
| "They were sufficient" | ❌ Wrong — one-day protests alone never topple governments |

**The real answer:** No Kings I & II were **necessary but not sufficient.** They built the foundation. They shifted the numbers. They created the infrastructure. They gave the opposition a brand that outpolls MAGA.

But the scholar David Meyer's point is correct: **"Protests do not transform the world in one fell swoop; they foster change over time when combined with other tactics."** The protests need to be combined with:
- Sustained disruption (strikes, boycotts, civil disobedience)
- Electoral mobilization (the 5,000 candidates, the midterm GOTV)
- Legal strategy (ACLU litigation, state-level resistance)
- Economic pressure (organized boycotts, labor action)

**No Kings III is the test of whether the movement has learned this lesson.** If 9 million march Saturday and go home Sunday, it's another data point. If 9 million march Saturday and the energy converts into sustained action — strikes, occupations, daily pressure — that's different.

The Women's March (2017) was bigger at the time than anything before it. It also evaporated within weeks. But the *infrastructure* it built led to the 2018 blue wave that flipped the House. The march itself "failed." The movement it spawned succeeded.

That's the model. **The question isn't whether March 28 changes things. It's whether November 2026 does.**

[Sources: Progressive.org](https://progressive.org/latest/what-the-no-kings-protests-accomplished-karn-20251021/), [Waging Nonviolence](https://wagingnonviolence.org/2025/10/whats-next-after-the-historic-no-kings-protest/), [Center for American Progress](https://www.americanprogress.org/article/americans-continue-to-build-a-peaceful-mass-movement-to-force-trump-administration-changes/), [The Hill](https://thehill.com/opinion/white-house/5361267-america-resists-trump-kings/)

---

## SO WHAT'S THE REAL ANSWER? — The Honest Take

You're asking the right question and there isn't a clean answer. But here's my best attempt at one.

---

### THE HISTORICAL PARALLEL THAT MATTERS

**The Women's March (January 2017) → Blue Wave (November 2018)**

An academic study by Jonathan Pinckney (published in *Social Forces*, Oxford) actually **proved the causal link** using county-level data. He found:

- Counties with larger Women's Marches had **higher Democratic vote share in 2018** — and this held even after controlling for pre-existing political leanings
- Larger marches → more Indivisible groups formed locally → more sustained organizing → more donations → more votes
- The same people who marched went home and attended town halls, lobbied officials, registered voters, knocked on doors
- Result: largest number of women ever elected to Congress, House flipped

**The march itself "failed."** Trump didn't resign. No policies changed. He mocked it. But the **infrastructure it built** flipped the House 22 months later.

[Sources: Oxford Academic / Social Forces](https://academic.oup.com/sf/advance-article-abstract/doi/10.1093/sf/soaf083/8171324), [ResearchGate — Fisher, "American Resistance"](https://www.researchgate.net/publication/344942920_American_Resistance_From_the_Women's_March_to_the_Blue_Wave)

---

### THE NO KINGS TRAJECTORY

Here's why No Kings may be the Women's March on steroids:

| Factor | Women's March (2017) | No Kings (2025-2026) |
|--------|---------------------|---------------------|
| Single-day turnout | ~4.1M | **5M → 7M → 9M (growing)** |
| Number of events | 650 | **2,100 → 2,700 → 3,000+** |
| Repeat mobilizations | Mostly one-off (annual repeats were smaller) | **3 events in 10 months, each BIGGER than the last** |
| Geographic reach | Mostly coastal/urban/blue | **38% of all counties including Trump country** |
| Sustained org infrastructure | Indivisible formed | **Indivisible + 325 orgs + Eyes on ICE + 5,000 candidates** |
| External crisis | None (just Trump being Trump) | **Active war, $4 gas, TSA collapse, ICE killings, DHS shutdown** |
| Midterm enthusiasm at this stage | High but not extraordinary | **65%+ at 9-10/10 — 8 months early** |
| Movement brand vs. MAGA | N/A (no unified brand) | **No Kings 43% vs MAGA 30%** |

The Women's March was a spontaneous emotional reaction that accidentally built infrastructure. **No Kings is *deliberately* building infrastructure.** They know the midterm connection. The pivot to "local legislative advocacy and voter protection" is already planned.

---

### WHAT MARCH 28 WILL ACTUALLY ACCOMPLISH

**Honestly? On March 29, the world will look mostly the same.** The war will continue. Gas will still be expensive. TSA workers still won't be paid. Trump will call it a joke.

But:

1. **It registers the number.** If 9M+ march, that's a data point every Republican running in a swing district has to reckon with. Not "those people in San Francisco." People in *their* district.

2. **It grows the local nodes.** Every event in every small town creates a local organizing structure that persists. Those structures become midterm GOTV operations.

3. **It recruits.** 5,000+ progressive candidates have already signed up through Run for Something. March 28 will add more.

4. **It maintains the pressure that created the DHS shutdown.** If turnout drops, Democrats lose the political cover for holding firm on body cameras and officer IDs.

5. **It tests the 3.5% threshold.** If it hits 11.7M, we're in uncharted territory. If it doesn't, we know the ceiling under current conditions.

---

### WHAT COMES NEXT — THE REAL GAME

You're right that there will probably be more No Kings events. The pattern:

| Event | Date | Context |
|-------|------|---------|
| No Kings I | June 14, 2025 | Army parade + Trump's birthday |
| No Kings II | October 18, 2025 | Pre-shutdown, building pressure |
| **No Kings III** | **March 28, 2026** | **War + ICE killings + DHS shutdown** |
| No Kings IV (likely) | **~June-July 2026?** | Post-primary season, pre-general campaign |
| No Kings V (likely) | **~October 2026?** | Final midterm push — "March on the Polls" |

The October event would be the one that matters most electorally — the Women's March equivalent of the final push before the vote.

**Movement Voter Project's explicit strategy:** Fund year-round local organizing in key districts → flip the House in November 2026 → build toward Democratic governing trifecta in 2028.

[Source: Movement Voter Project](https://movement.vote/blog/2025-06-23-how-do-we-stop-trump-flip-the-house-in-2026-heres-the-plan/), [Swing Left](https://swingleft.org/house)

---

### THE THREE POSSIBLE ARCS FOR 2026

**Arc 1: The 2018 Replay (45% probability)**
No Kings builds infrastructure → sustained organizing through summer → massive midterm turnout → Democrats flip the House → Trump faces investigations, subpoenas, potential impeachment proceedings → his second term becomes a lame duck.

**This is the "it works" scenario.** It's also the most historically grounded — it's exactly what happened with Women's March → 2018. The difference is the crisis conditions (war, gas, ICE killings) make the organizing energy much stronger.

If Democrats flip the House:
- Subpoena power over the war, ICE killings, DOGE fraud
- Ability to block Trump's budget
- Potential impeachment proceedings
- Trump becomes a caged animal — dangerous but constrained

**Arc 2: The Exhaustion Trap (35% probability)**
Protest fatigue sets in over the summer. The war either ends or becomes background noise. Gas prices stabilize or people adjust. Trump's approval recovers to mid-40s. Democrats gain seats but fall short of flipping the House. 2027-2028 becomes the real fight.

**This is the "close but not enough" scenario.** The protests weren't useless — they built infrastructure and shifted numbers — but the midterm falls short because the crisis energy dissipates before November.

**Arc 3: The Escalation Spiral (20% probability)**
Something breaks. Ground invasion of Iran. Major domestic confrontation at a protest. Another ICE killing caught on camera. General strike. The crisis intensifies rather than normalizes. Turnout in November is historic — 2026 becomes the highest-turnout midterm in American history. Democrats win big. But the country is deeply, fundamentally destabilized.

**This is the "it works but at enormous cost" scenario.** The movement succeeds electorally but the country is traumatized.

---

### THE DANIEL QUESTION — SO WHAT DO I DO?

You're not asking this academically. You're asking because you have a family and you're trying to decide whether to stay and fight or go to Canada.

Here's my honest framework:

**The protests matter AND long-term preparation is still smart.**

These aren't contradictory. They're complementary.

- **Go to Jersey City on March 28.** Be part of the number. Show your kids what participation looks like.
- **Start your background check when ready.** Not leaving in 2026, but background checks take time and having it done removes a future bottleneck.
- **Prepare the Express Entry paperwork at your own pace.** Because even if Democrats flip the House in November, Trump still has executive power, still controls ICE, still controls the military. A flipped House constrains him — it doesn't remove him.
- **Keep your passports moving.** Still need valid documents regardless of timeline.

The protests are building something real. The midterm is the prize. But the midterm is 8 months away, and the prize is "partial constraint on a president with war powers and ICE agents," not "everything is fine now."

**The right answer to your question is: it's both.** It's not nothing. It's building something. But what it's building is an 8-month project with uncertain odds. You're not leaving this year — that's fine, and it gives you time to see how the midterms play out before making bigger decisions.

March. Vote. Organize. AND have the Canadian application ready to go.
