## TRUMP DECLARES DEMOCRATS "AMERICA'S GREATEST ENEMY" — March 22, 2026

### What He Said

On Sunday, March 22, Trump posted on Truth Social:

> **"Now with the death of Iran, the greatest enemy America has is the Radical Left, Highly Incompetent, Democrat Party!"**

This came the same day he:
- Issued a 48-hour ultimatum to Iran to open the Strait of Hormuz "or we hit and obliterate their power plants"
- Announced ICE agents would be deployed to airports starting Monday (March 23)
- Attacked Texas Democrats James Talarico ("worst candidate I have ever seen") and Jasmine Crockett (claimed she had a "low IQ")
- Attacked Gavin Newsom

[Source: Washington Times](https://www.washingtontimes.com/news/2026/mar/22/trump-calls-democrats-greatest-enemy-america/), [Jerusalem Post](https://www.jpost.com/american-politics/article-890823), [Yahoo News](https://www.yahoo.com/news/articles/trump-calls-democrats-greatest-enemy-164428100.html)

---

### Why This Is Different From His Usual Rhetoric

Trump has called Democrats "the enemy within" before. He's called them "vermin." He's called them "fascists." But this statement is structurally different for three reasons:

1. **He ranked them.** He didn't just call Democrats an enemy — he called them THE greatest enemy, explicitly placing them above Iran, a country he is currently *bombing*. He's spending $1B/day on Operation Epic Fury, has 13 KIA, thousands of Iranian casualties, the Strait of Hormuz closed, oil at $114 — and he says the *Democrats* are the bigger threat.

2. **The timing is 5 days before No Kings III.** This isn't random rhetoric. 9 million people are about to take to the streets on March 28. He's pre-framing them as enemies of America. When 9 million "greatest enemies" are in the streets and the National Guard is deployed in Texas, Virginia, and elsewhere — that language matters.

3. **It came with action.** The same day: ICE to airports. National Guard mobilizing. FCC threatening broadcasters' licenses over Iran war coverage. This isn't just talk — it's talk *backed by enforcement apparatus*.

4. **He said this while requesting $200B more for the Iran war.** He declared "Iran is dead" in one post and is asking Congress for $200 billion to keep fighting them in the next. The contradiction is the point — Iran is "dead" so the war machine can pivot to the domestic "enemy."

---

### How People Are Responding

#### Democratic Leadership

**Hakeem Jeffries (House Minority Leader)** — the sharpest response:

> **"Donald Trump should keep his reckless mouth shut before he gets somebody killed."**

On CNN's *State of the Union*, Jeffries went further:
- "They have got no vision, no plan, no exit strategy"
- "They clearly didn't anticipate some of the things that have happened, including the closure of the Strait of Hormuz"
- Gas prices are "through the roof" adding to "an environment in America right now where life has already become too expensive for the American people because of failed policies by Donald Trump"

This is the most aggressive language Jeffries has used. "Keep his reckless mouth shut before he gets somebody killed" is not normal Minority Leader language. It signals that even cautious Democratic leadership recognizes this rhetoric is materially dangerous.

[Source: Jeffries Official Statement](https://jeffries.house.gov/2026/03/22/leader-jeffries-on-cnn-donald-trump-should-keep-his-reckless-mouth-shut-before-he-gets-somebody-killed/), [CNN](https://www.cnn.com/2026/03/22/politics/video/minority-leader-hakeem-jeffries-democratic-party-iran-war-trump-admin), [Fox News](https://www.foxnews.com/media/jeffries-tells-trump-keep-his-reckless-mouth-shut-after-president-calls-democratic-party-greatest-enemy)

#### The Threat Data That Makes This Real

Capitol Police released their 2025 threat data in January 2026. The numbers are staggering:

| Year | Threat Assessment Cases | Change |
|------|------------------------|--------|
| 2017 | ~4,000 | — |
| 2020 | ~8,600 | +115% |
| 2022 | 7,501 | — |
| 2023 | 8,008 | +7% |
| 2024 | 9,474 | +18% |
| **2025** | **14,938** | **+58%** |

**Nearly 15,000 threats against members of Congress in 2025.** That's a 58% spike in one year — the largest single-year increase ever recorded.

Key findings:
- **Threats jumped 600%** during Trump's first term vs. Obama's second term (148 criminally charged cases vs. 21) — per University of Chicago CPOST study
- After Trump posted "SEDITIOUS BEHAVIOR, punishable by DEATH!" targeting Democratic veterans in Congress, **Sen. Elissa Slotkin reported receiving close to 1,000 threats**
- NBC News tallied **at least 22 officials** on both sides receiving threat surges linked to specific Trump posts
- **Rep. Ilhan Omar sprayed with unknown substance** from a syringe at a town hall
- **Rep. Maxwell Frost punched in the face** at Sundance
- Capitol Police themselves said: **"Decreasing violent political rhetoric is one of the best ways to decrease the number of threats across the country"** — as close to naming Trump as they can get

[Sources: NBC News](https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/congress/threats-congress-spiked-2025-rose-third-year-row-capitol-police-say-rcna256259), [Axios](https://www.axios.com/2026/01/28/threats-congress-capitol-police-omar-frost), [Capitol Police](https://www.uscp.gov/media-center/press-releases/uscp-threat-assessment-cases-2025), [NBC Trump/threats investigation](https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/donald-trump/trump-attacks-political-opponents-spur-surge-threats-nbc-news-review-f-rcna247201)

#### The Free Speech Crackdown — Al Jazeera Report (March 23)

Trump's rhetoric isn't just aimed at Democrats. He's actively pressuring the media to fall in line on the Iran war:

- **FCC Chairman Brendan Carr** warned broadcasters they risk losing licenses if they "perpetrate fake news" about the Iran war
- **Senator Brian Schatz (D-HI):** "This is a clear directive to provide positive war coverage or else licenses may not be renewed"
- **Reporters Without Borders USA (Clayton Weimers):** "The second Trump administration has really been characterised by concrete actions to threaten or intimidate or control or weaken the media"
- **Defense Secretary Pete Hegseth** called for "patriotic" reporters to write more optimistic headlines about the war
- Media companies are complying: After Paramount and Warner Bros Discovery acquisitions, owners are pressuring staff to avoid being "overly adversarial"
- **Meta and Apple** are complying with administration subpoenas for personal data of social media accounts that expose ICE operations

[Source: Al Jazeera](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/23/threats-over-iran-war-bare-trump-efforts-to-transform-free-speech-experts), [Al Jazeera — press threats](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/14/trump-administration-threatens-news-outlets-over-critical-coverage-of-iran)

#### The No Kings Coalition Response

The No Kings coalition responded directly, framing it as fuel:

- **ACLU's Deirdre Schifeling:** Called it "unprecedented mobilization" against "President Trump's violent, inhumane treatment of our immigrant neighbors, attacks on our freedom of speech and voting rights, and the weaponization of the federal government"
- **Robert De Niro** (March 22): Compared Trump to "mad" King George III, told Americans to join March 28 protests, then "continue showing support and presence," then "vote in the November election"
- **Bernie Sanders** confirmed as headliner at the Twin Cities flagship rally
- **3,000+ events** now confirmed — up from 2,700 in October
- Organizers explicitly targeting **9 million** turnout

[Sources: Truthout](https://truthout.org/articles/no-kings-protests-set-to-sweep-us-even-as-trump-increases-attacks-on-activists/), [Common Dreams](https://www.commondreams.org/news/no-kings-2026), [Time](https://time.com/7358310/no-kings-protests-march-28-anti-trump-ice/), [Breitbart (De Niro)](https://www.breitbart.com/entertainment/2026/03/22/video-robert-de-niro-pushes-no-kings-leftists-to-take-to-the-streets-against-mentally-ill-tyrant-trump/)

---

### MY ANALYSIS: What's Actually Happening Here

Here's what I think you're really asking: **Is a sitting president designating ~half the country as "the greatest enemy" a line-crossing moment?**

**Yes. But not for the reason you might think.**

The line isn't the language itself — he's called Democrats enemies before. The line is the **operational context** around it:

**What "greatest enemy" looks like when you have the enforcement tools:**

| Tool | Status | Aimed at... |
|------|--------|-------------|
| ICE agents at airports | Deployed March 23 | Travelers, but also a show of force |
| National Guard | Abbott & Youngkin deployed for NK1 & NK2; no NK3 announcement yet but expected | Protesters labeled "antifa-linked" |
| FCC license threats | Active, March 14+ | Media covering the war critically |
| "Antifa" executive order | Active since Sept 2025 | Anyone the admin labels "antifa" |
| Social media subpoenas | Active via Meta, Apple | People exposing ICE operations |
| Capitol Police threats up 58% | 14,938 cases in 2025 | Members of Congress |
| DHS shutdown, no oversight | Day 37 | ICE operating without body cameras |
| Mario Guevara deportation | Happened | Journalist who livestreamed No Kings |

**The pattern:** Call them the enemy → deploy enforcement → pressure media silence → punish dissent.

This is what scholars of authoritarianism call **"defining the in-group and out-group."** When the president says Democrats are "the greatest enemy" and then deploys ICE to airports the same day, deploys National Guard for the protest 5 days later, and threatens broadcaster licenses — the rhetoric IS the policy. The words aren't separate from the actions.

**The convergence point is March 28-29:**
- March 28: 9M people in the streets, labeled "the greatest enemy"
- March 28: National Guard deployed in multiple states
- March 29: Trump's 48-hour Iran Hormuz ultimatum expires
- Late March: USS Tripoli + 5,000 Marines arriving in the Gulf

A president who just called half the country his greatest enemy, with the National Guard in the streets, while his Iran deadline expires and Marines arrive — that's the most volatile 48 hours of this administration.

**How people are responding: They're coming anyway.** The 3,000+ events, the 9M target, De Niro's video, Sanders headlining, the Never Trumper $1M ad campaign — the "greatest enemy" language isn't suppressing turnout. If anything, it's accelerating it. The No Kings coalition has explicitly adopted the framing: *"America has No Kings and the power belongs to the people."*

The question isn't whether people are scared. It's whether being labeled "the greatest enemy" by a president with ICE, the National Guard, and FCC license threats makes them more scared or more angry.

Right now? **More angry.**

The 43% support vs. 30% MAGA numbers haven't moved. The midterm enthusiasm is at 65%+ reporting 9-10/10 intensity. The Capitol Police threat data shows the danger is real. But the turnout data shows people are showing up despite it.

That's historically what happens. The Women's March happened BECAUSE of Trump. No Kings is happening BECAUSE of "greatest enemy." The authoritarianism IS the recruitment tool.

The risk isn't that people don't show up. The risk is what happens when 9 million "greatest enemies" are in the streets and a cornered president whose Iran deadline just expired needs a distraction.

---

## HAVE WE HIT THE 3.5% THRESHOLD? — Honest Assessment (March 23, 2026)

### The Numbers

The Chenoweth 3.5% rule says: no nonviolent movement that sustained 3.5% of the population at a peak event has ever failed to force change. In the US, that's **~11.7 million people** on a single day.

Here's where we actually are:

| Event | Date | Organizer Estimate | Independent Estimate (Morris/Xylom) | % of US Pop |
|-------|------|-------------------|--------------------------------------|-------------|
| Hands Off | April 2025 | 3M | Not independently verified | ~0.9% |
| **No Kings I** | June 14, 2025 | 5M | **4-6M** (Crowd Counting Consortium: 2-4.8M) | **1.2-1.8%** |
| **No Kings II** | Oct 18, 2025 | 7M | **5.0-6.5M** (Morris/Xylom) | **1.5-1.9%** |
| **No Kings III** | March 28, 2026 | Target: 9M | TBD | Target: ~2.7% |

**Cumulative participation** (all anti-Trump protests since inauguration): Strength In Numbers estimates **12.8 million people, or 3.7% of the population**, have demonstrated at least once as of October 2025.

[Source: Maddow Blog/MSNBC](https://www.ms.now/rachel-maddow-show/maddowblog/no-kings-protests-trump-successful-anti-authoritarian-movements-rcna238949), [G. Elliott Morris](https://www.gelliottmorris.com/p/second-no-kings-day-protests-likely), [Center for American Progress](https://www.americanprogress.org/article/how-peaceful-protest-by-just-3-5-percent-of-americans-could-force-major-policy-changes-from-the-trump-administration/)

---

### The Honest Answer: Sort Of — But It's Complicated

**Cumulatively? Yes.** 12.8 million people (3.7%) have protested at least once since January 2025. That's past the threshold. Maddow ran a whole segment on this in October: *"Does 12 million really seem so far away?"*

**On a single peak day? No. Not yet.**

The 3.5% rule is about a **single peak event**, not cumulative participation. The biggest single day was NK2 at 5-6.5M — that's roughly **1.5-1.9%**. Important, historic, unprecedented for the US. But it's still about half the threshold.

**To hit 3.5% on March 28, they need ~11.7 million.** The organizers are targeting 9M. Even if they hit that (which would be extraordinary), it's 2.7% — still short.

---

### Why This Is More Nuanced Than "Did We Hit the Number"

Here's what Chenoweth herself has said — and it's more cautious than the Twitter version of her research:

**1. The 3.5% figure is descriptive, not prescriptive.**

From her Harvard Kennedy School paper: *"The 3.5% participation metric may be useful as a rule of thumb; however, other factors — momentum, organization, strategic leadership, and sustainability — are likely as important as large-scale participation."*

She's saying: the number matters, but it's not magic. A disorganized 12 million accomplishes less than an organized 7 million with a plan.

**2. The rule was about toppling authoritarian regimes, not reforming democracies.**

This is the criticism from the *Deseret News* and from political scientist Kyle Matthews: Chenoweth's dataset is movements like the Philippines' People Power, Serbia's Otpor, the Arab Spring. These were campaigns to **remove governments entirely**. The US situation is different — you're trying to constrain an elected president within existing institutions (courts, Congress, midterms). The mechanism is different.

**3. Chenoweth herself says movements are getting less effective.**

From her cautionary update: authoritarian governments are doing a better job at *"controlling information flow, criminalizing protest, hardening security and police forces, and coordinating with other authoritarians."* She says resistance movements need to become *"more creative"* as they adapt.

Sound familiar? FCC threatening broadcaster licenses. DOJ threatening RICO charges against Indivisible. Meta handing over user data. ICE deporting a journalist who livestreamed No Kings. Trump declaring protesters "the greatest enemy."

**4. Two movements HAVE failed after hitting 3.5%.**

Brunei in 1962 (4% mobilized — crushed). Bahrain in 2011 (6% mobilized — crushed with Saudi military intervention). Both involved monarchs with heavy foreign backing and small populations. Not a perfect parallel to the US — but it means 3.5% isn't a guarantee.

---

### So Where Does That Actually Leave Us?

Here's my framework:

| Factor | Status | Assessment |
|--------|--------|------------|
| **Single-day peak participation** | ~5-6.5M (NK2). Target 9M for NK3 | ❌ Below 3.5% threshold (need 11.7M) |
| **Cumulative participation** | 12.8M / 3.7% as of Oct 2025 | ✅ Past threshold |
| **Trajectory** | 3M → 5M → 6.5M → 9M target. Accelerating. | 🟢 Right direction |
| **Geographic reach** | 38% of counties, including Trump counties | ✅ Exceeds historical benchmarks |
| **Organizational infrastructure** | 325+ coalition orgs, 3,000+ events, Eyes on ICE, de-escalation training | ✅ Strong and getting stronger |
| **Momentum / sustained pressure** | 4 major mobilizations in 12 months, strikes, ongoing local actions | ✅ Sustained, not one-off |
| **Strategic clarity** | Pivoting to midterm voter registration/protection after March 28 | ✅ Has an electoral theory of change |
| **Government counter-pressure** | RICO threats, journalist deportation, FCC threats, ICE surveillance, "greatest enemy" rhetoric | 🔴 Escalating — Chenoweth's warning about states getting better at suppression |
| **Elite defection** | Joe Kent resigned. Never Trumper $1M ad campaign. Some MAGA cracks. | 🟡 Early but not decisive |
| **V-Dem democracy score** | US officially lost "liberal democracy" status in 2026 V-Dem report | 🔴 The thing you're fighting against is real |

**The bottom line:**

The movement has NOT hit the 3.5% single-day threshold. NK3 probably won't either — even 9M would be 2.7%. But here's the thing Chenoweth's popularized rule misses: **83% of successful nonviolent campaigns never hit 3.5% either.** They succeeded through sustained pressure, strategic targeting, and elite defection — not just raw numbers.

What the No Kings movement HAS done:
- Built the largest sustained protest infrastructure in US history
- Maintained momentum across 4 mobilizations in 12 months (most movements peak at 1-2)
- Reached into 38% of counties including Trump territory
- Created the conditions for a midterm wave (the actual mechanism of change in a democracy)
- Cratered Trump's approval to 37%
- Flipped the support numbers (43% No Kings vs. 30% MAGA)
- Started cracking MAGA from the inside (Kent, the war opposition, the Kirk conspiracy)

What it has NOT done:
- Changed any Trump policy
- Stopped any war
- Stopped ICE raids
- Saved DHS funding
- Protected a single fired federal worker's job
- Hit 3.5% on a single day

**The uncomfortable truth:** In Chenoweth's framework, the movement is on the right trajectory but hasn't hit the number. In practical terms, the movement isn't going to "topple" Trump — that's not how the US works. What it CAN do is **flip the House in November 2026**, and the organizational infrastructure, voter enthusiasm, and approval collapse are all tracking toward that.

But flipping the House is 8 months away. And between now and then, Trump has ICE, the military, executive orders, and the word "enemy" aimed at half the country. The 3.5% question is almost academic — the real question is whether the movement translates to **votes in November** the way the Women's March translated to the 2018 Blue Wave.

The data says it can. The Oxford/Social Forces study showed Women's March → 2018 was causal, not coincidental. No Kings is bigger, more organized, and more sustained than the Women's March was.

But "can" isn't "will." And 8 months is a long time when your president is calling you the greatest enemy while bombing 7 countries.

[Sources: Harvard Kennedy School/Chenoweth](https://www.hks.harvard.edu/centers/carr/publications/questions-answers-and-some-cautionary-updates-regarding-35-rule), [American Bar Association](https://www.americanbar.org/groups/crsj/resources/human-rights/2025-october/defeating-tyranny/), [Deseret News](https://www.deseret.com/opinion/2025/10/22/no-kings-protests-numbers-jesse-watters-gayle-king/), [MSNBC/Maddow](https://www.ms.now/rachel-maddow-show/maddowblog/no-kings-protests-trump-successful-anti-authoritarian-movements-rcna238949), [Center for American Progress](https://www.americanprogress.org/article/americans-continue-to-build-a-peaceful-mass-movement-to-force-trump-administration-changes/), [V-Dem Institute](https://www.v-dem.net/), [Wikipedia — 3.5% rule](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/3.5%25_rule)

---

### BUT IS THE DIRECTION RIGHT? (The Real Question)

Forget the 3.5% number. The question is: **is the resistance going the correct direction?**

**Yes.** Here's the evidence:

**1. The growth curve is accelerating, not flattening.**
- 3M → 5M → 6.5M → 9M target, over 12 months
- Events: 2,100 → 2,700 → 3,000+
- Most protest movements peak at event 1 or 2 and decline. This one is still growing at event 4. That's the anomaly that matters more than any threshold.

**2. Geographic spread into hostile territory.**
- 38% of counties including Trump counties
- No Kings events in Lewisburg WV, Edmonds WA, Central Michigan, Corvallis OR, Ridgefield CT
- When the movement reaches 60%+ Trump counties, it's past the "just blue cities" phase

**3. The approval numbers moved and stayed moved.**
- Trump: 47% (inauguration) → 37% (current). No bounce-back from Iran war "rally around the flag."
- No Kings support: 43% vs MAGA 30%. A year ago these were reversed.
- When more people support the protest movement than the president's movement, that's not fringe — that's mainstream.

**4. Midterm enthusiasm is historic.**
- 65%+ of likely voters at 9-10/10 intensity for November 2026
- Women's March had similar numbers → produced the 2018 Blue Wave
- The Oxford/Social Forces study showed that link was causal, not coincidental

**5. Elite defection has started.**
- Joe Kent resigned, went on Tucker, said Israel drove Iran decision and intelligence didn't support it
- Never Trumper $1M ad campaign in 300 newspapers across 31 states
- MAGA coalition showing cracks over the war — the Kent/Tucker interview is the biggest internal challenge yet

**6. The infrastructure is organizational, not just emotional.**
- 325+ coalition organizations
- Eyes on ICE: 200,000+ trained
- De-escalation training at every event
- Legal observer networks
- Voter registration built into every event — the explicit pivot after March 28
- Interfaith gatherings before every NK3 event

**7. V-Dem officially downgraded the US** from liberal democracy, moving toward dictatorship faster than Hungary or Turkey. Academic validation creates permission for more people to join.

**What's NOT working yet:**
- Zero policy reversals from protests alone
- The mechanism (midterms) is 8 months away
- Counter-pressure is escalating: RICO threats, journalist deportation, FCC threats, "greatest enemy" rhetoric
- Sustained participation vs. peak attendance is unknown — how many march twice? How many knock doors?

**Bottom line:** The direction is right. The trajectory matches or exceeds the Women's March → 2018 Blue Wave timeline at every comparable stage. It's bigger, more organized, more geographically spread, and more sustained. The risk isn't that the direction is wrong — it's whether the country can survive the 8 months between now and when this direction actually produces power.

---

## THE FULL RESISTANCE PICTURE — Not Just No Kings (March 23, 2026)

No Kings is the most visible piece. But the resistance is a multi-front ecosystem. Here's every front, whether it's working, and the honest trajectory assessment.

---

### FRONT 1: THE COURTS

**This is the front that's actually winning.**

| Metric | Number | Source |
|--------|--------|--------|
| Total lawsuits filed against Trump admin | **358+** (through Dec 2025) | Just Security |
| **Plaintiff wins** | **232** | Just Security Tracker |
| Government wins | 113 | Just Security Tracker |
| Cases still pending | 304 | Just Security Tracker |
| **Win rate for plaintiffs** | **67%** | Just Security |
| ACLU legal actions in 2025 | 230+ | ACLU |
| ACLU success rate | **64%** delayed, diluted, or defeated | ACLU |
| State AG lawsuits filed | 80+ (22 states + DC) | Progressive State Leaders |
| **State AG win rate** | **43 of 53 resolved (81%)** | Progressive State Leaders |
| State laws passed via ACLU Firewall | 51 state laws, 80+ total policies | ACLU |

**Key wins:**
- Federal funding freeze **blocked** (First Circuit upheld)
- Sanctuary city funding cuts **blocked** — court protected 50 jurisdictions covering 30M+ residents
- Mass probationary employee firings **blocked** — Judge Alsup ordered reinstatement
- All 4 law firm executive orders **struck down** as unconstitutional
- National Guard deployment without governor consent **blocked** (SCOTUS, 6-3, Dec 2025)
- Michigan AG recovered **$2 billion** in federal funding through lawsuits alone
- Maryland recovered **$100M education + $50M medical research** funding

**The problem:** The Supreme Court keeps intervening for the administration. Stayed the probationary employee reinstatement order. 17 stays or vacations of lower court orders. The lower courts are a wall; SCOTUS is a door.

**Trajectory: ✅ Right direction.** The courts are the most effective check right now. 67% plaintiff win rate is extraordinary. But SCOTUS is the ceiling.

[Sources: Just Security Tracker](https://www.justsecurity.org/107087/tracker-litigation-legal-challenges-trump-administration/), [ACLU](https://www.aclu.org/campaigns-initiatives/aclu-vs-trump), [Lawfare Tracker](https://www.lawfaremedia.org/projects-series/trials-of-the-trump-administration/tracking-trump-administration-litigation), [Michigan Public](https://www.michiganpublic.org/criminal-justice-legal-system/2026-01-22/nessel-says-lawsuits-against-trump-administration-brought-2-billion-back-to-michigan)

---

### FRONT 2: STATE-LEVEL RESISTANCE

**The "blue wall" is holding and expanding.**

- **22 Democratic AGs + DC** running coordinated legal strategy — this is the most organized AG resistance in US history
- **Governors refusing cooperation:** Newsom (CA), Pritzker (IL), Hochul (NY): "You touch any more money from New York, we'll see you in court"
- **Sanctuary protections holding:** Courts blocked sanctuary funding cuts protecting 50 jurisdictions / 30M+ residents
- **State legislation:** 51 state laws passed pushing back against Trump agenda (ACLU Firewall for Freedom)
- **83% of anti-immigrant state bills blocked** at state level (from earlier research)
- **AG races now attracting record money** — $29M Republican, $28M Democratic (2x normal) for 2026

**Trajectory: ✅ Right direction.** States are the actual functioning check on executive power right now, more than Congress. The 81% AG win rate is the single most effective resistance vector.

[Sources: Stateline](https://stateline.org/2026/01/07/democratic-state-ags-will-lead-opposition-to-trump-in-new-year/), [Ballotpedia](https://ballotpedia.org/Multistate_lawsuits_against_the_federal_government_during_the_Trump_administration,_2025-2026), [NPR](https://www.npr.org/2026/01/17/nx-s1-5679562/trump-sanctuary-cities-ice-immigration)

---

### FRONT 3: ELECTIONS — THE LEADING INDICATORS

**This is where the data is most encouraging.**

| Indicator | Number | What It Means |
|-----------|--------|---------------|
| **Generic ballot** | **D+3 to D+3.9** (Morning Consult / Brookings) | 6.5-point swing from 2024's R+2.6 |
| **Special election overperformance** | **D+13 to D+15** vs. 2024 presidential margins | Massive — 2017 was D+9 before the Blue Wave |
| **GOP seats flipped in 2025** | **25 state seats** (21% of contested GOP seats) | Dems flipped seats in TX, LA, MS, IA — deep red |
| **Texas Senate flip** | Taylor Rehmet won a seat held by GOP for **30+ years** | Fort Worth area. This is not a blue bubble. |
| **Louisiana flip** | Chasity Verret Martinez won 62% in a Trump+13 district | |
| **Seats needed for House majority** | **3** | Democrats need to flip just 3 seats |
| **Battleground House seats** | 42 (20 R, 22 D) | Cook/Ballotpedia |
| **Senate seats up** | 35 (22 R, 13 D) — Dems need net +4 for majority | Steep but 22 R seats is the most R exposure since 2008 |
| **Trump approval with Hispanics** | **28%** | Morning Consult — was 46% on election day |
| **Trump approval with 18-29** | **29%** | Collapsed from ~40% |
| **Trump approval with independents** | **28%** | This is the ballgame for midterms |

**The comparison that matters:** In 2017, Democrats overperformed in special elections by D+9. That produced a **40-seat House gain** in 2018. Right now Democrats are overperforming by D+13 to D+15. If that holds, and they only need 3 seats...

**Trajectory: ✅ Strongly right direction.** Every electoral leading indicator is better than 2017-2018. The special election data is the hardest evidence — actual votes, not polls. Dems are flipping seats in Trump+13 districts. In Texas. In Louisiana. In Mississippi.

[Sources: Morning Consult](https://pro.morningconsult.com/trackers/2026-midterm-election-generic-ballot-polls), [Brookings](https://www.brookings.edu/articles/what-history-tells-us-about-the-2026-midterm-elections/), [Bolts](https://boltsmag.org/legislative-elections-results-2025/), [The Conversation](https://theconversation.com/do-special-election-results-spell-doom-for-republicans-in-2026-274912), [Newsweek](https://www.newsweek.com/list-of-democrats-double-digit-overperformances-in-2025-elections-11266946)

---

### FRONT 4: LABOR

**The sleeping giant woke up.**

- **Minneapolis AFL-CIO called a general strike** — January 23, 2026. First AFL-CIO general strike call in 75 years.
- Endorsed by SEIU Local 26, UNITE HERE Local 17, CWA Local 7250, multiple educators' locals, Minneapolis Regional Labor Federation
- **National strike followed January 30** — AFL-CIO, Indivisible, 50501 coordinated
- SEIU **ended its two-decade challenge** to AFL-CIO and merged resistance efforts — labor is unified for the first time in a generation
- AFL-CIO: "In 2026 we will organize, we will fight and we will vote"
- Union membership at **highest level in 16 years**
- Labor is fully embedded in No Kings coalition — not separate, integrated

**The problem:** Trump's anti-union EOs stripping 2/3 of federal workforce of bargaining rights — appeals court declined to block. NLRB still doesn't have full Republican quorum to reverse Biden-era precedents, which is actually helpful for now.

**Trajectory: ✅ Right direction.** A general strike call from the AFL-CIO is historic. Labor unity is historic. Union membership at 16-year highs is real. The question is whether labor translates to sustained political power or burns out.

[Sources: Labor Notes](https://labornotes.org/2026/01/will-ice-ignite-mass-strike-minnesota), [Jacobin](https://jacobin.com/2026/01/ice-minneapolis-general-strike-history), [AFL-CIO](https://aflcio.org/)

---

### FRONT 5: CIVIL SOCIETY / ORGANIZATIONAL INFRASTRUCTURE

- **ACLU:** $79M in new contributions since election. Average donation $79. Spending $40M+ to build state offices in all 50 states. 230+ legal actions. 64% success rate.
- **Indivisible:** Core organizer of No Kings. 3,000+ events. Eyes on ICE training (200K+ viewers). Voter registration pipeline built into every protest.
- **325+ coalition organizations** in the No Kings ecosystem
- **50501 Movement** — organizing in all 501 congressional districts (including non-voting)
- **Interfaith Alliance** — pre-protest gatherings before every NK3 event
- **DLCC** — won majority-deciding special elections in 5 state chambers

**Trajectory: ✅ Right direction.** The organizational infrastructure is deeper and wider than anything in 2017. The ACLU alone is bigger, richer, and more aggressive than during Trump's first term.

---

### FRONT 6: THE CRACKS INSIDE MAGA

This is early but real:

- **Joe Kent** resigned as Trump's intelligence official, went on Tucker for 121 minutes, said Israel drove the Iran war, intelligence didn't support it, insinuated Israel killed Charlie Kirk, FBI now investigating him
- **Tucker Carlson** is platforming anti-war MAGA dissent — his audience is 3-5M per episode
- **Never Trumper Republicans** — $1M ad campaign in 300 newspapers across 31 states supporting No Kings III (Home of the Brave, Bill Kristol on board)
- **74% of Americans oppose ground troops in Iran** — including significant MAGA voters
- **SCOTUS split 3-3 among conservatives** on National Guard case — Roberts, Kavanaugh, Barrett broke from Thomas, Alito, Gorsuch
- **SAVE Act dead** — can't get 60 votes. Even with unified government, Trump can't pass major legislation
- **DHS shutdown Day 37** — Republicans can't agree among themselves

**Trajectory: 🟡 Early.** These are cracks, not a break. Kent is one guy. The Never Trumpers are a niche. 74% opposing ground troops hasn't translated to Republican votes against the war. But the MAGA coalition has never faced a sustained foreign war with rising gas prices and body bags before. The Iran war is the variable that could accelerate the cracking.

---

### THE SCORECARD

| Front | Working? | Trajectory | Impact Level |
|-------|----------|------------|-------------|
| **Courts** | Yes — 67% win rate | ✅ Right direction | 🟢 High — actually blocking policy |
| **State resistance** | Yes — 81% AG win rate | ✅ Right direction | 🟢 High — protecting 30M+ residents |
| **Elections** | Yes — D+13-15 overperformance | ✅ Strongly right direction | 🟢 Highest — this is how it ends |
| **Labor** | Yes — first general strike in 75 years | ✅ Right direction | 🟡 Medium — power still building |
| **Civil society** | Yes — record funding, membership, organization | ✅ Right direction | 🟢 High — infrastructure for everything else |
| **Street protests (No Kings)** | Yes — still growing at event 4 | ✅ Right direction | 🟡 Medium — shifts opinion, doesn't change policy directly |
| **MAGA internal cracks** | Early — Kent, Tucker, Never Trumpers | 🟡 Too early to assess | 🟡 Low now, potentially high if war drags |

**The overall picture:**

Every front is moving in the right direction. That's not spin — it's what the data shows. Courts are blocking. States are holding. Special elections are flipping deep-red seats. Labor is unified for the first time in a generation. Civil society is better funded and organized than 2017. The protests are still growing.

**What's different from 2017:** In Trump's first term, the resistance was mostly reactive — marches, outrage, but disorganized. This time it's **coordinated across all six fronts simultaneously.** The ACLU is litigating while Indivisible is organizing while the AFL-CIO is striking while state AGs are suing while Democrats are winning special elections. That's not one thing working. That's an ecosystem.

**The honest caveat:** All of this is necessary but none of it is sufficient *until November 2026*. Courts can block but SCOTUS can unblock. States can resist but Trump can escalate. Protests can shift opinion but opinion doesn't constrain executive power. The only thing that actually changes the power structure is **flipping the House** (and ideally the Senate), and that's 8 months away.

But is the direction right? **Yes. On every front. Unambiguously.**

The question was never "is the resistance doing enough today." The question is "is the resistance building the thing that wins in November." And the answer, based on every leading indicator we have — special elections, generic ballot, approval collapse, organizational infrastructure, geographic spread — is yes.

---

## HOW DO YOU ACTUALLY OUST TRUMP AFTER MIDTERMS? — The Honest Math (March 23, 2026)

### The Three Constitutional Paths

| Path | Requirement | Who Decides | Realistic? |
|------|-------------|-------------|------------|
| **Impeachment + Removal** | House majority (impeach) → Senate 2/3 (convict) | 218 House + 67 Senate | The only real path |
| **25th Amendment** | VP + majority of Cabinet → if contested, 2/3 of BOTH chambers | Vance + Cabinet + 67 Senate + 290 House | Harder than impeachment. Dead on arrival. |
| **Resignation (Nixon model)** | Party leaders tell him it's over, he leaves | GOP leadership + Trump's ego | Requires the Nixon scenario |

**Let's be blunt about each one.**

---

### PATH 1: IMPEACHMENT — The Math

**Step 1: Impeach in the House (simple majority — 218 votes)**

If Democrats flip the House in November 2026 (they need +3 seats), they'd have the majority. They can impeach. Period.

But here's the thing: **impeachment already happened. Twice.** It didn't remove him either time. Impeachment without conviction is a press release.

There's already a resolution on the table — **H.Res.353**, introduced in the current Congress, with 7 articles including obstruction, abuse of appropriations power, abuse of trade powers, First Amendment violations, bribery/corruption, and "tyranny." It went nowhere in the Republican House. In a Democratic House, it passes on day one.

**Step 2: Convict in the Senate (67 votes)**

This is where it dies or doesn't. Here's the 2027 Senate math after the midterms:

**Best realistic Democratic scenario after November 2026:**

| Seats | Current (2026) | Best case after midterms |
|-------|---------------|-------------------------|
| Democrats + Independents | 47 | **51** (flip ME, NC, OH, IA) |
| Republicans | 53 | **49** |
| **Needed for conviction** | — | **67** |
| **GOP defections needed** | — | **16** |

Even in Democrats' absolute best-case Senate scenario — flipping Maine (Collins), North Carolina (open seat, Roy Cooper running), Ohio (Sherrod Brown running for special election), and Iowa — they'd get to maybe 51. They'd still need **16 Republican senators** to vote to convict.

For context: In Trump's second impeachment trial (Jan 2021, after the Capitol attack), only **7 Republicans** voted to convict. And that was after a literal insurrection that nearly got them killed. Sixteen is more than double that number.

[Sources: CNN](https://www.cnn.com/2026/01/20/politics/democrats-trump-identity-impeachment-2026), [NBC News](https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2026-election/trump-predicts-impeachment-if-republicans-lose-2026-midterms-rcna252604), [Congress.gov — H.Res.353](https://www.congress.gov/bill/119th-congress/house-resolution/353), [ABC News](https://abcnews.com/Politics/democrats-grapple-rising-clamor-trump-impeachment-ahead-midterms/story?id=129291674)

---

### PATH 2: 25TH AMENDMENT — Dead on Arrival

Requires VP Vance + majority of this Cabinet (Bondi, Hegseth, Noem, Rubio) to declare Trump unfit. Then if Trump contests it (he would), 2/3 of BOTH chambers must agree within 21 days. That's 67 senators AND 290 House members.

This is **harder** than impeachment. And it requires Vance to initiate it. The same Vance who called Trump "America's Hitler" in private and then became his VP. He's not doing this unless Trump is literally incapacitated.

Not a serious path.

---

### PATH 3: THE NIXON MODEL — What Would It Actually Take

Nixon wasn't impeached. He resigned on August 8, 1974, the day after Barry Goldwater, Hugh Scott, and John Rhodes — the three top Republican leaders — went to the White House and told him the votes weren't there to survive.

**What made Republicans break with Nixon:**

| Event | Date | Effect |
|-------|------|--------|
| Watergate break-in | June 1972 | Initial scandal, GOP rallied around Nixon |
| Senate hearings begin | May 1973 | Public erosion starts |
| Saturday Night Massacre | Oct 1973 | Nixon fires special prosecutor. First GOP calls for resignation |
| Approval hits 27% | Late 1973 | Stayed there for 9 months |
| **Special election losses** | 1973-1974 | **Democrats won 5 of 5 special elections in GOP districts — including Gerald Ford's old seat.** This is what convinced Republicans Nixon was an electoral anchor. |
| Supreme Court orders tapes | July 1974 | Unanimous ruling |
| "Smoking gun" tape released | Aug 5, 1974 | **This is the break.** Proved he'd been lying. All 10 GOP Judiciary Committee holdouts flipped to pro-impeachment overnight. |
| Goldwater delegation | Aug 7, 1974 | Told Nixon he had maybe 15 Senate votes. Not enough to survive. |
| **Resignation** | Aug 8, 1974 | |

**The key insight: It wasn't about morality. It was about electoral survival.**

Republicans didn't abandon Nixon because they suddenly grew a conscience. They abandoned him because:
1. His approval was at 27% and **stayed there**
2. They were losing special elections in safe Republican districts
3. The smoking gun tape made it impossible to defend him without looking like a fool
4. **1974 midterms were coming** and they could see the wipeout

Sound familiar? Because here's where we are:

| Nixon Parallel | Nixon (1973-74) | Trump (2025-26) |
|----------------|-----------------|-----------------|
| Approval floor | 27% | 37% (higher) |
| Special election losses | 5 for 5 in GOP districts | Dems flipping TX, LA, MS seats. D+13-15 overperformance. |
| Party unity on key vote | Crumbling | War Powers vote: only Rand Paul broke (Senate). Only Davidson + Massie (House). **Party holding.** |
| "Smoking gun" equivalent | Tape proving he lied about Watergate | ??? — doesn't exist yet |
| Electoral fear | 1974 midterms (they lost 49 House seats) | 2026 midterms (they fear the same) |

---

### SO WHAT WOULD ACTUALLY HAVE TO HAPPEN?

Here's my honest framework. For Trump to be ousted after the midterms, you'd need a **specific sequence** — not just bad polls, not just lost elections, but a convergence:

**CONDITION 1: Democrats flip the House (probability: ~65-70%)**

This is the most likely piece. D+13-15 special election overperformance, only need +3 seats, 42 competitive races, Trump at 37% approval / 28% with independents. Cook Political, Sabato, and 538 all have this as likely-to-lean-Democratic.

Without the House, nothing else matters. No impeachment, no investigations with subpoena power, no leverage.

**CONDITION 2: Democrats gain significant Senate seats (probability: ~35-40% for 50+, ~10-15% for 53+)**

The Senate map is harder. 22 Republican seats up (most exposure since 2008), but 20 of those are in states Trump won by double digits. Realistic pickups:
- **Maine** (Collins) — lean competitive
- **North Carolina** (open, Roy Cooper) — toss-up
- **Ohio** (special election, Sherrod Brown) — competitive
- **Iowa** — reach but possible in a wave
- **Alaska** (Peltola running) — dark horse

Democrats need net +4 for majority (defending GA, MI). Getting to 51 is possible. Getting to 53-54 is a stretch. Getting to 67 is impossible through elections alone.

**CONDITION 3: A "smoking gun" — something that makes defending Trump impossible (probability: ???)**

This is the piece nobody can predict. For Nixon, it was the tape. What would it be for Trump?

Possibilities:
- **Iran war catastrophe** — massive US casualties in a ground operation, evidence of fabricated intelligence (the Kent allegations), or a Hormuz disaster that craters the economy. If gas hits $7-8 and body bags are coming home daily, the war becomes Iraq 2006 — and Iraq 2006 cost Republicans the House AND the Senate.
- **Financial corruption proof** — something concrete and undeniable. Emoluments on steroids. A recording. Wire transfers. The kind of thing that makes Fox News anchors pause.
- **An order so extreme it breaks the military** — an attempt to invoke the Insurrection Act against protesters, or an order a general publicly refuses. The Milley scenario but public.
- **Health/cognitive event** — something undeniable and visible. This triggers 25th Amendment discussions for real.
- **Criminal conviction in NY or GA** — already pending cases. A conviction doesn't remove him but creates the "convicted president" framing.

Without a smoking gun, Republican senators have no *permission* to break. Even if they want to (and Jeff Flake estimated 30-35 would vote to convict on a secret ballot), they need cover. The smoking gun provides the cover.

**CONDITION 4: Republican senators fear their voters more than they fear Trump (probability: depends on Conditions 1-3)**

This is the Nixon lesson. Goldwater didn't go to the White House because he had a moral awakening. He went because he could count votes — and the votes said conviction was coming. Republican senators will break when:

- Their OWN poll numbers tank (not just Trump's)
- Their donors call and say "enough"
- Fox News turns (and it hasn't — but Tucker is already cracking on the war)
- The midterm results prove that Trump is an electoral anchor, not an asset

The war powers vote in March 2026 showed **only 1 Republican senator (Rand Paul)** breaking on Iran. But — crucially — multiple senators expressed "hesitation about ground troops." Cassidy said "I don't think the American people want to see troops on the ground." That's not a break, but it's a crack. And cracks widen under pressure.

The CNN analysis noted: *"GOP opposition to the Iran war is basically where Iraq war opposition started in 2006. And it's quite possible support could fall, especially if the war drags on and the costs increase."*

---

### THE REALISTIC SCENARIOS (Post-Midterms, January 2027+)

**Scenario A: Impeachment Without Removal — 50% probability**

Democrats win the House, impeach Trump on multiple articles (war powers abuse, obstruction, corruption), Senate trial happens, 52-55 senators vote to convict (including 5-8 Republicans from blue/purple states), but falls short of 67. Trump is impeached for a historic third time but not removed. He calls it a "witch hunt" for a third time.

This is the most likely scenario. It constrains Trump through investigations (subpoena power, public hearings, testimony) but doesn't remove him. It's the 2019 playbook again — but with more ammunition and a weaker Trump.

**Scenario B: The Nixon Exit — 10-15% probability**

Something breaks. A smoking gun emerges from the Iran war (fabricated intelligence, Kent testifies under oath, a military catastrophe). The midterms are a bloodbath for Republicans (40+ House seats, 4+ Senate seats). Gas is at $6+. Approval is at 28%. Republican senators start doing the math: defending Trump in 2028 = career death.

A delegation — maybe Thune, maybe McConnell (retired but influential), maybe a group of 2028 Senate candidates — tells Trump privately: resign or face conviction. Trump, facing the prospect of being the first president actually removed, negotiates a deal: resign in exchange for Vance pardon. Vance becomes president.

This requires: a smoking gun + electoral bloodbath + economic crisis + military crisis all converging. It's not impossible — all four of those things are in motion right now. But it's a low-probability convergence.

**Scenario C: Constrained But Not Removed — 30% probability**

Democrats win the House but Republicans hold the Senate (51-49 or 50-50). Trump is impeached but not tried (or tried and acquitted quickly). However, the Democratic House uses subpoena power, controls the budget, blocks appointments, and effectively makes governing impossible. Trump becomes a lame duck two years early — raging, executive-ordering, but unable to pass legislation.

This is the "partial win" scenario. It doesn't oust Trump but it stops the bleeding. It's what 2018 actually did in Trump's first term.

**Scenario D: Nothing Changes — 5-10% probability**

Republicans hold the House (gerrymandering, voter suppression, rally-around-the-flag). Trump is fully unconstrained. No Kings movement collapses from exhaustion. The 2028 presidential election becomes the only remaining check.

Low probability based on current data, but not zero. The 2024 precedent (Dems overperformed specials but lost the presidential) is a caution against overconfidence.

---

### THE JEFF FLAKE QUESTION

Here's the most haunting data point in all of this:

Former Senator Jeff Flake estimated that **30-35 Republican senators would vote to convict Trump on a secret ballot.**

Thirty-five. That's more than enough. That's 47 Democrats + 35 Republicans = 82 votes. Removal by 15 votes.

**The problem is it's not a secret ballot.** And every Republican senator knows that voting to convict means a Trump-backed primary challenger, death threats, and the end of their career in the current GOP.

So the question isn't "do enough Republicans privately want him gone?" **They do.** The question is "what would make them willing to do it publicly?" And the answer is: they have to fear their *voters* more than they fear Trump. They have to believe that keeping Trump is a bigger career risk than crossing him.

That's what the midterms can do. If the 2026 results show that Trump is electoral poison — if Republicans lose 40+ House seats, lose the Senate, lose governor's races — then suddenly the math flips. Keeping Trump becomes the risky move. And those 30-35 secret-ballot votes might become real ones.

---

### BOTTOM LINE

**Can Trump be ousted after midterms?** Yes, constitutionally. The mechanism exists.

**Will he be?** Probably not through conviction (need 16+ GOP senators to break publicly). But the Nixon model — resign under pressure — is not zero probability, and every current trend is pushing in that direction.

**What has to happen:**
1. ✅ Democrats flip the House (trending strongly)
2. 🟡 Democrats gain Senate seats (possible but hard to get past 51-52)
3. ❓ A smoking gun emerges (unpredictable — but Iran war, Kent testimony, financial corruption all in play)
4. ❓ Republican senators decide Trump is a bigger threat to their careers than crossing him (requires #1 + #2 + #3)

**The thing to watch isn't No Kings turnout or approval polls. It's whether the Iran war produces an Iraq-2006 moment.** Iraq broke the Republican Party's grip on Congress. Iran could do the same — but faster, because the costs are higher (oil at $114 vs. $60 in 2006), the casualties could mount faster (ground invasion planning vs. years of slow bleed), and Trump's approval started lower (37% vs. Bush's 38% in Oct 2006).

If the Iran war goes badly — really badly, ground troops badly, $7 gas badly, allies-abandon-us badly — then the 30-35 senators who'd convict on a secret ballot might find the courage to do it on a public one.

That's the path. It's narrow. But it exists, and everything happening right now is making it wider.

[Sources: FiveThirtyEight — Nixon](https://fivethirtyeight.com/features/it-took-a-long-time-for-republicans-to-abandon-nixon/), [Washington Post — Nixon Republicans](https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/2020/02/12/romneys-not-really-alone-republican-senators-were-ready-oust-nixon-1974/), [CNN — War Powers vote](https://www.cnn.com/2026/03/04/politics/who-voted-war-powers-senator-iran-vis), [TIME — Senate rejects war powers](https://time.com/7382503/trump-iran-war-congress-vote/), [Common Dreams — GOP polling](https://www.commondreams.org/news/trump-iran-war-polling), [NBC — Senate races](https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2026-election/10-senate-races-will-decide-balance-power-2026-rcna248276), [Sabato's Crystal Ball](https://centerforpolitics.org/crystalball/our-initial-senate-ratings-republicans-start-as-strong-favorites-to-hold-majority/), [Washingtonian — impeachment loophole](https://washingtonian.com/2019/10/10/the-impeachment-loophole-no-ones-talking-about/)

---

## LAST 48 HOURS — March 23-25, 2026

### 🔴 IRAN WAR — Day 25

**The situation is schizophrenic.** Trump is simultaneously claiming peace talks are happening AND deploying the 82nd Airborne for a possible ground invasion.

**The "talks" (March 24):**
- Trump: "We're in negotiations right now" — says Vance, Rubio leading talks, claims "15 points of agreement," nuclear weapons is "No. 1, 2 and 3"
- Iran has reportedly **received** Trump's 15-point plan via Pakistani intermediaries (AP, citing sources in Islamabad)
- **Iran's response:** Foreign Ministry says talks are "fake news" to "manipulate financial and oil markets." Military spokesperson: Americans are "only negotiating with themselves."
- Iranian source told CNN there was "outreach" — softer than "no dialogue," but not confirmation of talks
- China's Wang Yi urged Iran to engage in talks "as soon as possible"
- **Pakistan** emerging as key go-between; in-person meeting "could be held in coming days"
- **Hegseth "quite disappointed"** by prospect of negotiations — Trump himself said the Defense Secretary and Joint Chiefs Chairman Gen. Dan Caine were "the only two people that were quite disappointed"

**The military escalation (simultaneous with "talks"):**
- **🚨 82nd Airborne ordered to deploy** — 2,000-3,000 paratroopers, including Maj. Gen. Brandon Tegtmeier and division HQ staff, ordered to Middle East
- Fort Bragg's 1st Brigade Combat Team (Immediate Response Force — can deploy anywhere in 24 hours) included
- Combined with two Marine Expeditionary Units already heading to Gulf: **6,000-8,000 US ground troops** now moving into position
- **Kharg Island** identified as likely target — 5-mile island handling 90% of Iran's oil exports, already bombed, packed with oil infrastructure AND civilians
- Stars and Stripes: "82nd Airborne considered for Iran deployment as Marines move into position"
- The Intercept: "Leaders of Elite Paratrooper Unit Ordered to Middle East as Trump Weighs Iran Ground War"

**The ongoing war:**
- CENTCOM: **9,000+ Iranian targets hit**, 140+ naval vessels destroyed, 9,000+ combat flights since Feb 28
- **Bushehr nuclear power plant struck AGAIN** (March 24) — second time. IAEA Director General Grossi warned the first strike (March 17) crossed the "reddest line" of nuclear safety. A hit on an operating reactor = radiological incident.
- Iran hitting back: missiles at Israel (one hit a Tel Aviv street), attacks on US bases in Kuwait, Jordan, Bahrain
- **Saudi Arabia** intercepted ~20 drones targeting Eastern Province oil facilities
- **Kuwait International Airport** hit by drone — fire at fuel tank
- Bahrain has intercepted 153 missiles and 301 drones since war began
- **82,000+ civilian structures damaged/destroyed in Iran** (Iranian Red Crescent)
- **17 Red Crescent bases struck, 94 ambulances hit**

**Casualties — Day 25:**
- Iran: **1,200+ killed** (Israeli/American strikes)
- Lebanon: **1,072+ killed**, 2,966 injured, **1.2 million displaced** (1 in 5 Lebanese)
- Israel: 17 killed
- US: **13 KIA, 290+ WIA** (wounded number jumped from ~200 last update)

**The contradiction:** Trump is deploying the 82nd Airborne (America's premier rapid-deployment ground force) while claiming negotiations are going well. These things don't happen at the same time unless you're either preparing for failure or using the deployment as leverage. Either way, 6,000-8,000 ground troops are now moving toward Iran.

[Sources: Al Jazeera Day 25](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/24/us-israel-war-on-iran-whats-happening-on-day-25-of-attacks), [CNN Day 25](https://www.cnn.com/world/live-news/iran-war-us-israel-trump-03-24-26), [NPR](https://www.npr.org/2026/03/25/nx-s1-5760675/iran-war-military-deployment), [CBS — 82nd Airborne](https://www.cbsnews.com/news/u-s-deploy-82nd-airborne-iran-middle-east/), [Stars and Stripes](https://www.stripes.com/branches/army/2026-03-24/karag-82nd-airborne-marines-iran-21167074.html), [The Intercept](https://theintercept.com/2026/03/24/82nd-airborne-leadership-ordered-to-middle-east-as-trump-iran-war/), [CNN — 82nd Airborne](https://www.cnn.com/2026/03/24/politics/us-army-sending-troops-middle-east-iran), [World Nuclear News — Bushehr](https://world-nuclear-news.org/articles/iran-tells-iaea-a-projectile-hit-bushehr-nuclear-plant-premises), [UPI — Bushehr second strike](https://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2026/03/24/iran-Bushehr-nuclear-lant/1241774408744/)

### 🔴 LEBANON — Ground Invasion Deepening

- Israel deployed a **second division** to southern Lebanon
- **All bridges over the Litani River destroyed** — Defense Minister Katz ordered it, cutting south from north
- Lebanon's President Aoun: bridge strikes are "a prelude to a ground invasion and an attempt to obstruct humanitarian aid"
- Katz: Israel "will control the security zone up to the Litani" — displaced residents **will not be permitted to return**
- **Smotrich called for ANNEXATION of southern Lebanon** — "a change of Israel's borders" is necessary
- Spain's PM Sanchez: Israel "seeks to inflict the same level of damage and destruction" on Lebanon as on Gaza
- **Canada told Israel** Lebanon's sovereignty "must not be violated"
- Hezbollah still fighting — launched 5 attacks on Israeli positions in single morning

**1,072 dead. 1.2 million displaced. Bridges destroyed. Annexation language. This is looking more like a permanent occupation than a security operation.**

[Sources: Al Jazeera — Canada/Lebanon](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/25/canada-tells-israel-that-lebanons-sovereignty-must-not-be-violated), [Al Jazeera — Smotrich annexation](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/23/smotrich-urges-israel-to-annex-southern-lebanon-as-assault-intensifies), [Al Jazeera — Beirut strikes](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/24/israel-kills-two-in-beirut-as-it-intensifies-attacks-across-lebanon)

### 🟢 MULLIN CONFIRMED AND SWORN IN — DHS Secretary #9

**This actually happened.** Markwayne Mullin confirmed 54-45, sworn in by Trump March 24.

- **Fetterman (D-PA) and Heinrich (D-NM) voted yes** — Fetterman's committee save was critical
- **Rand Paul was the only Republican no**
- Key policy: Agents **required to secure judicial warrants** to enter homes/businesses — a major change from Noem's DHS
- Said he'd like ICE to "become more a transport than on the front line"
- **Oklahoma seat filled temporarily** — Gov. Stitt appointed energy exec Alan Armstrong (must sign affidavit NOT to run for full term; special election in November 2026)

**What this means:** Mullin is a moderate shift from Noem. Judicial warrant requirement is a real policy change the protest movement helped force. But he's still Trump's guy, still enforcing the same immigration agenda, just with slightly more procedural guardrails.

[Sources: DHS](https://www.dhs.gov/news/2026/03/24/us-senate-confirms-markwayne-mullin-secretary-department-homeland-security), [CBS](https://www.cbsnews.com/news/markwayne-mullin-confirmed-dhs-secretary-senate/), [NPR](https://www.npr.org/2026/03/23/g-s1-114813/markwayne-mullin-confirmed-homeland-security), [Fox News](https://www.foxnews.com/politics/mullin-sworn-dhs-chief-after-gop-fracture-forced-dem-save-nomination)

### 🔴 DHS SHUTDOWN — Day 39. A Deal Takes Shape (Maybe).

**The framework:**
- Senate negotiators coalescing around a deal: fund **94% of DHS** while withholding **$5.5 billion** for ICE's Enforcement and Removal Operations
- Republicans would try to fund ICE separately through budget reconciliation — uncertain path requiring total GOP unity
- **Neither side is happy:** Democrats didn't get policy changes (no end to administrative warrants, masked agents). Republicans are splitting ICE funding out and hoping reconciliation works.

**Trump is blocking it.** Demanding Republicans link DHS funding to the SAVE Act (voter ID bill that doesn't have 60 votes and everyone knows it).

**The damage:**
- **450+ TSA officers have quit** since shutdown started
- 61,000 TSA employees working without pay
- ICE agents at airports **passing out water bottles** to travelers in 4-hour TSA lines (Houston Bush Intercontinental). TSA union: "an insult to the employees."
- **Delta suspended special services for members of Congress** due to shutdown
- Congress members losing their own flying perks — NPR: "Congress loses a flying perk as DHS shutdown continues"

**The irony:** ICE is funded (through One Big Beautiful Bill). TSA is not. So the enforcement arm Trump cares about keeps operating while the transportation security arm collapses. ICE agents are literally doing TSA's job now.

[Sources: MSNBC](https://www.ms.now/news/deal-to-end-dhs-shutdown-parties-uneasy), [CBS](https://www.cbsnews.com/news/dhs-shutdown-senate-deal/), [CNN](https://www.cnn.com/2026/03/23/politics/dhs-shutdown-tsa-republicans-proposal-democrats), [NPR — Congress perks](https://www.npr.org/2026/03/24/g-s1-114961/tsa-congress-dhs-shutdown), [PolitiFact](https://www.politifact.com/article/2026/mar/23/TSA-ICE-DHS-shutdown-funding-paid-Trump-airport/)

### 🟢🟢🟢 DEMOCRAT FLIPS TRUMP'S HOME DISTRICT — Mar-a-Lago Special Election

**This is the headline of the week for the midterms.**

**Emily Gregory (D) defeated Jon Maples (R) by 2.4 points** in Florida House District 87 — the district that includes Trump's Mar-a-Lago resort.

| Metric | 2024 | March 25, 2026 |
|--------|------|-----------------|
| District partisan lean | Trump +9, Caruso (R) won by +19 | **Gregory (D) won by +2.4** |
| Swing | — | **~21 points toward Democrats** |
| Trump endorsement | — | Maples had Trump's "Complete and Total Endorsement" — **lost anyway** |
| Key issue | — | Affordability — Dems' strongest message |

**The broader pattern:**
- **29 state legislative seats flipped** from R to D since Trump returned to White House (Jan 2025)
- Democrats overperforming Harris 2024 margins by **~11 points** across all 2026 special elections
- Previous flips include: Texas Senate (Trump+17 district, held by GOP 30 years), Louisiana (Trump+13), Arkansas, New Hampshire
- **Trump voted by mail** in this election — despite pushing Congress to curtail mail voting and calling it a source of fraud

**Why this matters:** This isn't just any district. This is *Trump's home district.* His neighbors voted against his endorsed candidate. If you can't hold Mar-a-Lago, what CAN you hold? The midterm implications are severe.

[Sources: CNBC](https://www.cnbc.com/2026/03/24/trump-emily-gregory-special-election-democrat-mar-a-lago.html), [Washington Post](https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/2026/03/24/emily-gregory-trump-district-win/), [CNN](https://www.cnn.com/2026/03/24/politics/florida-democrats-state-district-mar-a-lago-special-election), [Axios](https://www.axios.com/2026/03/25/democrats-flip-florida-seat-trump-mar-a-lago-emily-gregory), [Al Jazeera](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/25/democrat-captures-florida-house-seat-in-trumps-mar-a-lago-district)

Reuters/Ipsos poll (completed March 24):
- **36% approve** (down from 40% last week — 4-point drop in one week)
- **62% disapprove**
- **25% approve of cost-of-living handling** — lower than any Biden rating on the economy

- **61% disapprove of Iran strikes**
- **46%** say war will make US **less safe** (only 26% say safer)

**The 36% matters.** Nixon was at 27% when he resigned. Bush was at 38% in October 2006 when Democrats took both chambers. Trump is now closer to Nixon territory than Bush territory. And it's dropping 4 points per week.

### 🔴 ICE / ENFORCEMENT INCIDENTS — Updated Through March 25, 2026

**The running total is grim.**

| Metric | Number | Source |
|--------|--------|--------|
| **Shootings by immigration agents** since Jan 20, 2025 | **33+** | PBS, Wikipedia tracker |
| **Deaths from shootings** | **9** | Snopes (verified March 10) |
| **Deaths in ICE custody** (2025 + early 2026) | **43-45** | Organiser, Marshall Project |
| **Deaths in ICE custody** (January 2026 alone) | **6** | American Immigration Council |
| Instances of agents firing at/into vehicles | **13+** | Wall Street Journal |
| US citizens shot | **5+** | PBS |
| **Public disapproval of ICE** | **60%** | PBS/NPR/Marist |

**New incidents in the last 48 hours:**

**1. Minnesota sues DOJ + DHS over shooting evidence (March 24)**

AG Keith Ellison and Hennepin County Attorney Mary Moriarty filed a federal lawsuit to force the Trump administration to hand over evidence in the Good, Pretti, and Sosa-Celis shootings. This is a major escalation:

- State demands: the car Good was killed in (currently shrink-wrapped in a federal warehouse), names of agents who killed Pretti, the guns used in all three cases
- DOJ flew an attorney to Minnesota in February — told the state "we want YOUR evidence, but we won't share ours"
- Minnesota submitted formal Touhy demands in February. **DOJ never responded.** Not a denial. Nothing. Deadlines passed in silence.
- Ellison: "The feds' choice not to share evidence with us is arbitrary, capricious, and has no rational basis"
- Trump admin has argued Minnesota doesn't have jurisdiction — state argues 10th Amendment gives them the right to investigate crimes on their soil
- **The feds are literally hiding the evidence of their own agents killing US citizens on American soil**

[Sources: MPR News](https://www.mprnews.org/story/2026/03/24/minnesota-asks-court-to-force-feds-to-share-ice-shooting-evidence), [Washington Post](https://www.washingtonpost.com/nation/2026/03/24/minnesota-shootings-evidence-lawsuit-ice/), [PBS](https://www.pbs.org/newshour/nation/minnesota-sues-to-obtain-evidence-in-shootings-by-federal-officers-during-ice-surge), [Fox 9](https://www.fox9.com/news/minnesota-sues-doj-dhs-over-access-evidence-renee-good-alex-pretti-shootings), [Minnesota Reformer](https://minnesotareformer.com/2026/03/24/minnesota-sues-trump-administration-over-access-to-evidence-in-shootings-by-federal-agents/)

**2. ICE violently arrests mother and daughter at SFO (March 22, viral March 23-24)**

Viral video shows plainclothes ICE agents forcibly handcuffing a crying woman at San Francisco International Airport while her ~10-year-old daughter stands by screaming. Key details:

- **Angelina and Wendy Godinez-Lopez** — Sacramento mother and daughter, had "outstanding final order of removal since 2019" per DHS
- Agents were not in uniform, did not identify themselves when bystanders asked repeatedly
- DHS claimed she "attempted to flee and resisted" — video shows the crowd confused about who these men are
- **Both were deported to Guatemala within hours** — no court hearing, no lawyer
- Happened ONE DAY before Trump announced ICE deployment to airports (March 23)
- DHS insists it was "unrelated" to the airport deployment announcement
- **Potential violation of California sanctuary law** — Mission Local reports SFO is investigating
- Sen. Wiener: "ICE's tactics are violent and unacceptable, and they need to stay the hell away from San Francisco and SFO"
- Rep. Matsui demanding answers — said she was a "Sacramento mother"

[Sources: KTVU](https://www.ktvu.com/news/ice-agents-arrest-crying-woman-sfo), [ABC7](https://abc7news.com/post/lawmakers-respond-ice-agents-detain-woman-sfo/18756606/), [SF Standard](https://sfstandard.com/2026/03/23/ice-at-sfo-detain-woman-video/), [Democracy Now](https://www.democracynow.org/2026/3/24/headlines/videos_show_ice_agents_violently_arresting_mother_and_daughter_at_san_francisco_airport), [TMZ](https://www.tmz.com/2026/03/23/ice-officers-handcuff-woman-at-san-francisco-international-airport/), [Mission Local](https://missionlocal.org/2026/03/arrest-at-sfo-sparks-concerns-ice/)

**3. ISIS-inspired IED attack at Gracie Mansion protest (March 7 — context for current climate)**

Not new-new but important context for the protest environment heading into March 28:

- Two ISIS-inspired men (Emir Balat, 18, and Ibrahim Kayumi, 19, from Pennsylvania) threw TATP-based IEDs with shrapnel (nuts, bolts, screws) at a counter-protest outside NYC Mayor Mamdani's Gracie Mansion
- Balat told investigators he wanted an attack "bigger than the Boston Marathon bombing"
- Devices were capable of "serious injury or death" per NYPD
- Federal charges: material support for terrorism, weapon of mass destruction, transportation of explosives
- Both ISIS-inspired — Balat traveled to Istanbul May-Aug 2025
- **Most significant terrorism incident in NYC since 2017 Port Authority attack**
- This is the security environment No Kings III is happening in — 3 days from now

[Sources: CNN](https://www.cnn.com/2026/03/07/us/gracie-mansion-protests-ignited-device), [DOJ](https://www.justice.gov/opa/pr/two-isis-supporters-charged-attempting-detonate-explosive-devices-during-protests-outside), [CBS](https://www.cbsnews.com/news/fbi-investigation-terrorism-explosive-device-new-york-city-mayor-mamdani-gracie-mansion/)

**4. Ruben Ray Martinez video released (March 7 — resurfaced)**

New footage of the March 2025 ICE killing of 23-year-old US citizen Ruben Ray Martinez on South Padre Island. Video shows:
- His car was "barely moving" and "braking, not accelerating"
- He was "shot at point-blank range through his side window by an ICE agent who was in no danger"
- Contradicts DHS claim he tried to run over officers
- Grand jury ruled justifiable homicide anyway
- Same pattern as Good and Pretti — DHS lies, video contradicts, no accountability

[Sources: Washington Post](https://www.washingtonpost.com/immigration/2026/03/07/ruben-martinez-dhs-killing-texas-video/), [KSAT](https://www.ksat.com/news/ksat-investigates/2026/03/07/footage-new-records-show-what-led-to-ice-shooting-a-san-antonio-man-in-south-padre-island-last-year/), [Texas Tribune](https://www.texastribune.org/2026/02/20/texas-ice-fatal-shooting-south-padre-island/)

---

### THE PATTERN

Every single one of these follows the same script:

1. ICE/CBP agents kill or assault someone
2. DHS immediately claims self-defense / "they tried to run us over" / "domestic terrorism"
3. Video emerges contradicting DHS
4. Federal government refuses to share evidence with state investigators
5. No agent is charged
6. Nobody is fired
7. The next incident happens

33 shootings. 9 dead. 43-45 dead in custody. Zero agents criminally charged. Zero agents fired. The federal government is now being **sued** by a state just to get access to the evidence of its own agents killing American citizens.

This is the enforcement apparatus that Trump just called the "greatest enemy's" opposition. This is what's operating at airports as of March 23. This is what will be in the streets alongside the National Guard on March 28.

### 🔴 IRAN WAR — Day 27. The Schizophrenia Deepens.

Trump is simultaneously extending peace deadlines AND Israel is bombing nuclear reactors. Nothing about this is coherent.

**The "talks" (updated):**
- Trump extended his Hormuz power-plant-strike deadline by **10 more days — to April 6**. That's the second extension (original: March 24 → March 29 → now April 6). He's blinking.
- Claims "talks going very well" — Vance, Rubio, Witkoff, and **Jared Kushner** now all involved
- Iran's counter-proposal expected to arrive today (March 27) via Pakistani intermediaries
- **But:** Iran's military says Americans are "only negotiating with themselves." Foreign Ministry calls it "fake news."
- **China's Wang Yi** urged Iran to engage in talks "as soon as possible" — significant, China doesn't usually push Iran publicly

**The Vance-Netanyahu blow-up (March 25-26):**
- Vance held a **tense phone call** with Netanyahu — **chided him** for making "overly optimistic predictions" about the war
- Specifically challenged Netanyahu's pre-war claims that: the regime would fall quickly, a popular uprising would happen, the war would be easy
- **None of those things happened.** Day 27, regime intact, no uprising, Hormuz closed, 1,900+ Iranians dead
- Vance "highly skeptical" of Israel's rosy assessments, expects war to continue "another few weeks"
- **Then Israel retaliated:** A right-wing Israeli newspaper (owned by Miriam Adelson, GOP mega-donor) ran a story claiming Vance yelled at Netanyahu over settler violence in the West Bank — multiple sources say this story was **planted by the Israeli side**
- US official: **"It's an Israeli op against JD"** — accusing Israel of trying to sideline Vance from the peace negotiations
- **This is extraordinary.** The US VP is publicly feuding with the Israeli PM over a war the US started. Israel is allegedly running media ops against the American Vice President. The alliance is cracking.

[Sources: Axios — Vance/Netanyahu](https://www.axios.com/2026/03/27/vance-iran-peace-talks), [Times of Israel](https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog-march-27-2026/), [Raw Story — Israeli smear](https://www.rawstory.com/jd-vance-iran-israel/)

**Israel struck Arak nuclear reactor (March 27):**
- IDF bombed Iran's **Arak heavy water reactor** — a facility that can produce plutonium for nuclear weapons
- IDF said it targeted "the component intended for plutonium production, in order to prevent the reactor from being restored"
- IAEA: no radiological effects, no casualties (reactor still under construction, no nuclear material present)
- Also struck Khondab heavy water facility and Ardakan uranium processing facility
- This is the 3rd nuclear facility hit: Fordow/Natanz (Operation Midnight Hammer, June 2025), Bushehr (hit twice, March 17 + 24), now Arak
- Israel doing this while Trump is trying to negotiate = deliberate sabotage of the peace track

[Sources: Times of Israel](https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/idf-confirms-bombing-irans-heavy-water-reactor-key-nuclear-facility-in-arak/), [Al Jazeera](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/6/19/israel-attacks-irans-arak-nuclear-reactor-as-iran-strikes-israeli-hospital), [IAEA](https://www.timesofisrael.com/iaea-says-no-fear-of-radiological-effects-after-idf-hits-iran-heavy-water-reactor/)

**Iran's Hormuz "toll booth":**
- Iran is now **charging commercial ships $2 million per transit** through Hormuz
- Only ~16 ships crossed with AIS on in the week of March 15-22 (normally hundreds daily)
- Ships rerouted from normal lanes to an alternate path close to Iranian coastline — IRGC checks nationality, ownership, cargo, crew before granting permission
- Ships from "friendly" nations (China, Malaysia, India, Egypt, South Korea) allowed through
- Iranian lawmaker: "Collecting $2 million reflects Iran's strength"
- India objected, saying international law guarantees free navigation
- **This is de facto control of a global chokepoint.** Iran turned the Strait of Hormuz into a toll road.

[Sources: Al Jazeera](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/26/tehranstollbooth-how-iran-picks-who-to-let-through-strait-of-hormuz), [Bloomberg](https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2026-03-24/iran-charges-some-ships-hormuz-transit-fees-for-safe-passage), [Foreign Policy](https://foreignpolicy.com/2026/03/26/iran-strait-hormuz-war-tolls-shipping/), [Fox News](https://www.foxnews.com/world/iran-chokes-strait-hormuz-reported-2m-tanker-toll-regime-threatens-global-oil-supply)

**Pentagon considering 10,000 MORE troops:**
- WSJ reports Defense Department considering sending **10,000 additional troops** to Middle East
- This would be ON TOP of the 82nd Airborne (2,000-3,000) and two MEUs (9,000 Marines/sailors)
- Total potential ground force: **20,000+**
- Iranian parliament speaker warned US against putting troops on the ground
- White House says Trump "isn't planning" ground troops — while the Pentagon literally draws up scenarios for ground troops
- Ukraine's Zelenskyy: Ukrainian drone combat experts helping **five Middle East/Gulf countries** counter Iranian drone attacks

**Casualty update — Day 27:**

| Theater | Dead | Injured | Displaced |
|---------|------|---------|-----------|
| **Iran** | **1,900+** | **20,000+** | 180,000 (homes destroyed) |

[Sources: CNN Day 27](https://www.cnn.com/2026/03/27/world/live-news/iran-war-us-israel-trump), [Al Jazeera Day 27](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2026/3/27/iran-war-live-trump-delays-attacks-on-iranian-energy-sector-by-10-days), [NBC](https://www.nbcwashington.com/news/national-international/israel-iran-trump-war-march-27-2026-live-updates/4082263/), [NPR](https://www.npr.org/2026/03/26/nx-s1-5761882/iran-war-peace-conditions)

### 🟢 DHS SHUTDOWN — Day 41. SENATE PASSED A DEAL. House Blocking It.

**What happened overnight (March 26-27):**

The Senate voted **by unanimous consent after 2 AM** to fund most of DHS — everything EXCEPT ICE and Border Patrol.

| What's funded | What's NOT funded |
|---------------|-------------------|
| TSA (61,000 workers finally get paid) | ICE Enforcement & Removal ($5.5B) |
| Coast Guard | Customs & Border Protection |
| FEMA | — |
| Secret Service | — |
| Cybersecurity (CISA) | — |

**The trade:** Democrats gave up their policy demands (no end to administrative warrants, no body camera mandate, no masked agent ban). Republicans split ICE funding out to try through reconciliation. Nobody's happy.

**Trump tried to pay TSA himself.** Signed an executive order Thursday to "immediately" pay TSA officers using money from One Big Beautiful Bill. Legal experts: "very skeptical" he has authority to redirect appropriated funds. This is almost certainly unconstitutional — but TSA workers don't care about constitutional theory, they want paychecks.

**The House is killing it.**
- Conference Chair Lisa McClain (R-MI): called it **"garbage"**
- Speaker Johnson: "shameful" to break up DHS funding
- House Republicans will NOT vote on the Senate bill
- **So the shutdown continues** for TSA, Coast Guard, FEMA, Secret Service until the House acts

**TSA crisis — updated numbers:**
- **480+ officers have quit** (up from 450 two days ago)
- Absences **40%** at some airports
- 61,000 workers still unpaid after 41 days
- ICE agents at airports handing out water bottles to travelers in 4+ hour lines (the people shutting down the agency are consoling the people the shutdown is hurting)

**Schumer:** "This could have been done three weeks ago. This is exactly what we wanted."

[Sources: NPR](https://www.npr.org/2026/03/27/g-s1-115366/senate-dhs-tsa-deal), [CBS](https://www.cbsnews.com/live-updates/dhs-shutdown-2026-senate-funding-day-41/), [TIME](https://time.com/article/2026/03/27/senate-dhs-shutdown-deal-ice-tsa-funding-trump-republicans/), [CNBC](https://www.cnbc.com/2026/03/27/dhs-tsa-shutdown-congress.html), [Washington Post](https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/2026/03/26/trump-tsa-unilateral-payment/)

---

### ⚖️ MADURO COURT APPEARANCE — March 26

**Key outcomes:**
- Judge Hellerstein: **"I'm not going to dismiss the case."** Rejected defense motion to throw out drug trafficking charges.
- But he seemed **skeptical of prosecution's position** on legal fees — signaled that blocking Venezuela from paying Maduro's lawyers may violate his constitutional right to counsel
- Maduro appeared thinner, less defiant. Shackled at ankles. Said "good morning" in English. Joked with lawyers.
- **Trump wants MORE charges** — said at Cabinet meeting he's hopeful additional charges will be brought for facilitating drug/human trafficking into the US
- Defense: head-of-state immunity argument. Prosecution: you were captured, you're here, the indictment stands.
- Ruling on legal fees: TBD. Trial date: TBD. Next hearing: TBD.
- Noisy protests outside — both pro- and anti-Trump groups

**Charges (reminder):** Narco-terrorism conspiracy, cocaine importation conspiracy, machine gun possession, conspiracy to possess machine guns. **Life in prison if convicted.**

[Sources: CNN](https://www.cnn.com/2026/03/26/world/live-news/nicolas-maduro-new-york-court), [NBC](https://www.nbcnews.com/news/us-news/nicolas-maduro-wife-back-federal-court-first-time-arraignment-rcna265273), [NPR](https://www.npr.org/2026/03/27/nx-s1-5763491/judge-venezuela-maduro-legal-costs-us-drug-trafficking), [Al Jazeera](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/3/26/venezuelas-maduro-set-to-again-appear-in-us-court-how-strong-is-the-case)

- 3,100+ events in all 50 states
- Events on 6 continents

- A Democrat who just flipped Trump's home district by 21 points
- 43% public support vs. 30% MAGA
- 65%+ midterm enthusiasm at 9-10/10

This is the collision. Tomorrow we find out what happens.
